$ ./sync-git-auto.sh sync "Your commit message"
ln: failed to create symbolic link '/c/Users/rehan/OneDrive/Desktop/github_repos/logs/sync-git-auto-latest.log': No such file or directory
[2025-06-19 06:09:44] Script exited with code 1

rehan@LAPTOP-KTJEL1I2 MINGW64 ~/OneDrive/Desktop/github_repos/Quran-recitation-mvp/mvp (main|REBASE 2/50)
$  help me make this script run #!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail
IFS=$'\n\t'

# === Configuration ===
# Base directory containing multiple git repos
BASE_DIR="${BASE_DIR:-/c/Users/rehan/OneDrive/Desktop/github_repos}"
# Directory to store logs
LOG_DIR="$BASE_DIR/logs"
# Lockfile to prevent concurrent runs
LOCKFILE="$BASE_DIR/sync-git-auto.lock"
# Number of retries for transient commands
MAX_RETRIES=5
# Base wait (seconds) for retry backoff
RETRY_WAIT_BASE=5
# Git remote and branch
GITHUB_REMOTE="${GITHUB_REMOTE:-origin}"
MAIN_BRANCH="${MAIN_BRANCH:-main}"

# Timestamp for this run
RUN_TS="$(date +'%Y%m%d-%H%M%S')"
RUN_LOG="$LOG_DIR/sync-git-auto-$RUN_TS.log"
# Symlink to latest
LATEST_LOG="$LOG_DIR/sync-git-auto-latest.log"

# Arrays to collect summary
declare -a SUMMARY_OK
declare -a SUMMARY_FAIL

# === Utility functions ===

timestamp() {
  date "+%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S"
}

log() {
  local msg="$*"
  echo "[$(timestamp)] $msg" | tee -a "$RUN_LOG"
}

# Abort script on unexpected exit, removing lockfile
cleanup() {
  local code=$?
  if [[ -f "$LOCKFILE" ]]; then
    rm -f "$LOCKFILE"
  fi
  if (( code != 0 )); then
    log "Script exited with code $code"
  else
    log "Script completed successfully"
  fi
}
trap cleanup EXIT

# Acquire lock: fail if already running
acquire_lock() {
  if [[ -f "$LOCKFILE" ]]; then
    local pid
    pid=$(<"$LOCKFILE")
    if kill -0 "$pid" &>/dev/null; then
      echo "Another instance (PID $pid) is running. Exiting." >&2
      exit 1
    else
      log "Stale lockfile detected (PID $pid not running). Overwriting."
    fi
  fi
  echo $$ > "$LOCKFILE"
}

# Retry a command with exponential backoff
retry_cmd() {
  local retries=0
  local wait_sec=$RETRY_WAIT_BASE
  local cmd=( "$@" )
  until "${cmd[@]}"; do
    ((retries++))
    if (( retries >= MAX_RETRIES )); then
      log "ERROR: Command failed after $retries attempts: ${cmd[*]}"
      return 1
    fi
    log "WARN: Command failed, retry $retries/$MAX_RETRIES: ${cmd[*]}"
    log "Retrying in $wait_sec seconds..."
    sleep "$wait_sec"
    wait_sec=$(( wait_sec * 2 ))
  done
}

# Check connectivity to Git remote for this repo
check_connectivity() {
  # quick ls-remote to test credentials/network
  if ! git ls-remote "$GITHUB_REMOTE" &>/dev/null; then
    log "ERROR: Cannot reach remote '$GITHUB_REMOTE' for $(pwd)."
    return 1
  fi
  return 0
}

# Detect and abort any in-progress rebase/merge safely
abort_rebase_merge_if_any() {
  # Called from inside repo dir
  if [[ -d ".git/rebase-apply" || -d ".git/rebase-merge" ]]; then
    log "Detected in-progress rebase in $(pwd). Attempting to abort..."
    if git rebase --abort &>/dev/null; then
      log "Rebase aborted."
    else
      log "Warning: Failed to abort rebase cleanly."
    fi
  fi
  if [[ -f ".git/MERGE_HEAD" ]]; then
    log "Detected in-progress merge in $(pwd). Attempting to abort..."
    if git merge --abort &>/dev/null; then
      log "Merge aborted."
    else
      log "Warning: Failed to abort merge cleanly."
    fi
  fi
}

# Stash uncommitted changes (including untracked), returns 0 if stashed (STASHED=1), else STASHED=0
stash_uncommitted() {
  STASHED=0
  # check if working tree is dirty
  if ! git diff --quiet || ! git diff --cached --quiet || [[ -n "$(git ls-files --others --exclude-standard)" ]]; then
    if git stash push --include-untracked -m "sync-git-auto stash before pull" &>/dev/null; then
      log "Stashed local changes."
      STASHED=1
    else
      log "Warning: Failed to stash local changes."
    fi
  fi
}

# Pop stash if previously stashed
pop_stash_if_any() {
  if [[ "${STASHED:-0}" -eq 1 ]]; then
    if git stash list | grep -q "sync-git-auto stash before pull"; then
      if git stash pop &>/dev/null; then
        log "Re-applied stashed changes."
      else
        log "Warning: Failed to re-apply stashed changes; please reapply manually."
      fi
    fi
  fi
}

clean_empty_dirs() {
  log "Cleaning empty directories..."
  find . -type d -empty -not -path "./.git*" -exec rm -rf {} + 2>/dev/null || true
}

get_all_repos() {
  find "$BASE_DIR" -mindepth 1 -maxdepth 1 -type d -exec test -d "{}/.git" \; -print || true
}

# Validate that remote exists and is reachable
validate_remote() {
  local repo="$1"
  cd "$repo"
  if ! git remote get-url "$GITHUB_REMOTE" &>/dev/null; then
    log "ERROR: Remote '$GITHUB_REMOTE' not set in $repo"
    cd - >/dev/null
    return 1
  fi
  if ! check_connectivity; then
    log "ERROR: Cannot reach remote in $repo"
    cd - >/dev/null
    return 1
  fi
  cd - >/dev/null
  return 0
}

# Checkout main, pull latest with rebase, handling stashes
checkout_and_pull_main() {
  abort_rebase_merge_if_any
  if ! retry_cmd git checkout "$MAIN_BRANCH"; then return 1; fi

  stash_uncommitted
  if ! retry_cmd git pull --rebase "$GITHUB_REMOTE" "$MAIN_BRANCH"; then
    log "ERROR: git pull --rebase failed on $(pwd)"
    abort_rebase_merge_if_any
    pop_stash_if_any
    return 1
  fi
  pop_stash_if_any
  return 0
}

sync_repo() {
  local repo="$1"; shift
  local commit_msg="$1"
  log "=== Sync start: $repo ==="
  cd "$repo"

  if ! validate_remote "$repo"; then
    SUMMARY_FAIL+=("$repo (remote issue)"); cd - >/dev/null; return 1
  fi

  if ! checkout_and_pull_main; then
    log "ERROR: Could not update main in $repo"
    SUMMARY_FAIL+=("$repo (pull failed)"); cd - >/dev/null; return 1
  fi

  # Stage changes except sensitive
  git add --all -- ":(exclude)config/" ":(exclude).env"
  if ! git diff --cached --quiet; then
    if ! git commit -m "$commit_msg"; then
      log "WARN: Commit failed in $repo"
    else
      log "Committed local changes in $repo"
    fi
  else
    log "No local changes to commit in $repo"
  fi

  clean_empty_dirs

  # Pull again in case remote updated after commit
  if ! checkout_and_pull_main; then
    log "ERROR: Pull after commit failed in $repo"
    SUMMARY_FAIL+=("$repo (pull after commit failed)"); cd - >/dev/null; return 1
  fi

  # Push
  if ! retry_cmd git push "$GITHUB_REMOTE" "$MAIN_BRANCH"; then
    log "ERROR: Push failed in $repo"
    SUMMARY_FAIL+=("$repo (push failed)"); cd - >/dev/null; return 1
  fi

  log "Sync succeeded for $repo"
  SUMMARY_OK+=("$repo")
  cd - >/dev/null
  return 0
}

merge_branches() {
  local repo="$1"; shift
  local auto_resolve="$1"; shift
  local branches=( "$@" )
  log "=== Merge start: $repo branches: ${branches[*]} ==="
  cd "$repo"

  if ! validate_remote "$repo"; then
    SUMMARY_FAIL+=("$repo (remote issue)"); cd - >/dev/null; return 1
  fi

  if ! checkout_and_pull_main; then
    log "ERROR: Could not update main before merge in $repo"
    SUMMARY_FAIL+=("$repo (pre-merge pull failed)"); cd - >/dev/null; return 1
  fi

  for br in "${branches[@]}"; do
    log "Merging $br into main in $repo"
    if ! retry_cmd git fetch "$GITHUB_REMOTE" "$br:$br"; then
      log "WARN: Failed to fetch $br in $repo"
      SUMMARY_FAIL+=("$repo (fetch $br failed)")
      continue
    fi

    if git merge --no-ff "$br" -m "Merged $br into $MAIN_BRANCH"; then
      log "Merged $br cleanly in $repo"
    else
      log "Conflict merging $br in $repo"
      if [[ "$auto_resolve" == "true" ]]; then
        log "Auto-resolving by accepting theirs for $br in $repo"
        git checkout --theirs . || log "Warn: checkout --theirs failed"
        git add . || log "Warn: git add after theirs failed"
        git commit -m "Auto-resolved conflict: accepted theirs from $br" || log "Warn: commit auto-resolve failed"
      else
        log "ERROR: Conflict in $repo on branch $br; manual resolution required"
        SUMMARY_FAIL+=("$repo (conflict on $br)")
        abort_rebase_merge_if_any
        cd - >/dev/null
        return 1
      fi
    fi
  done

  clean_empty_dirs

  if ! retry_cmd git push "$GITHUB_REMOTE" "$MAIN_BRANCH"; then
    log "ERROR: Push after merge failed in $repo"
    SUMMARY_FAIL+=("$repo (push after merge failed)"); cd - >/dev/null; return 1
  fi

  log "Merge succeeded for $repo"
  SUMMARY_OK+=("$repo")
  cd - >/dev/null
  return 0
}

clean_repo() {
  local repo="$1"
  log "=== Clean start: $repo ==="
  cd "$repo"
  if git filter-repo --force --invert-paths \
       --path config/firebase-credentials.json \
       --path config/google-credentials.json \
       --path .env; then
    log "Filter-repo succeeded in $repo"
    if git remote | grep -q "^$GITHUB_REMOTE\$"; then
      if retry_cmd git push --force "$GITHUB_REMOTE" "$MAIN_BRANCH"; then
        log "Force-pushed cleaned history in $repo"
      else
        log "ERROR: Force-push after clean failed in $repo"
        SUMMARY_FAIL+=("$repo (clean push failed)")
      fi
    else
      log "No '$GITHUB_REMOTE' remote in $repo; skipping push"
      SUMMARY_FAIL+=("$repo (no origin for clean)")
    fi
  else
    log "ERROR: git filter-repo failed in $repo"
    SUMMARY_FAIL+=("$repo (filter-repo failed)")
  fi
  cd - >/dev/null
}

send_alert() {
  # Placeholder for alerting on failures, e.g. email or Slack
  # e.g.: echo "Sync failures on $(hostname) at $(timestamp)" | mail -s "Sync Script Alert" your-email@example.com
  :
}

usage() {
  cat <<EOF
Usage:
  $0 sync [commit message]                  # Commit & push local changes, pull upstream
  $0 merge [--auto-resolve] <branches...>   # Merge given branches into main
  $0 clean                                  # Clean sensitive files from history via git filter-repo

Examples:
  ./sync-git-auto.sh sync "My changes"
  ./sync-git-auto.sh merge --auto-resolve feature1 feature2
  ./sync-git-auto.sh clean
EOF
  exit 1
}

main() {
  # Prepare log directory
  mkdir -p "$LOG_DIR"
  # Symlink latest log
  ln -sf "$RUN_LOG" "$LATEST_LOG"

  acquire_lock

  if (( $# < 1 )); then
    usage
  fi

  local cmd="$1"; shift

  mapfile -t repos < <(get_all_repos)
  if (( ${#repos[@]} == 0 )); then
    log "No git repos found under $BASE_DIR"
    exit 1
  fi

  case "$cmd" in
    sync)
      local commit_msg="${1:-Auto commit}"
      log "=== RUN sync; commit message: '$commit_msg' ==="
      for repo in "${repos[@]}"; do
        if ! sync_repo "$repo" "$commit_msg"; then
          log "Sync encountered issues in $repo"
        fi
      done
      ;;
    merge)
      local auto_resolve="false"
      if [[ "${1:-}" == "--auto-resolve" ]]; then
        auto_resolve="true"; shift
      fi
      if (( $# < 1 )); then
        log "ERROR: No branches specified for merge"
        usage
      fi
      local branches=( "$@" )
      log "=== RUN merge; auto_resolve=$auto_resolve; branches=${branches[*]} ==="
      for repo in "${repos[@]}"; do
        if ! merge_branches "$repo" "$auto_resolve" "${branches[@]}"; then
          log "Merge encountered issues in $repo"
        fi
      done
      ;;
    clean)
      log "=== RUN clean ==="
      for repo in "${repos[@]}"; do
        clean_repo "$repo"
      done
      ;;
    *)
      usage
      ;;
  esac

  # Summary
  log "=== Summary ==="
  log "Succeeded in:"
  for r in "${SUMMARY_OK[@]}"; do
    log "  - $r"
  done
  if (( ${#SUMMARY_FAIL[@]} > 0 )); then
    log "Failed or requires manual attention in:"
    for r in "${SUMMARY_FAIL[@]}"; do
      log "  - $r"
    done
    send_alert "sync-git-auto: Some repos failed or need manual resolution. Check log: $RUN_LOG"
  else
    log "All repos processed successfully."
  fi
}

main "$@"

Catching failures of ln -sf and falling back to copying the log file if symlinks aren’t supported.

main() {
  # Prepare log directory
  if ! mkdir -p "$LOG_DIR"; then
    echo "ERROR: Could not create log directory: $LOG_DIR" >&2
    exit 1
  fi

  # Ensure RUN_LOG file exists so tee in log() can append
  touch "$RUN_LOG"

  # Symlink latest log; if fails, fall back to copying and log a warning
  if ln -sf "$RUN_LOG" "$LATEST_LOG" 2>/dev/null; then
    :
  else
    log "WARN: Could not create symlink $LATEST_LOG; falling back to copying"
    if ! cp -f "$RUN_LOG" "$LATEST_LOG"; then
      log "ERROR: Failed to copy log to $LATEST_LOG"
    else
      log "Copied log to $LATEST_LOG"
    fi
  fi

  acquire_lock

  if (( $# < 1 )); then
    usage
  fi

  local cmd="$1"; shift

  mapfile -t repos < <(get_all_repos)
  if (( ${#repos[@]} == 0 )); then
    log "No git repos found under $BASE_DIR"
    exit 1
  fi

  case "$cmd" in
    sync)
      local commit_msg="${1:-Auto commit}"
      log "=== RUN sync; commit message: '$commit_msg' ==="
      for repo in "${repos[@]}"; do
        if ! sync_repo "$repo" "$commit_msg"; then

          log "Merge encountered issues in $repo"
        fi
      done
      ;;
    clean)
      log "=== RUN clean ==="
      for repo in "${repos[@]}"; do
        clean_repo "$repo"
      done
      ;;
    *)
      usage
      ;;
  esac

  # Summary
  log "=== Summary ==="

  for r in "${SUMMARY_OK[@]}"; do
    log "  - $r"
  done

    for r in "${SUMMARY_FAIL[@]}"; do
      log "  - $r"
    done
    send_alert "sync-git-auto: Some repos failed or need manual resolution. Check log: $RUN_LOG"
  else
    log "All repos processed successfully."
  fi
}

Key changes explained:

After mkdir -p "$LOG_DIR", we touch "$RUN_LOG" so that the file exists before any log calls.

We wrap ln -sf "$RUN_LOG" "$LATEST_LOG" in an if; on failure, we log a warning and cp -f the log instead. This covers filesystems or permission contexts (e.g. OneDrive, Windows) where symlinks aren’t allowed.

The rest of the script (locking, sync/merge logic) remains unchanged.

With this, rerun ./sync-git-auto.sh sync "Your commit message" and you should no longer see the “ln: failed to create symbolic link” error; instead you’ll get a warning logged and a copy of the log as sync-git-auto-latest.log.

  until "${cmd[@]}"; do
    ((retries++))
    if (( retries >= MAX_RETRIES )); then
      log "ERROR: Command failed after $retries attempts: ${cmd[*]}"
      return 1
    fi
    log "WARN: Command failed, retry $retries/$MAX_RETRIES: ${cmd[*]}"
    log "Retrying in $wait_sec seconds..."
    sleep "$wait_sec"
    wait_sec=$(( wait_sec * 2 ))
  done
}

# Check connectivity to Git remote for this repo
check_connectivity() {
  if ! git ls-remote "$GITHUB_REMOTE" &>/dev/null; then
    log "ERROR: Cannot reach remote '$GITHUB_REMOTE' for $(pwd)."
    return 1
  fi
  return 0
}

# Detect and abort any in-progress rebase/merge safely
abort_rebase_merge_if_any() {
  if [[ -d ".git/rebase-apply" || -d ".git/rebase-merge" ]]; then
    log "Detected in-progress rebase in $(pwd). Attempting to abort..."
    if git rebase --abort &>/dev/null; then
      log "Rebase aborted."
    else
      log "Warning: Failed to abort rebase cleanly."
    fi
  fi
  if [[ -f ".git/MERGE_HEAD" ]]; then
    log "Detected in-progress merge in $(pwd). Attempting to abort..."
    if git merge --abort &>/dev/null; then
      log "Merge aborted."
    else
      log "Warning: Failed to abort merge cleanly."
    fi
  fi
}

# Stash uncommitted changes (including untracked), returns 0 if stashed (STASHED=1), else STASHED=0
stash_uncommitted() {
  STASHED=0
  if ! git diff --quiet || ! git diff --cached --quiet || [[ -n "$(git ls-files --others --exclude-standard)" ]]; then
    if git stash push --include-untracked -m "sync-git-auto stash before pull" &>/dev/null; then
      log "Stashed local changes."
      STASHED=1
    else
      log "Warning: Failed to stash local changes."
    fi
  fi
}

# Pop stash if previously stashed
pop_stash_if_any() {
  if [[ "${STASHED:-0}" -eq 1 ]]; then
    if git stash list | grep -q "sync-git-auto stash before pull"; then
      if git stash pop &>/dev/null; then
        log "Re-applied stashed changes."
      else
        log "Warning: Failed to re-apply stashed changes; please reapply manually."
      fi
    fi
  fi
}

# Clean empty directories (excluding .git)
clean_empty_dirs() {
  log "Cleaning empty directories..."
  find . -type d -empty -not -path "./.git*" -exec rm -rf {} + 2>/dev/null || true
}

# Find all immediate subdirectories under BASE_DIR that are git repos
get_all_repos() {
  find "$BASE_DIR" -mindepth 1 -maxdepth 1 -type d -exec test -d "{}/.git" \; -print || true
}

# Validate that remote exists and is reachable
validate_remote() {
  local repo="$1"
  cd "$repo"
  if ! git remote get-url "$GITHUB_REMOTE" &>/dev/null; then
    log "ERROR: Remote '$GITHUB_REMOTE' not set in $repo"
    cd - >/dev/null
    return 1
  fi
  if ! check_connectivity; then
    log "ERROR: Cannot reach remote in $repo"
    cd - >/dev/null
    return 1
  fi
  cd - >/dev/null
  return 0
}

# Checkout main, pull latest with rebase, handling stashes
checkout_and_pull_main() {
  abort_rebase_merge_if_any
  if ! retry_cmd git checkout "$MAIN_BRANCH"; then return 1; fi

  stash_uncommitted
  if ! retry_cmd git pull --rebase "$GITHUB_REMOTE" "$MAIN_BRANCH"; then
    log "ERROR: git pull --rebase failed on $(pwd)"
    abort_rebase_merge_if_any
    pop_stash_if_any
    return 1
  fi
  pop_stash_if_any
  return 0
}

sync_repo() {
  local repo="$1"; shift
  local commit_msg="$1"
  log "=== Sync start: $repo ==="
  cd "$repo"

  if ! validate_remote "$repo"; then
    SUMMARY_FAIL+=("$repo (remote issue)"); cd - >/dev/null; return 1
  fi

  if ! checkout_and_pull_main; then
    log "ERROR: Could not update main in $repo"
    SUMMARY_FAIL+=("$repo (pull failed)"); cd - >/dev/null; return 1
  fi

  # Stage changes except sensitive
  git add --all -- ":(exclude)config/" ":(exclude).env"
  if ! git diff --cached --quiet; then
    if ! git commit -m "$commit_msg"; then
      log "WARN: Commit failed in $repo"
    else
      log "Committed local changes in $repo"
    fi
  else
    log "No local changes to commit in $repo"
  fi

  clean_empty_dirs

  # Pull again in case remote updated after commit
  if ! checkout_and_pull_main; then
    log "ERROR: Pull after commit failed in $repo"
    SUMMARY_FAIL+=("$repo (pull after commit failed)"); cd - >/dev/null; return 1
  fi

  # Push
  if ! retry_cmd git push "$GITHUB_REMOTE" "$MAIN_BRANCH"; then
    log "ERROR: Push failed in $repo"
    SUMMARY_FAIL+=("$repo (push failed)"); cd - >/dev/null; return 1
  fi

  log "Sync succeeded for $repo"
  SUMMARY_OK+=("$repo")
  cd - >/dev/null
  return 0
}

merge_branches() {
  local repo="$1"; shift
  local auto_resolve="$1"; shift
  local branches=( "$@" )
  log "=== Merge start: $repo branches: ${branches[*]} ==="
  cd "$repo"

  if ! validate_remote "$repo"; then
    SUMMARY_FAIL+=("$repo (remote issue)"); cd - >/dev/null; return 1
  fi

  if ! checkout_and_pull_main; then
    log "ERROR: Could not update main before merge in $repo"
    SUMMARY_FAIL+=("$repo (pre-merge pull failed)"); cd - >/dev/null; return 1
  fi

  for br in "${branches[@]}"; do
    log "Merging $br into main in $repo"
    if ! retry_cmd git fetch "$GITHUB_REMOTE" "$br:$br"; then
      log "WARN: Failed to fetch $br in $repo"
      SUMMARY_FAIL+=("$repo (fetch $br failed)")
      continue
    fi

    if git merge --no-ff "$br" -m "Merged $br into $MAIN_BRANCH"; then
      log "Merged $br cleanly in $repo"
    else
      log "Conflict merging $br in $repo"
      if [[ "$auto_resolve" == "true" ]]; then
        log "Auto-resolving by accepting theirs for $br in $repo"
        git checkout --theirs . || log "Warn: checkout --theirs failed"
        git add . || log "Warn: git add after theirs failed"
        git commit -m "Auto-resolved conflict: accepted theirs from $br" || log "Warn: commit auto-resolve failed"
      else
        log "ERROR: Conflict in $repo on branch $br; manual resolution required"
        SUMMARY_FAIL+=("$repo (conflict on $br)")
        abort_rebase_merge_if_any
        cd - >/dev/null
        return 1
      fi
    fi
  done

  clean_empty_dirs

  if ! retry_cmd git push "$GITHUB_REMOTE" "$MAIN_BRANCH"; then
    log "ERROR: Push after merge failed in $repo"
    SUMMARY_FAIL+=("$repo (push after merge failed)"); cd - >/dev/null; return 1
  fi

  log "Merge succeeded for $repo"
  SUMMARY_OK+=("$repo")
  cd - >/dev/null
  return 0
}

clean_repo() {
  local repo="$1"
  log "=== Clean start: $repo ==="
  cd "$repo"
  if git filter-repo --force --invert-paths \
       --path config/firebase-credentials.json \
       --path config/google-credentials.json \
       --path .env; then
    log "Filter-repo succeeded in $repo"
    if git remote | grep -q "^$GITHUB_REMOTE\$"; then
      if retry_cmd git push --force "$GITHUB_REMOTE" "$MAIN_BRANCH"; then
        log "Force-pushed cleaned history in $repo"
      else
        log "ERROR: Force-push after clean failed in $repo"
        SUMMARY_FAIL+=("$repo (clean push failed)")
      fi
    else
      log "No '$GITHUB_REMOTE' remote in $repo; skipping push"
      SUMMARY_FAIL+=("$repo (no origin for clean)")
    fi
  else
    log "ERROR: git filter-repo failed in $repo"
    SUMMARY_FAIL+=("$repo (filter-repo failed)")
  fi
  cd - >/dev/null
}

send_alert() {
  # Placeholder for alerting on failures, e.g. email or Slack
  :
}

usage() {
  cat <<EOF
Usage:
  $0 sync [commit message]                  # Commit & push local changes, pull upstream
  $0 merge [--auto-resolve] <branches...>   # Merge given branches into main
  $0 clean                                  # Clean sensitive files from history via git filter-repo

Examples:
  ./sync-git-auto.sh sync "My changes"
  ./sync-git-auto.sh merge --auto-resolve feature1 feature2
  ./sync-git-auto.sh clean
EOF
  exit 1
}

main() {
  # Prepare log directory
  if ! mkdir -p "$LOG_DIR"; then
    echo "ERROR: Could not create log directory: $LOG_DIR" >&2
    exit 1
  fi

  # Timestamp for this run
  RUN_TS="$(date +'%Y%m%d-%H%M%S')"
  RUN_LOG="$LOG_DIR/sync-git-auto-$RUN_TS.log"
  LATEST_LOG="$LOG_DIR/sync-git-auto-latest.log"

  # Ensure RUN_LOG exists so log() can append
  touch "$RUN_LOG"

  # Symlink latest log; if fails, fall back to copying
  if ln -sf "$RUN_LOG" "$LATEST_LOG" 2>/dev/null; then
    :
  else
    log "WARN: Could not create symlink $LATEST_LOG; falling back to copying"
    if cp -f "$RUN_LOG" "$LATEST_LOG"; then
      log "Copied log to $LATEST_LOG"
    else
      log "ERROR: Failed to copy log to $LATEST_LOG"
    fi
  fi

  acquire_lock

  if (( $# < 1 )); then
    usage
  fi

  local cmd="$1"; shift

  # Gather repos
  mapfile -t repos < <(get_all_repos)
  if (( ${#repos[@]} == 0 )); then
    log "No git repos found under $BASE_DIR"
    exit 1
  fi

  case "$cmd" in
    sync)
      local commit_msg="${1:-Auto commit}"
      log "=== RUN sync; commit message: '$commit_msg' ==="
      for repo in "${repos[@]}"; do
        if ! sync_repo "$repo" "$commit_msg"; then
          log "Sync encountered issues in $repo"
        fi
      done
      ;;
    merge)
      local auto_resolve="false"
      if [[ "${1:-}" == "--auto-resolve" ]]; then
        auto_resolve="true"; shift
      fi
      if (( $# < 1 )); then
        log "ERROR: No branches specified for merge"
        usage
      fi
      local branches=( "$@" )
      log "=== RUN merge; auto_resolve=$auto_resolve; branches=${branches[*]} ==="
      for repo in "${repos[@]}"; do
        if ! merge_branches "$repo" "$auto_resolve" "${branches[@]}"; then
          log "Merge encountered issues in $repo"
        fi
      done
      ;;
    clean)
      log "=== RUN clean ==="
      for repo in "${repos[@]}"; do
        clean_repo "$repo"
      done
      ;;
    *)
      usage
      ;;
  esac

  # Summary
  log "=== Summary ==="
  log "Succeeded in:"
  for r in "${SUMMARY_OK[@]}"; do
    log "  - $r"
  done
  if (( ${#SUMMARY_FAIL[@]} > 0 )); then
    log "Failed or requires manual attention in:"
    for r in "${SUMMARY_FAIL[@]}"; do
      log "  - $r"
    done
    send_alert "sync-git-auto: Some repos failed or need manual resolution. Check log: $RUN_LOG"
  else
    log "All repos processed successfully."
  fi
}

main "$@"
Notes:

Ensure the file uses Unix line endings (LF). Run dos2unix sync-git-auto.sh if needed.

Invoke explicitly with Bash: bash -x ./sync-git-auto.sh sync "Your commit message" to trace execution.

The functions (e.g. get_all_repos) are defined before main, so calls won’t be “command not found.”

The log directory is created and the run-log file touched before any logging. The symlink to latest log falls back to copying if symlinks aren’t supported.

Adjust any paths or exclusions as needed.

Make the script executable (chmod +x sync-git-auto.sh) or run via bash ….

#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail
IFS=$'\n\t'

# === Configuration ===
# Base directory containing multiple git repos
BASE_DIR="${BASE_DIR:-/c/Users/rehan/OneDrive/Desktop/github_repos}"
# Directory to store logs
LOG_DIR="$BASE_DIR/logs"
# Lockfile to prevent concurrent runs
LOCKFILE="$BASE_DIR/sync-git-auto.lock"
# Number of retries for transient commands (used for network ops like push/fetch)
MAX_RETRIES=5
# Base wait (seconds) for retry backoff
RETRY_WAIT_BASE=5
# Git remote and branch
GITHUB_REMOTE="${GITHUB_REMOTE:-origin}"
MAIN_BRANCH="${MAIN_BRANCH:-main}"

# Arrays to collect summary
declare -a SUMMARY_OK
declare -a SUMMARY_FAIL

# === Utility functions ===

timestamp() {
  date "+%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S"
}

# Log a message, appending to RUN_LOG (which should exist/touch’ed beforehand)
log() {
  local msg="$*"
  echo "[$(timestamp)] $msg" | tee -a "$RUN_LOG"
}

# Abort script on unexpected exit, removing lockfile
cleanup() {
  local code=$?
  if [[ -f "$LOCKFILE" ]]; then
    rm -f "$LOCKFILE"
  fi
  if (( code != 0 )); then
    log "Script exited with code $code"
  else
    log "Script completed successfully"
  fi
}
trap cleanup EXIT

# Acquire lock: fail if already running
acquire_lock() {
  if [[ -f "$LOCKFILE" ]]; then
    local pid
    pid=$(<"$LOCKFILE")
    if kill -0 "$pid" &>/dev/null; then
      echo "Another instance (PID $pid) is running. Exiting." >&2
      exit 1
    else
      log "Stale lockfile detected (PID $pid not running). Overwriting."
    fi
  fi
  echo $$ > "$LOCKFILE"
}

# Retry a command (array form) with exponential backoff for transient failures
retry_cmd() {
  local retries=0
  local wait_sec=$RETRY_WAIT_BASE
  local cmd=( "$@" )
  until "${cmd[@]}"; do
    ((retries++))
    if (( retries >= MAX_RETRIES )); then
      log "ERROR: Command failed after $retries attempts: ${cmd[*]}"
      return 1
    fi
    log "WARN: Command failed, retry $retries/$MAX_RETRIES: ${cmd[*]}"
    log "Retrying in $wait_sec seconds..."
    sleep "$wait_sec"
    wait_sec=$(( wait_sec * 2 ))
  done
}

# Check connectivity to Git remote for this repo
check_connectivity() {
  if ! git ls-remote "$GITHUB_REMOTE" &>/dev/null; then
    log "ERROR: Cannot reach remote '$GITHUB_REMOTE' for $(pwd)."
    return 1
  fi
  return 0
}

# Detect and abort any in-progress rebase/merge safely
abort_rebase_merge_if_any() {
  if [[ -d ".git/rebase-apply" || -d ".git/rebase-merge" ]]; then
    log "Detected in-progress rebase in $(pwd). Attempting to abort..."
    if git rebase --abort &>/dev/null; then
      log "Rebase aborted."
    else
      log "Warning: Failed to abort rebase cleanly."
    fi
  fi
  if [[ -f ".git/MERGE_HEAD" ]]; then
    log "Detected in-progress merge in $(pwd). Attempting to abort..."
    if git merge --abort &>/dev/null; then
      log "Merge aborted."
    else
      log "Warning: Failed to abort merge cleanly."
    fi
  fi
}

# Stash uncommitted changes (including untracked), returns STASHED=1 if stashed, else 0
stash_uncommitted() {
  STASHED=0
  if ! git diff --quiet || ! git diff --cached --quiet || [[ -n "$(git ls-files --others --exclude-standard)" ]]; then
    if git stash push --include-untracked -m "sync-git-auto stash before pull" &>/dev/null; then
      log "Stashed local changes."
      STASHED=1
    else
      log "Warning: Failed to stash local changes."
    fi
  fi
}

# Pop stash if previously stashed
pop_stash_if_any() {
  if [[ "${STASHED:-0}" -eq 1 ]]; then
    if git stash list | grep -q "sync-git-auto stash before pull"; then
      if git stash pop &>/dev/null; then
        log "Re-applied stashed changes."
      else
        log "Warning: Failed to re-apply stashed changes; please reapply manually."
      fi
    fi
  fi
}

# Clean empty directories (excluding .git)
clean_empty_dirs() {
  log "Cleaning empty directories..."
  find . -type d -empty -not -path "./.git*" -exec rm -rf {} + 2>/dev/null || true
}

# Find all immediate subdirectories under BASE_DIR that are git repos
get_all_repos() {
  find "$BASE_DIR" -mindepth 1 -maxdepth 1 -type d -exec test -d "{}/.git" \; -print || true
}

# Validate that remote exists and is reachable
validate_remote() {
  local repo="$1"
  cd "$repo"
  if ! git remote get-url "$GITHUB_REMOTE" &>/dev/null; then
    log "ERROR: Remote '$GITHUB_REMOTE' not set in $repo"
    cd - >/dev/null
    return 1
  fi
  if ! check_connectivity; then
    log "ERROR: Cannot reach remote in $repo"
    cd - >/dev/null
    return 1
  fi
  cd - >/dev/null
  return 0
}

# Checkout main, pull latest with rebase, handling stashes and conflicts without retry loop
checkout_and_pull_main() {
  abort_rebase_merge_if_any
  # Ensure on main branch
  if ! git checkout "$MAIN_BRANCH"; then
    log "ERROR: Cannot checkout $MAIN_BRANCH in $(pwd)"
    return 1
  fi

  stash_uncommitted

  # Pull with rebase once; if conflicts arise, abort rebase and return failure
  if ! git pull --rebase "$GITHUB_REMOTE" "$MAIN_BRANCH"; then
    log "ERROR: git pull --rebase failed on $(pwd) (likely due to conflicts or network). Aborting rebase."
    abort_rebase_merge_if_any
    pop_stash_if_any
    return 1
  fi

  pop_stash_if_any
  return 0
}

sync_repo() {
  local repo="$1"; shift
  local commit_msg="$1"
  log "=== Sync start: $repo ==="
  cd "$repo"

  if ! validate_remote "$repo"; then
    SUMMARY_FAIL+=("$repo (remote issue)"); cd - >/dev/null; return 1
  fi

  if ! checkout_and_pull_main; then
    log "ERROR: Could not update main in $repo"
    SUMMARY_FAIL+=("$repo (pull failed)"); cd - >/dev/null; return 1
  fi

  # Stage changes except sensitive
  git add --all -- ":(exclude)config/" ":(exclude).env"
  if ! git diff --cached --quiet; then
    if git commit -m "$commit_msg"; then
      log "Committed local changes in $repo"
    else
      log "WARN: Commit failed in $repo"
    fi
  else
    log "No local changes to commit in $repo"
  fi

  clean_empty_dirs

  # Pull again once after commit; handle conflicts similarly
  if ! checkout_and_pull_main; then
    log "ERROR: Pull after commit failed in $repo"
    SUMMARY_FAIL+=("$repo (pull after commit failed)"); cd - >/dev/null; return 1
  fi

  # Push with retry
  if ! retry_cmd git push "$GITHUB_REMOTE" "$MAIN_BRANCH"; then
    log "ERROR: Push failed in $repo"
    SUMMARY_FAIL+=("$repo (push failed)"); cd - >/dev/null; return 1
  fi

  log "Sync succeeded for $repo"
  SUMMARY_OK+=("$repo")
  cd - >/dev/null
  return 0
}

merge_branches() {
  local repo="$1"; shift
  local auto_resolve="$1"; shift
  local branches=( "$@" )
  log "=== Merge start: $repo branches: ${branches[*]} ==="
  cd "$repo"

  if ! validate_remote "$repo"; then
    SUMMARY_FAIL+=("$repo (remote issue)"); cd - >/dev/null; return 1
  fi

  if ! checkout_and_pull_main; then
    log "ERROR: Could not update main before merge in $repo"
    SUMMARY_FAIL+=("$repo (pre-merge pull failed)"); cd - >/dev/null; return 1
  fi

  for br in "${branches[@]}"; do
    log "Merging $br into main in $repo"
    if ! retry_cmd git fetch "$GITHUB_REMOTE" "$br:$br"; then
      log "WARN: Failed to fetch $br in $repo"
      SUMMARY_FAIL+=("$repo (fetch $br failed)"
)
      continue
    fi

    if git merge --no-ff "$br" -m "Merged $br into $MAIN_BRANCH"; then
      log "Merged $br cleanly in $repo"
    else
      log "Conflict merging $br in $repo"
      if [[ "$auto_resolve" == "true" ]]; then
        log "Auto-resolving by accepting theirs for $br in $repo"
        git checkout --theirs . || log "Warn: checkout --theirs failed"
        git add . || log "Warn: git add after theirs failed"
        if git commit -m "Auto-resolved conflict: accepted theirs from $br"; then
          log "Auto-resolve commit succeeded"
        else
          log "Warn: commit auto-resolve failed"
        fi
      else
        log "ERROR: Conflict in $repo on branch $br; manual resolution required"
        SUMMARY_FAIL+=("$repo (conflict on $br)")
        abort_rebase_merge_if_any
        cd - >/dev/null
        return 1
      fi
    fi
  done

  clean_empty_dirs

  if ! retry_cmd git push "$GITHUB_REMOTE" "$MAIN_BRANCH"; then
    log "ERROR: Push after merge failed in $repo"
    SUMMARY_FAIL+=("$repo (push after merge failed)"); cd - >/dev/null; return 1
  fi

  log "Merge succeeded for $repo"
  SUMMARY_OK+=("$repo")
  cd - >/dev/null
  return 0
}

clean_repo() {
  local repo="$1"
  log "=== Clean start: $repo ==="
  cd "$repo"
  if git filter-repo --force --invert-paths \
       --path config/firebase-credentials.json \
       --path config/google-credentials.json \
       --path .env; then
    log "Filter-repo succeeded in $repo"
    if git remote | grep -q "^$GITHUB_REMOTE\$"; then
      if retry_cmd git push --force "$GITHUB_REMOTE" "$MAIN_BRANCH"; then
        log "Force-pushed cleaned history in $repo"
      else
        log "ERROR: Force-push after clean failed in $repo"
        SUMMARY_FAIL+=("$repo (clean push failed)")
      fi
    else
      log "No '$GITHUB_REMOTE' remote in $repo; skipping push"
      SUMMARY_FAIL+=("$repo (no origin for clean)")
    fi
  else
    log "ERROR: git filter-repo failed in $repo"
    SUMMARY_FAIL+=("$repo (filter-repo failed)")
  fi
  cd - >/dev/null
}

send_alert() {
  # Placeholder for alerting on failures, e.g. email or Slack
  :
}

usage() {
  cat <<EOF
Usage:
  $0 sync [commit message]                  # Commit & push local changes, pull upstream
  $0 merge [--auto-resolve] <branches...>   # Merge given branches into main
  $0 clean                                  # Clean sensitive files from history via git filter-repo

Examples:
  ./sync-git-auto.sh sync "My changes"
  ./sync-git-auto.sh merge --auto-resolve feature1 feature2
  ./sync-git-auto.sh clean
EOF
  exit 1
}

main() {
  # Prepare log directory
  if ! mkdir -p "$LOG_DIR"; then
    echo "ERROR: Could not create log directory: $LOG_DIR" >&2
    exit 1
  fi

  # Timestamp for this run
  RUN_TS="$(date +'%Y%m%d-%H%M%S')"
  RUN_LOG="$LOG_DIR/sync-git-auto-$RUN_TS.log"
  LATEST_LOG="$LOG_DIR/sync-git-auto-latest.log"

  # Ensure RUN_LOG exists so log() can append
  touch "$RUN_LOG"

  # Symlink latest log; if fails, fall back to copying
  if ln -sf "$RUN_LOG" "$LATEST_LOG" 2>/dev/null; then
    :
  else
    log "WARN: Could not create symlink $LATEST_LOG; falling back to copying"
    if cp -f "$RUN_LOG" "$LATEST_LOG"; then
      log "Copied log to $LATEST_LOG"
    else
      log "ERROR: Failed to copy log to $LATEST_LOG"
    fi
  fi

  acquire_lock

  if (( $# < 1 )); then
    usage
  fi

  local cmd="$1"; shift

  # Gather repos
  mapfile -t repos < <(get_all_repos)
  if (( ${#repos[@]} == 0 )); then
    log "No git repos found under $BASE_DIR"
    exit 1
  fi

  case "$cmd" in
    sync)
      local commit_msg="${1:-Auto commit}"
      log "=== RUN sync; commit message: '$commit_msg' ==="
      for repo in "${repos[@]}"; do
        if ! sync_repo "$repo" "$commit_msg"; then
          log "Sync encountered issues in $repo"
        fi
      done
      ;;
    merge)
      local auto_resolve="false"
      if [[ "${1:-}" == "--auto-resolve" ]]; then
        auto_resolve="true"; shift
      fi
      if (( $# < 1 )); then
        log "ERROR: No branches specified for merge"
        usage
      fi
      local branches=( "$@" )
      log "=== RUN merge; auto_resolve=$auto_resolve; branches=${branches[*]} ==="
      for repo in "${repos[@]}"; do
        if ! merge_branches "$repo" "$auto_resolve" "${branches[@]}"; then
          log "Merge encountered issues in $repo"
        fi
      done
      ;;
    clean)
      log "=== RUN clean ==="
      for repo in "${repos[@]}"; do
        clean_repo "$repo"
      done
      ;;
    *)
      usage
      ;;
  esac

  # Summary
  log "=== Summary ==="
  log "Succeeded in:"
  for r in "${SUMMARY_OK[@]}"; do
    log "  - $r"
  done
  if (( ${#SUMMARY_FAIL[@]} > 0 )); then
    log "Failed or requires manual attention in:"
    for r in "${SUMMARY_FAIL[@]}"; do
      log "  - $r"
    done
    send_alert "sync-git-auto: Some repos failed or need manual resolution. Check log: $RUN_LOG"
  else
    log "All repos processed successfully."
  fi
}

main "$@"
Key changes:

In checkout_and_pull_main, we removed wrapping git pull --rebase in retry_cmd. Instead, we run it once: if it fails (e.g. due to conflicts), we immediately abort the rebase, pop any stash, log an error, and return failure. This prevents endless retries when conflicts persist.

Similar logic for the second pull after committing changes.

Network operations like git push or git fetch still use retry_cmd, since those may transiently fail.

The rest of the flow remains: ensure functions are defined before use, Unix line endings, explicit bash -x ... testing, etc.

With this version, when a rebase conflict occurs, the script will log the conflict failure and move on (or stop for that repo), rather than retrying the pull multiple times. You can then manually inspect and resolve the conflicts in that repository.

Thought for a few seconds
Below is the full updated script. It adds, at the very end of main, a human-friendly summary printed to stdout, showing how many repos succeeded/failed and listing failures with reasons, plus where to find the detailed log. It also keeps the existing log-based summary. You can adjust the exact wording as you like.

Edit
#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail
IFS=$'\n\t'

# === Configuration ===
# Base directory containing multiple git repos
BASE_DIR="${BASE_DIR:-/c/Users/rehan/OneDrive/Desktop/github_repos}"
# Directory to store logs
LOG_DIR="$BASE_DIR/logs"
# Lockfile to prevent concurrent runs
LOCKFILE="$BASE_DIR/sync-git-auto.lock"
# Number of retries for transient commands (used for network ops like push/fetch)
MAX_RETRIES=5
# Base wait (seconds) for retry backoff
RETRY_WAIT_BASE=5
# Git remote and branch
GITHUB_REMOTE="${GITHUB_REMOTE:-origin}"
MAIN_BRANCH="${MAIN_BRANCH:-main}"

# Arrays to collect summary
declare -a SUMMARY_OK
declare -a SUMMARY_FAIL

# === Utility functions ===

timestamp() {
  date "+%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S"
}

# Log a message, appending to RUN_LOG (which should exist/touch’ed beforehand)
log() {
  local msg="$*"
  echo "[$(timestamp)] $msg" | tee -a "$RUN_LOG"
}

# Abort script on unexpected exit, removing lockfile
cleanup() {
  local code=$?
  if [[ -f "$LOCKFILE" ]]; then
    rm -f "$LOCKFILE"
  fi
  if (( code != 0 )); then
    log "Script exited with code $code"
  else
    log "Script completed successfully"
  fi
}
trap cleanup EXIT

# Acquire lock: fail if already running
acquire_lock() {
  if [[ -f "$LOCKFILE" ]]; then
    local pid
    pid=$(<"$LOCKFILE")
    if kill -0 "$pid" &>/dev/null; then
      echo "Another instance (PID $pid) is running. Exiting." >&2
      exit 1
    else
      log "Stale lockfile detected (PID $pid not running). Overwriting."
    fi
  fi
  echo $$ > "$LOCKFILE"
}

# Retry a command (array form) with exponential backoff for transient failures
retry_cmd() {
  local retries=0
  local wait_sec=$RETRY_WAIT_BASE
  local cmd=( "$@" )
  until "${cmd[@]}"; do
    ((retries++))
    if (( retries >= MAX_RETRIES )); then
      log "ERROR: Command failed after $retries attempts: ${cmd[*]}"
      return 1
    fi
    log "WARN: Command failed, retry $retries/$MAX_RETRIES: ${cmd[*]}"
    log "Retrying in $wait_sec seconds..."
    sleep "$wait_sec"
    wait_sec=$(( wait_sec * 2 ))
  done
}

# Check connectivity to Git remote for this repo
check_connectivity() {
  if ! git ls-remote "$GITHUB_REMOTE" &>/dev/null; then
    log "ERROR: Cannot reach remote '$GITHUB_REMOTE' for $(pwd)."
    return 1
  fi
  return 0
}

# Detect and abort any in-progress rebase/merge safely
abort_rebase_merge_if_any() {
  if [[ -d ".git/rebase-apply" || -d ".git/rebase-merge" ]]; then
    log "Detected in-progress rebase in $(pwd). Attempting to abort..."
    if git rebase --abort &>/dev/null; then
      log "Rebase aborted."
    else
      log "Warning: Failed to abort rebase cleanly."
    fi
  fi
  if [[ -f ".git/MERGE_HEAD" ]]; then
    log "Detected in-progress merge in $(pwd). Attempting to abort..."
    if git merge --abort &>/dev/null; then
      log "Merge aborted."
    else
      log "Warning: Failed to abort merge cleanly."
    fi
  fi
}

# Stash uncommitted changes (including untracked), returns STASHED=1 if stashed, else 0
stash_uncommitted() {
  STASHED=0
  if ! git diff --quiet || ! git diff --cached --quiet || [[ -n "$(git ls-files --others --exclude-standard)" ]]; then
    if git stash push --include-untracked -m "sync-git-auto stash before pull" &>/dev/null; then
      log "Stashed local changes."
      STASHED=1
    else
      log "Warning: Failed to stash local changes."
    fi
  fi
}

# Pop stash if previously stashed
pop_stash_if_any() {
  if [[ "${STASHED:-0}" -eq 1 ]]; then
    if git stash list | grep -q "sync-git-auto stash before pull"; then
      if git stash pop &>/dev/null; then
        log "Re-applied stashed changes."
      else
        log "Warning: Failed to re-apply stashed changes; please reapply manually."
      fi
    fi
  fi
}

# Clean empty directories (excluding .git)
clean_empty_dirs() {
  log "Cleaning empty directories..."
  find . -type d -empty -not -path "./.git*" -exec rm -rf {} + 2>/dev/null || true
}

# Find all immediate subdirectories under BASE_DIR that are git repos
get_all_repos() {
  find "$BASE_DIR" -mindepth 1 -maxdepth 1 -type d -exec test -d "{}/.git" \; -print || true
}

# Validate that remote exists and is reachable
validate_remote() {
  local repo="$1"
  cd "$repo"
  if ! git remote get-url "$GITHUB_REMOTE" &>/dev/null; then
    log "ERROR: Remote '$GITHUB_REMOTE' not set in $repo"
    cd - >/dev/null
    return 1
  fi
  if ! check_connectivity; then
    log "ERROR: Cannot reach remote in $repo"
    cd - >/dev/null
    return 1
  fi
  cd - >/dev/null
  return 0
}

# Checkout main, pull latest with rebase, handling stashes and conflicts without retry loop
checkout_and_pull_main() {
  abort_rebase_merge_if_any
  # Ensure on main branch
  if ! git checkout "$MAIN_BRANCH"; then
    log "ERROR: Cannot checkout $MAIN_BRANCH in $(pwd)"
    return 1
  fi

  stash_uncommitted

  # Pull with rebase once; if conflicts arise, abort rebase and return failure
  if ! git pull --rebase "$GITHUB_REMOTE" "$MAIN_BRANCH"; then
    log "ERROR: git pull --rebase failed on $(pwd) (likely due to conflicts or network). Aborting rebase."
    abort_rebase_merge_if_any
    pop_stash_if_any
    return 1
  fi

  pop_stash_if_any
  return 0
}

sync_repo() {
  local repo="$1"; shift
  local commit_msg="$1"
  log "=== Sync start: $repo ==="
  cd "$repo"

  if ! validate_remote "$repo"; then
    SUMMARY_FAIL+=("$repo (remote issue)"); cd - >/dev/null; return 1
  fi

  if ! checkout_and_pull_main; then
    log "ERROR: Could not update main in $repo"
    SUMMARY_FAIL+=("$repo (pull failed)"); cd - >/dev/null; return 1
  fi

  # Stage changes except sensitive
  git add --all -- ":(exclude)config/" ":(exclude).env"
  if ! git diff --cached --quiet; then
    if git commit -m "$commit_msg"; then
      log "Committed local changes in $repo"
    else
      log "WARN: Commit failed in $repo"
    fi
  else
    log "No local changes to commit in $repo"
  fi

  clean_empty_dirs

  # Pull again once after commit; handle conflicts similarly
  if ! checkout_and_pull_main; then
    log "ERROR: Pull after commit failed in $repo"
    SUMMARY_FAIL+=("$repo (pull after commit failed)"); cd - >/dev/null; return 1
  fi

  # Push with retry
  if ! retry_cmd git push "$GITHUB_REMOTE" "$MAIN_BRANCH"; then
    log "ERROR: Push failed in $repo"
    SUMMARY_FAIL+=("$repo (push failed)"); cd - >/dev/null; return 1
  fi

  log "Sync succeeded for $repo"
  SUMMARY_OK+=("$repo")
  cd - >/dev/null
  return 0
}

merge_branches() {
  local repo="$1"; shift
  local auto_resolve="$1"; shift
  local branches=( "$@" )
  log "=== Merge start: $repo branches: ${branches[*]} ==="
  cd "$repo"

  if ! validate_remote "$repo"; then
    SUMMARY_FAIL+=("$repo (remote issue)"); cd - >/dev/null; return 1
  fi

  if ! checkout_and_pull_main; then
    log "ERROR: Could not update main before merge in $repo"
    SUMMARY_FAIL+=("$repo (pre-merge pull failed)"); cd - >/dev/null; return 1
  fi

  for br in "${branches[@]}"; do
    log "Merging $br into main in $repo"
    if ! retry_cmd git fetch "$GITHUB_REMOTE" "$br:$br"; then
      log "WARN: Failed to fetch $br in $repo"
      SUMMARY_FAIL+=("$repo (fetch $br failed)")
      continue
    fi

    if git merge --no-ff "$br" -m "Merged $br into $MAIN_BRANCH"; then
      log "Merged $br cleanly in $repo"
    else
      log "Conflict merging $br in $repo"
      if [[ "$auto_resolve" == "true" ]]; then
        log "Auto-resolving by accepting theirs for $br in $repo"
        git checkout --theirs . || log "Warn: checkout --theirs failed"
        git add . || log "Warn: git add after theirs failed"
        if git commit -m "Auto-resolved conflict: accepted theirs from $br"; then
          log "Auto-resolve commit succeeded"
        else
          log "Warn: commit auto-resolve failed"
        fi
      else
        log "ERROR: Conflict in $repo on branch $br; manual resolution required"
        SUMMARY_FAIL+=("$repo (conflict on $br)")
        abort_rebase_merge_if_any
        cd - >/dev/null
        return 1
      fi
    fi
  done

  clean_empty_dirs

  if ! retry_cmd git push "$GITHUB_REMOTE" "$MAIN_BRANCH"; then
    log "ERROR: Push after merge failed in $repo"
    SUMMARY_FAIL+=("$repo (push after merge failed)"); cd - >/dev/null; return 1
  fi

  log "Merge succeeded for $repo"
  SUMMARY_OK+=("$repo")
  cd - >/dev/null
  return 0
}

clean_repo() {
  local repo="$1"
  log "=== Clean start: $repo ==="
  cd "$repo"
  if git filter-repo --force --invert-paths \
       --path config/firebase-credentials.json \
       --path config/google-credentials.json \
       --path .env; then
    log "Filter-repo succeeded in $repo"
    if git remote | grep -q "^$GITHUB_REMOTE\$"; then
      if retry_cmd git push --force "$GITHUB_REMOTE" "$MAIN_BRANCH"; then
        log "Force-pushed cleaned history in $repo"
      else
        log "ERROR: Force-push after clean failed in $repo"
        SUMMARY_FAIL+=("$repo (clean push failed)")
      fi
    else
      log "No '$GITHUB_REMOTE' remote in $repo; skipping push"
      SUMMARY_FAIL+=("$repo (no origin for clean)")
    fi
  else
    log "ERROR: git filter-repo failed in $repo"
    SUMMARY_FAIL+=("$repo (filter-repo failed)")
  fi
  cd - >/dev/null
}

send_alert() {
  # Placeholder for alerting on failures, e.g. email or Slack
  :
}

usage() {
  cat <<EOF
Usage:
  $0 sync [commit message]                  # Commit & push local changes, pull upstream
  $0 merge [--auto-resolve] <branches...>   # Merge given branches into main
  $0 clean                                  # Clean sensitive files from history via git filter-repo

Examples:
  ./sync-git-auto.sh sync "My changes"
  ./sync-git-auto.sh merge --auto-resolve feature1 feature2
  ./sync-git-auto.sh clean
EOF
  exit 1
}

main() {
  # Prepare log directory
  if ! mkdir -p "$LOG_DIR"; then
    echo "ERROR: Could not create log directory: $LOG_DIR" >&2
    exit 1
  fi

  # Timestamp for this run
  RUN_TS="$(date +'%Y%m%d-%H%M%S')"
  RUN_LOG="$LOG_DIR/sync-git-auto-$RUN_TS.log"
  LATEST_LOG="$LOG_DIR/sync-git-auto-latest.log"

  # Ensure RUN_LOG exists so log() can append
  touch "$RUN_LOG"

  # Symlink latest log; if fails, fall back to copying
  if ln -sf "$RUN_LOG" "$LATEST_LOG" 2>/dev/null; then
    :
  else
    log "WARN: Could not create symlink $LATEST_LOG; falling back to copying"
    if cp -f "$RUN_LOG" "$LATEST_LOG"; then
      log "Copied log to $LATEST_LOG"
    else
      log "ERROR: Failed to copy log to $LATEST_LOG"
    fi
  fi

  acquire_lock

  if (( $# < 1 )); then
    usage
  fi

  local cmd="$1"; shift

  # Gather repos
  mapfile -t repos < <(get_all_repos)
  if (( ${#repos[@]} == 0 )); then
    log "No git repos found under $BASE_DIR"
    echo "No git repos found under $BASE_DIR. Exiting."
    exit 1
  fi

  case "$cmd" in
    sync)
      local commit_msg="${1:-Auto commit}"
      log "=== RUN sync; commit message: '$commit_msg' ==="
      for repo in "${repos[@]}"; do
        if ! sync_repo "$repo" "$commit_msg"; then
          log "Sync encountered issues in $repo"
        fi
      done
      ;;
    merge)
      local auto_resolve="false"
      if [[ "${1:-}" == "--auto-resolve" ]]; then
        auto_resolve="true"; shift
      fi
      if (( $# < 1 )); then
        log "ERROR: No branches specified for merge"
        usage
      fi
      local branches=( "$@" )
      log "=== RUN merge; auto_resolve=$auto_resolve; branches=${branches[*]} ==="
      for repo in "${repos[@]}"; do
        if ! merge_branches "$repo" "$auto_resolve" "${branches[@]}"; then
          log "Merge encountered issues in $repo"
        fi
      done
      ;;
    clean)
      log "=== RUN clean ==="
      for repo in "${repos[@]}"; do
        clean_repo "$repo"
      done
      ;;
    *)
      usage
      ;;
  esac

  # Summary in log
  log "=== Summary ==="
  log "Succeeded in:"
  for r in "${SUMMARY_OK[@]}"; do
    log "  - $r"
  done
  if (( ${#SUMMARY_FAIL[@]} > 0 )); then
    log "Failed or requires manual attention in:"
    for r in "${SUMMARY_FAIL[@]}"; do
      log "  - $r"
    done
    send_alert "sync-git-auto: Some repos failed or need manual resolution. Check log: $RUN_LOG"
  else
    log "All repos processed successfully."
  fi

  # ===== Human-friendly summary printed to stdout =====
  echo
  local count_ok=${#SUMMARY_OK[@]}
  local count_fail=${#SUMMARY_FAIL[@]}
  echo "=== sync-git-auto summary ==="
  echo "Total repositories processed: $((count_ok + count_fail))."
  echo "  • Succeeded: $count_ok"
  echo "  • Failed or needing attention: $count_fail"
  if (( count_fail > 0 )); then
    echo
    echo "Repositories with issues:"
    for item in "${SUMMARY_FAIL[@]}"; do
      # item is in form "/path/to/repo (reason)"
      echo "  - $item"
    done
    echo
    echo "Please inspect these repositories manually. Common steps:"
    echo "  * cd into the repo, run 'git status' to see unmerged/conflicting files."
    echo "  * Resolve conflicts, then 'git add' and 'git rebase --continue' or similar."
    echo "  * After fixing, you can re-run './sync-git-auto.sh sync \"Your commit message\"' to retry."
  fi
  echo
  echo "Detailed log is at: $RUN_LOG"
  echo "Latest-log symlink (or copy) at: $LATEST_LOG"
  echo "============================"
}

main "$@"
What’s new:

After the existing logging-based summary, we added a “Human-friendly summary” section in main, printing to stdout:

Total count of repos processed, succeeded vs failed.

If failures exist, list each with its reason, and brief guidance on resolving conflicts or remote issues.

Location of the detailed log file (RUN_LOG) and the “latest” symlink or copy (LATEST_LOG).

We also echo a message and exit early if no repos found under BASE_DIR.

The rest of the logic (handling pull conflicts by aborting, retrying network ops, etc.) remains as before.

With this version, when you run:

  - /c/Users/rehan/OneDrive/Desktop/github_repos/RepoB (remote issue)

  * Resolve conflicts, then 'git add' and 'git rebase --continue' or similar.

bash

Edit
#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail
IFS=$'\n\t'

# === Configuration ===
BASE_DIR="${BASE_DIR:-/c/Users/rehan/OneDrive/Desktop/github_repos}"
LOG_DIR="$BASE_DIR/logs"
LOCKFILE="$BASE_DIR/sync-git-auto.lock"
MAX_RETRIES=5
RETRY_WAIT_BASE=5
GITHUB_REMOTE="${GITHUB_REMOTE:-origin}"
MAIN_BRANCH="${MAIN_BRANCH:-main}"

declare -a SUMMARY_OK
declare -a SUMMARY_FAIL

timestamp() {
  date "+%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S"
}

log() {
  local msg="$*"
  echo "[$(timestamp)] $msg" | tee -a "$RUN_LOG"
}

cleanup() {
  local code=$?
  if [[ -f "$LOCKFILE" ]]; then rm -f "$LOCKFILE"; fi
  if (( code != 0 )); then
    log "Script exited with code $code"
  else
    log "Script completed successfully"
  fi
}
trap cleanup EXIT

acquire_lock() {
  if [[ -f "$LOCKFILE" ]]; then
    local pid; pid=$(<"$LOCKFILE")
    if kill -0 "$pid" &>/dev/null; then
      echo "Another instance (PID $pid) is running. Exiting." >&2
      exit 1
    else
      log "Stale lockfile detected (PID $pid not running). Overwriting."
    fi
  fi
  echo $$ > "$LOCKFILE"
}

retry_cmd() {
  local retries=0 wait_sec=$RETRY_WAIT_BASE
  local cmd=( "$@" )
  until "${cmd[@]}"; do
    ((retries++))
    if (( retries >= MAX_RETRIES )); then
      log "ERROR: Command failed after $retries attempts: ${cmd[*]}"
      return 1
    fi
    log "WARN: Command failed, retry $retries/$MAX_RETRIES: ${cmd[*]}"
    log "Retrying in $wait_sec seconds..."
    sleep "$wait_sec"
    wait_sec=$(( wait_sec * 2 ))
  done
}

check_connectivity() {
  if ! git ls-remote "$GITHUB_REMOTE" &>/dev/null; then
    log "ERROR: Cannot reach remote '$GITHUB_REMOTE' for $(pwd)."
    return 1
  fi
  return 0
}

abort_rebase_merge_if_any() {
  if [[ -d ".git/rebase-apply" || -d ".git/rebase-merge" ]]; then
    log "Detected in-progress rebase in $(pwd). Attempting to abort..."
    if git rebase --abort &>/dev/null; then log "Rebase aborted."; else log "Warning: Failed to abort rebase cleanly."; fi
  fi
  if [[ -f ".git/MERGE_HEAD" ]]; then
    log "Detected in-progress merge in $(pwd). Attempting to abort..."
    if git merge --abort &>/dev/null; then log "Merge aborted."; else log "Warning: Failed to abort merge cleanly."; fi
  fi
}

stash_uncommitted() {
  STASHED=0
  if ! git diff --quiet || ! git diff --cached --quiet || [[ -n "$(git ls-files --others --exclude-standard)" ]]; then
    if git stash push --include-untracked -m "sync-git-auto stash before pull" &>/dev/null; then
      log "Stashed local changes."; STASHED=1
    else
      log "Warning: Failed to stash local changes."
    fi
  fi
}

pop_stash_if_any() {
  if [[ "${STASHED:-0}" -eq 1 ]]; then
    if git stash list | grep -q "sync-git-auto stash before pull"; then
      if git stash pop &>/dev/null; then log "Re-applied stashed changes."; else log "Warning: Failed to re-apply stashed changes; please reapply manually."; fi
    fi
  fi
}

clean_empty_dirs() {
  log "Cleaning empty directories..."
  find . -type d -empty -not -path "./.git*" -exec rm -rf {} + 2>/dev/null || true
}

get_all_repos() {
  find "$BASE_DIR" -mindepth 1 -maxdepth 1 -type d -exec test -d "{}/.git" \; -print || true
}

validate_remote() {
  local repo="$1"
  cd "$repo"
  if ! git remote get-url "$GITHUB_REMOTE" &>/dev/null; then
    log "ERROR: Remote '$GITHUB_REMOTE' not set in $repo"
    cd - >/dev/null; return 1
  fi
  if ! check_connectivity; then
    log "ERROR: Cannot reach remote in $repo"
    cd - >/dev/null; return 1
  fi
  cd - >/dev/null; return 0
}

# Capture detailed context on failure: conflicts or checkout issues
capture_repo_state() {
  log "Capturing repository state in $(pwd):"
  log "-> git status:"
  git status | tee -a "$RUN_LOG"
  log "-> Unmerged/conflicting files:"
  local conflicts
  conflicts=$(git diff --name-only --diff-filter=U || true)
  if [[ -n "$conflicts" ]]; then
    while IFS= read -r f; do log "   - $f"; done <<<"$conflicts"
  else
    log "   (none listed)"
  fi
  log "-> Recent reflog entries:"
  git reflog -n 5 | tee -a "$RUN_LOG"
}

checkout_and_pull_main() {
  abort_rebase_merge_if_any
  if ! git checkout "$MAIN_BRANCH"; then
    log "ERROR: Cannot checkout $MAIN_BRANCH in $(pwd)"
    capture_repo_state
    return 1
  fi

  stash_uncommitted

  if ! git pull --rebase "$GITHUB_REMOTE" "$MAIN_BRANCH"; then
    log "ERROR: git pull --rebase failed on $(pwd) (likely due to conflicts or network). Aborting rebase."
    abort_rebase_merge_if_any
    capture_repo_state
    pop_stash_if_any
    return 1
  fi

  pop_stash_if_any
  return 0
}

sync_repo() {
  local repo="$1"; shift
  local commit_msg="$1"
  log "=== Sync start: $repo ==="
  cd "$repo"

  if ! validate_remote "$repo"; then
    SUMMARY_FAIL+=("$repo (remote issue)"); cd - >/dev/null; return 1
  fi

  if ! checkout_and_pull_main; then
    log "ERROR: Could not update main in $repo"
    SUMMARY_FAIL+=("$repo (pull failed or conflicts)"); cd - >/dev/null; return 1
  fi

  git add --all -- ":(exclude)config/" ":(exclude).env"
  if ! git diff --cached --quiet; then
    if git commit -m "$commit_msg"; then
      log "Committed local changes in $repo"
    else
      log "WARN: Commit failed in $repo"
    fi
  else
    log "No local changes to commit in $repo"
  fi

  clean_empty_dirs

  if ! checkout_and_pull_main; then
    log "ERROR: Pull after commit failed in $repo"
    SUMMARY_FAIL+=("$repo (pull after commit failed or conflicts)"); cd - >/dev/null; return 1
  fi

  if ! retry_cmd git push "$GITHUB_REMOTE" "$MAIN_BRANCH"; then
    log "ERROR: Push failed in $repo"
    SUMMARY_FAIL+=("$repo (push failed)"); cd - >/dev/null; return 1
  fi

  log "Sync succeeded for $repo"
  SUMMARY_OK+=("$repo")
  cd - >/dev/null; return 0
}

merge_branches() {
  local repo="$1"; shift
  local auto_resolve="$1"; shift
  local branches=( "$@" )
  log "=== Merge start: $repo branches: ${branches[*]} ==="
  cd "$repo"

  if ! validate_remote "$repo"; then
    SUMMARY_FAIL+=("$repo (remote issue)"); cd - >/dev/null; return 1
  fi

  if ! checkout_and_pull_main; then
    log "ERROR: Could not update main before merge in $repo"
    SUMMARY_FAIL+=("$repo (pre-merge pull failed)"); cd - >/dev/null; return 1
  fi

  for br in "${branches[@]}"; do
    log "Merging $br into main in $repo"
    if ! retry_cmd git fetch "$GITHUB_REMOTE" "$br:$br"; then
      log "WARN: Failed to fetch $br in $repo"
      SUMMARY_FAIL+=("$repo (fetch $br failed)"); continue
    fi

    if git merge --no-ff "$br" -m "Merged $br into $MAIN_BRANCH"; then
      log "Merged $br cleanly in $repo"
    else
      log "Conflict merging $br in $repo"
      if [[ "$auto_resolve" == "true" ]]; then
        log "Auto-resolving by accepting theirs for $br in $repo"
        git checkout --theirs . || log "Warn: checkout --theirs failed"
        git add . || log "Warn: git add after theirs failed"
        if git commit -m "Auto-resolved conflict: accepted theirs from $br"; then
          log "Auto-resolve commit succeeded"
        else
          log "Warn: commit auto-resolve failed"
        fi
      else
        log "ERROR: Conflict in $repo on branch $br; manual resolution required"
        capture_repo_state
        SUMMARY_FAIL+=("$repo (conflict on $br)")
        abort_rebase_merge_if_any
        cd - >/dev/null; return 1
      fi
    fi
  done

  clean_empty_dirs

  if ! retry_cmd git push "$GITHUB_REMOTE" "$MAIN_BRANCH"; then
    log "ERROR: Push after merge failed in $repo"
    SUMMARY_FAIL+=("$repo (push after merge failed)"); cd - >/dev/null; return 1
  fi

  log "Merge succeeded for $repo"
  SUMMARY_OK+=("$repo")
  cd - >/dev/null; return 0
}

clean_repo() {
  local repo="$1"
  log "=== Clean start: $repo ==="
  cd "$repo"
  if git filter-repo --force --invert-paths \
       --path config/firebase-credentials.json \
       --path config/google-credentials.json \
       --path .env; then
    log "Filter-repo succeeded in $repo"
    if git remote | grep -q "^$GITHUB_REMOTE\$"; then
      if retry_cmd git push --force "$GITHUB_REMOTE" "$MAIN_BRANCH"; then
        log "Force-pushed cleaned history in $repo"
      else
        log "ERROR: Force-push after clean failed in $repo"
        SUMMARY_FAIL+=("$repo (clean push failed)")
      fi
    else
      log "No '$GITHUB_REMOTE' remote in $repo; skipping push"
      SUMMARY_FAIL+=("$repo (no origin for clean)")
    fi
  else
    log "ERROR: git filter-repo failed in $repo"
    SUMMARY_FAIL+=("$repo (filter-repo failed)")
  fi
  cd - >/dev/null
}

send_alert() {
  # Placeholder for alerting on failures
  :
}

usage() {
  cat <<EOF
Usage:
  $0 sync [commit message]                  # Commit & push local changes, pull upstream
  $0 merge [--auto-resolve] <branches...>   # Merge given branches into main
  $0 clean                                  # Clean sensitive files from history via git filter-repo

Examples:
  ./sync-git-auto.sh sync "My changes"
  ./sync-git-auto.sh merge --auto-resolve feature1 feature2
  ./sync-git-auto.sh clean
EOF
  exit 1
}

main() {
  if ! mkdir -p "$LOG_DIR"; then
    echo "ERROR: Could not create log directory: $LOG_DIR" >&2
    exit 1
  fi

  RUN_TS="$(date +'%Y%m%d-%H%M%S')"
  RUN_LOG="$LOG_DIR/sync-git-auto-$RUN_TS.log"
  LATEST_LOG="$LOG_DIR/sync-git-auto-latest.log"

  touch "$RUN_LOG"
  if ! ln -sf "$RUN_LOG" "$LATEST_LOG" 2>/dev/null; then
    log "WARN: Could not create symlink $LATEST_LOG; falling back to copying"
    if cp -f "$RUN_LOG" "$LATEST_LOG"; then log "Copied log to $LATEST_LOG"; else log "ERROR: Failed to copy log to $LATEST_LOG"; fi
  fi

  acquire_lock

  if (( $# < 1 )); then usage; fi
  local cmd="$1"; shift

  mapfile -t repos < <(get_all_repos)
  if (( ${#repos[@]} == 0 )); then
    log "No git repos found under $BASE_DIR"
    echo "No git repos found under $BASE_DIR. Exiting."
    exit 1
  fi

  case "$cmd" in
    sync)
      local commit_msg="${1:-Auto commit}"
      log "=== RUN sync; commit message: '$commit_msg' ==="
      for repo in "${repos[@]}"; do
        if ! sync_repo "$repo" "$commit_msg"; then
          log "Sync encountered issues in $repo"
        fi
      done
      ;;
    merge)
      local auto_resolve="false"
      if [[ "${1:-}" == "--auto-resolve" ]]; then auto_resolve="true"; shift; fi
      if (( $# < 1 )); then log "ERROR: No branches specified for merge"; usage; fi
      local branches=( "$@" )
      log "=== RUN merge; auto_resolve=$auto_resolve; branches=${branches[*]} ==="
      for repo in "${repos[@]}"; do
        if ! merge_branches "$repo" "$auto_resolve" "${branches[@]}"; then
          log "Merge encountered issues in $repo"
        fi
      done
      ;;
    clean)
      log "=== RUN clean ==="
      for repo in "${repos[@]}"; do clean_repo "$repo"; done
      ;;
    *)
      usage
      ;;
  esac

  log "=== Summary ==="
  log "Succeeded in:"
  for r in "${SUMMARY_OK[@]}"; do log "  - $r"; done
  if (( ${#SUMMARY_FAIL[@]} > 0 )); then
    log "Failed or requires manual attention in:"
    for r in "${SUMMARY_FAIL[@]}"; do log "  - $r"; done
    send_alert "sync-git-auto: Some repos failed or need manual resolution. Check log: $RUN_LOG"
  else
    log "All repos processed successfully."
  fi

  # Human-friendly summary
  echo
  local count_ok=${#SUMMARY_OK[@]}
  local count_fail=${#SUMMARY_FAIL[@]}
  echo "=== sync-git-auto summary ==="
  echo "Processed $((count_ok + count_fail)) repos: $count_ok succeeded, $count_fail issues."
  if (( count_fail > 0 )); then
    echo
    echo "Issues detected in the following repos (see detailed log for context):"
    for item in "${SUMMARY_FAIL[@]}"; do
      echo "  - $item"
    done
    echo
    echo "For each, inspect the repository directory:"
    echo "  * cd into the repo; run 'git status' to see current state."
    echo "  * Look in the log ($RUN_LOG) for captured 'git status' and conflicting files."
    echo "  * Resolve conflicts or remote issues, then re-run sync-git-auto."
  fi
  echo
  echo "Detailed log: $RUN_LOG"
  echo "Latest log link (or copy): $LATEST_LOG"
  echo "============================"
}

main "$@"
Changes made:

Introduced a capture_repo_state function: on pull/rebase failure or checkout failure, logs git status, unmerged files (git diff --name-only --diff-filter=U), and recent reflog entries for context.

In checkout_and_pull_main, when git checkout or git pull --rebase fails, we call capture_repo_state so the log contains details aiding diagnosis.

In sync_repo, failure reasons now tagged (pull failed or conflicts) so summary indicates conflicts.

The human-friendly summary now directs you to inspect each failed repo, referencing the detailed log where the captured state appears.

This gives more visibility into current state and error context to help resolve conflicts or other issues.
