export AUTO_MERGE_STRATEGY=theirs   # or "ours"
bash -x ./sync-git-auto.sh sync "Your commit message"
bash
Copy
Edit
#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail
IFS=$'\n\t'

# === Configuration ===
BASE_DIR="${BASE_DIR:-/c/Users/rehan/OneDrive/Desktop/github_repos}"
LOG_DIR="${LOG_DIR:-$BASE_DIR/logs}"
LOCKFILE="$BASE_DIR/sync-git-auto.lock"
MAX_RETRIES=5
RETRY_WAIT_BASE=5
GITHUB_REMOTE="${GITHUB_REMOTE:-origin}"
MAIN_BRANCH="${MAIN_BRANCH:-main}"
SENSITIVE_PATHS=("config/" ".env")
# Optional auto-merge strategy: "ours" or "theirs". Leave unset to require manual resolution.
AUTO_MERGE_STRATEGY="${AUTO_MERGE_STRATEGY:-}"

# Summary arrays
declare -a SUMMARY_OK
declare -a SUMMARY_FAIL
declare -a NEEDS_MANUAL_RESOLVE
declare -a CONFLICT_REPORTS  # stores "<repo-path>:<report-file>"

timestamp() { date "+%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S"; }

log() {
  echo "[$(timestamp)] $*" | tee -a "$RUN_LOG"
}

cleanup() {
  local code=$?
  [[ -f "$LOCKFILE" ]] && rm -f "$LOCKFILE"
  if (( code != 0 )); then
    log "Script exited with code $code"
  else
    log "Script completed successfully"
  fi
}
trap cleanup EXIT

acquire_lock() {
  if [[ -f "$LOCKFILE" ]]; then
    local pid; pid=$(<"$LOCKFILE")
    if kill -0 "$pid" &>/dev/null; then
      echo "Another instance (PID $pid) running. Exiting." >&2
      exit 1
    else
      log "Stale lockfile detected (PID $pid not running). Overwriting."
    fi
  fi
  echo $$ > "$LOCKFILE"
}

retry_cmd() {
  local retries=0 wait_sec=$RETRY_WAIT_BASE
  local cmd=( "$@" )
  until "${cmd[@]}"; do
    ((retries++))
    if (( retries >= MAX_RETRIES )); then
      log "ERROR: Command failed after $retries attempts: ${cmd[*]}"
      return 1
    fi
    log "WARN: Command failed, retry $retries/$MAX_RETRIES: ${cmd[*]}"
    sleep "$wait_sec"
    wait_sec=$(( wait_sec * 2 ))
  done
}

check_connectivity() {
  if ! git ls-remote "$GITHUB_REMOTE" &>/dev/null; then
    log "ERROR: Cannot reach remote '$GITHUB_REMOTE' for $(pwd)."
    return 1
  fi
  return 0
}

abort_rebase_merge_if_any() {
  if [[ -d ".git/rebase-apply" || -d ".git/rebase-merge" ]]; then
    log "Detected in-progress rebase in $(pwd). Aborting..."
    git rebase --abort &>/dev/null || log "Warning: rebase abort failed"
  fi
  if [[ -f ".git/MERGE_HEAD" ]]; then
    log "Detected in-progress merge in $(pwd). Aborting..."
    git merge --abort &>/dev/null || log "Warning: merge abort failed"
  fi
}

stash_uncommitted() {
  STASHED=0
  if ! git diff --quiet || ! git diff --cached --quiet || [[ -n "$(git ls-files --others --exclude-standard)" ]]; then
    if git stash push --include-untracked -m "sync-git-auto stash" &>/dev/null; then
      log "Stashed local changes."; STASHED=1
    else
      log "Warning: Failed to stash local changes."
    fi
  fi
}

pop_stash_if_any() {
  if [[ "${STASHED:-0}" -eq 1 ]]; then
    if git stash list | grep -q "sync-git-auto stash"; then
      git stash pop &>/dev/null && log "Re-applied stashed changes." || log "Warning: Failed to reapply stash."
    fi
  fi
}

clean_empty_dirs() {
  log "Cleaning empty directories..."
  find . -type d -empty -not -path "./.git*" -exec rm -rf {} + 2>/dev/null || true
}

get_all_repos() {
  find "$BASE_DIR" -mindepth 1 -maxdepth 1 -type d -exec test -d "{}/.git" \; -print || true
}

validate_remote() {
  local repo="$1"; cd "$repo"
  if ! git remote get-url "$GITHUB_REMOTE" &>/dev/null; then
    log "ERROR: Remote '$GITHUB_REMOTE' not set in $repo"
    cd - >/dev/null; return 1
  fi
  if ! check_connectivity; then
    log "ERROR: Cannot reach remote in $repo"
    cd - >/dev/null; return 1
  fi
  cd - >/dev/null; return 0
}

capture_repo_state() {
  log "Capturing state in $(pwd):"
  log "-> git status:"
  git status | tee -a "$RUN_LOG"
  log "-> Unmerged/conflicts:"
  local conflicts
  conflicts=$(git diff --name-only --diff-filter=U || true)
  if [[ -n "$conflicts" ]]; then
    while IFS= read -r f; do log "   - $f"; done <<<"$conflicts"
  else
    log "   (none)"
  fi
  log "-> Recent reflog:"
  git reflog -n 5 | tee -a "$RUN_LOG"
}

ensure_gitignore_and_unstage_sensitive() {
  # At repo root: append sensitive patterns and unstage any staged sensitive files
  local changed=0
  for pat in "${SENSITIVE_PATHS[@]}"; do
    if ! grep -qxF "$pat" .gitignore 2>/dev/null; then
      echo "$pat" >> .gitignore
      changed=1
      log "Appended '$pat' to .gitignore"
    fi
  done
  if (( changed )); then
    git add .gitignore
    git commit -m "chore: update .gitignore to exclude sensitive files" || log "Warn: .gitignore commit failed"
  fi
  # Unstage any staged sensitive files
  local staged
  staged=$(git diff --cached --name-only || true)
  while IFS= read -r f; do
    for pat in "${SENSITIVE_PATHS[@]}"; do
      if [[ "$f" == "$pat"* || "$f" == "$pat" ]]; then
        git rm --cached --ignore-unmatch "$f" &>/dev/null && log "Unstaged sensitive file: $f"
      fi
    done
  done <<<"$staged"
}

# Save local work on a WIP branch if necessary, then update main by merging remote and WIP
prepare_and_pull_main() {
  abort_rebase_merge_if_any

  # Determine if local changes or local commits diverge from remote
  local need_wip=0
  # Uncommitted?
  if ! git diff --quiet || ! git diff --cached --quiet || [[ -n "$(git ls-files --others --exclude-standard)" ]]; then
    need_wip=1
  else
    # Check divergence: compare HEAD and origin/main if both exist
    if git rev-parse --verify HEAD &>/dev/null && git rev-parse --verify "$GITHUB_REMOTE/$MAIN_BRANCH" &>/dev/null; then
      local LOCAL_HASH REMOTE_HASH
      LOCAL_HASH=$(git rev-parse HEAD)
      REMOTE_HASH=$(git rev-parse "$GITHUB_REMOTE/$MAIN_BRANCH")
      if [[ "$LOCAL_HASH" != "$REMOTE_HASH" ]]; then
        need_wip=1
      fi
    fi
  fi

  local wip_branch=""
  if (( need_wip )); then
    # Create unique WIP branch
    local ts=$(date +'%Y%m%d-%H%M%S')
    wip_branch="sync-wip-$ts"
    git branch "$wip_branch" || { log "ERROR: Could not create WIP branch $wip_branch"; return 1; }
    log "Created WIP branch '$wip_branch' to save local work"
  fi

  # Checkout main
  if ! git checkout "$MAIN_BRANCH"; then
    log "ERROR: Cannot checkout $MAIN_BRANCH in $(pwd)"; capture_repo_state; return 1
  fi

  # Fetch remote main
  if ! retry_cmd git fetch "$GITHUB_REMOTE" "$MAIN_BRANCH"; then
    log "ERROR: fetch failed for $GITHUB_REMOTE/$MAIN_BRANCH"; return 1
  fi

  # Merge remote/main into local main (fast-forward or merge commit)
  if ! git merge --ff-only "$GITHUB_REMOTE/$MAIN_BRANCH" &>/dev/null; then
    log "Local main not fast-forwardable; merging remote/main"
    if ! git merge "$GITHUB_REMOTE/$MAIN_BRANCH" -m "Merge remote $GITHUB_REMOTE/$MAIN_BRANCH into main"; then
      log "ERROR: Merge remote/main into local main failed. Attempting auto-merge strategy or reporting."
      capture_repo_state
      # Save conflict diff
      local repo_name
      repo_name=$(basename "$(pwd)")
      local report="$LOG_DIR/${repo_name}-conflict-remote-$(date +'%Y%m%d-%H%M%S').diff"
      git diff > "$report"
      CONFLICT_REPORTS+=("$(pwd):$report")
      # Try auto-merge strategy if set
      if [[ -n "$AUTO_MERGE_STRATEGY" ]]; then
        log "Attempting auto-merge strategy '$AUTO_MERGE_STRATEGY' for remote/main"
        # Abort current failed merge, then retry with -X
        git merge --abort &>/dev/null || true
        if git merge -X"$AUTO_MERGE_STRATEGY" "$GITHUB_REMOTE/$MAIN_BRANCH" -m "Auto-merged remote/main with strategy $AUTO_MERGE_STRATEGY"; then
          log "Auto-merge with strategy '$AUTO_MERGE_STRATEGY' succeeded"
        else
          log "Auto-merge with strategy '$AUTO_MERGE_STRATEGY' failed"
          NEEDS_MANUAL_RESOLVE+=("$(pwd) (merge remote/main)")
          return 1
        fi
      else
        NEEDS_MANUAL_RESOLVE+=("$(pwd) (merge remote/main)")
        return 1
      fi
    else
      log "Merged remote/main into local main successfully"
    fi
  else
    log "Fast-forwarded main to $GITHUB_REMOTE/$MAIN_BRANCH"
  fi

  # Merge WIP branch back
  if [[ -n "$wip_branch" ]]; then
    log "Merging WIP branch '$wip_branch' into main"
    if git merge --no-ff "$wip_branch" -m "Merge local WIP ($wip_branch) into main"; then
      log "Merged WIP into main cleanly"
      git branch -d "$wip_branch" &>/dev/null && log "Deleted WIP branch '$wip_branch'"
    else
      log "Conflict merging WIP branch '$wip_branch' into main. Attempting auto-merge strategy or reporting."
      capture_repo_state
      # Save conflict diff
      local repo_name
      repo_name=$(basename "$(pwd)")
      local report="$LOG_DIR/${repo_name}-conflict-wip-$(date +'%Y%m%d-%H%M%S').diff"
      git diff > "$report"
      CONFLICT_REPORTS+=("$(pwd):$report")
      if [[ -n "$AUTO_MERGE_STRATEGY" ]]; then
        log "Attempting auto-merge strategy '$AUTO_MERGE_STRATEGY' for WIP"
        git merge --abort &>/dev/null || true
        if git merge -X"$AUTO_MERGE_STRATEGY" "$wip_branch" -m "Auto-merge WIP with strategy $AUTO_MERGE_STRATEGY"; then
          log "Auto-merge WIP with strategy '$AUTO_MERGE_STRATEGY' succeeded"
          git branch -d "$wip_branch" &>/dev/null && log "Deleted WIP branch '$wip_branch'"
        else
          log "Auto-merge WIP with strategy '$AUTO_MERGE_STRATEGY' failed"
          NEEDS_MANUAL_RESOLVE+=("$(pwd) (merge WIP)")
          return 1
        fi
      else
        NEEDS_MANUAL_RESOLVE+=("$(pwd) (merge WIP)")
        return 1
      fi
    fi
  fi

  return 0
}

sync_repo() {
  local repo="$1"; shift
  local commit_msg="$1"
  log "=== Sync start: $repo ==="
  cd "$repo"
  if ! validate_remote "$repo"; then
    SUMMARY_FAIL+=("$repo (remote issue)"); cd - >/dev/null; return 1
  fi

  # Stage & commit uncommitted changes to avoid loss
  if ! git diff --quiet || ! git diff --cached --quiet || [[ -n "$(git ls-files --others --exclude-standard)" ]]; then
    git add .
    if git commit -m "$commit_msg"; then
      log "Committed local uncommitted changes on main"
    else
      log "WARN: Commit of local changes failed"
    fi
  fi

  ensure_gitignore_and_unstage_sensitive

  # Integrate remote/main and local work
  if ! prepare_and_pull_main; then
    log "ERROR: Could not integrate remote/main with local in $repo"
    SUMMARY_FAIL+=("$repo (needs manual merge)")
    cd - >/dev/null; return 1
  fi

  ensure_gitignore_and_unstage_sensitive
  clean_empty_dirs

  # Push updated main
  if ! retry_cmd git push "$GITHUB_REMOTE" "$MAIN_BRANCH"; then
    log "ERROR: Push failed in $repo"
    SUMMARY_FAIL+=("$repo (push failed)"); cd - >/dev/null; return 1
  fi

  SUMMARY_OK+=("$repo")
  log "Sync succeeded for $repo"
  cd - >/dev/null; return 0
}

merge_branches() {
  local repo="$1"; shift
  local auto_resolve="$1"; shift
  local branches=( "$@" )
  log "=== Merge start: $repo branches: ${branches[*]} ==="
  cd "$repo"
  if ! validate_remote "$repo"; then
    SUMMARY_FAIL+=("$repo (remote issue)"); cd - >/dev/null; return 1
  fi

  # First sync with remote
  if ! sync_repo "$repo" "WIP before merge"; then
    log "ERROR: Pre-merge sync failed in $repo"
    cd - >/dev/null; return 1
  fi

  for br in "${branches[@]}"; do
    log "Merging branch '$br' into main in $repo"
    if ! retry_cmd git fetch "$GITHUB_REMOTE" "$br:$br"; then
      log "WARN: Failed to fetch $br"; SUMMARY_FAIL+=("$repo (fetch $br failed)"); continue
    fi
    if git merge --no-ff "$br" -m "Merge $br into main"; then
      log "Merged $br cleanly"
    else
      log "Conflict merging $br in $repo. Attempting auto-merge or reporting."
      capture_repo_state
      # Save conflict diff
      local repo_name=$(basename "$(pwd)")
      local report="$LOG_DIR/${repo_name}-conflict-merge-${br}-$(date +'%Y%m%d-%H%M%S').diff"
      git diff > "$report"
      CONFLICT_REPORTS+=("$(pwd):$report")
      if [[ "$auto_resolve" == "true" && -n "$AUTO_MERGE_STRATEGY" ]]; then
        log "Attempting auto-merge strategy '$AUTO_MERGE_STRATEGY' for branch $br"
        git merge --abort &>/dev/null || true
        if git merge -X"$AUTO_MERGE_STRATEGY" "$br" -m "Auto-merge $br with strategy $AUTO_MERGE_STRATEGY"; then
          log "Auto-merge $br succeeded"
        else
          log "Auto-merge $br failed"
          NEEDS_MANUAL_RESOLVE+=("$(pwd) (conflict merging $br)")
          continue
        fi
      else
        NEEDS_MANUAL_RESOLVE+=("$(pwd) (conflict merging $br)")
        continue
      fi
    fi
    ensure_gitignore_and_unstage_sensitive
  done

  clean_empty_dirs

  if ! retry_cmd git push "$GITHUB_REMOTE" "$MAIN_BRANCH"; then
    SUMMARY_FAIL+=("$repo (push after merge failed)"); cd - >/dev/null; return 1
  fi

  SUMMARY_OK+=("$repo")
  log "Merge succeeded for $repo"
  cd - >/dev/null; return 0
}

clean_repo() {
  local repo="$1"
  log "=== Clean start: $repo ==="
  cd "$repo"
  if git filter-repo --force --invert-paths \
       --path config/firebase-credendials.json \
       --path config/google-credendials.json \
       --path .env; then
    log "Filter-repo succeeded"
    if git remote | grep -q "^$GITHUB_REMOTE\$"; then
      retry_cmd git push --force "$GITHUB_REMOTE" "$MAIN_BRANCH" && log "Force-pushed cleaned history" || SUMMARY_FAIL+=("$repo (clean push failed)")
    else
      log "No remote; skipping push"; SUMMARY_FAIL+=("$repo (no origin for clean)"
)
    fi
  else
    SUMMARY_FAIL+=("$repo (filter-repo failed)"); log "ERROR: filter-repo failed"
  fi
  cd - >/dev/null
}

usage() {
  cat <<EOF
Usage:
  $0 sync [commit message]                  # Commit local changes, merge remote changes, push
  $0 merge [--auto-resolve] <branches...>   # Merge given branches into main after syncing
  $0 clean                                  # Remove sensitive files from history

To enable automatic merge strategies on conflict, export:
  export AUTO_MERGE_STRATEGY=ours   # or "theirs"
EOF
  exit 1
}

main() {
  mkdir -p "$LOG_DIR"
  RUN_TS="$(date +'%Y%m%d-%H%M%S')"
  RUN_LOG="$LOG_DIR/sync-git-auto-$RUN_TS.log"
  LATEST_LOG="$LOG_DIR/sync-git-auto-latest.log"
  touch "$RUN_LOG"
  ln -sf "$RUN_LOG" "$LATEST_LOG" 2>/dev/null || cp -f "$RUN_LOG" "$LATEST_LOG"

  acquire_lock

  if (( $# < 1 )); then usage; fi
  local cmd="$1"; shift

  mapfile -t repos < <(get_all_repos)
  if (( ${#repos[@]} == 0 )); then
    log "No git repos under $BASE_DIR"; echo "No repos found. Exiting."; exit 1
  fi

  case "$cmd" in
    sync)
      local commit_msg="${1:-Auto commit}"
      log "=== RUN sync; commit message: '$commit_msg' ==="
      for repo in "${repos[@]}"; do
        sync_repo "$repo" "$commit_msg" || log "Sync issues in $repo"
      done
      ;;
    merge)
      local auto_resolve="false"
      if [[ "${1:-}" == "--auto-resolve" ]]; then auto_resolve="true"; shift; fi
      if (( $# < 1 )); then log "ERROR: No branches for merge"; usage; fi
      local branches=( "$@" )
      log "=== RUN merge; auto_resolve=$auto_resolve; branches=${branches[*]} ==="
      for repo in "${repos[@]}"; do
        merge_branches "$repo" "$auto_resolve" "${branches[@]}" || log "Merge issues in $repo"
      done
      ;;
    clean)
      log "=== RUN clean ==="
      for repo in "${repos[@]}"; do clean_repo "$repo"; done
      ;;
    *)
      usage
      ;;
  esac

  # Summary
  log "=== Summary ==="
  log "Succeeded in:"
  if (( ${#SUMMARY_OK[@]} > 0 )); then
    for r in "${SUMMARY_OK[@]}"; do log "  - $r"; done
  else
    log "  - (none)"
  fi
  if (( ${#SUMMARY_FAIL[@]} > 0 )); then
    log "Failed or remote issues:"
    for r in "${SUMMARY_FAIL[@]}"; do log "  - $r"; done
  fi
  if (( ${#NEEDS_MANUAL_RESOLVE[@]} > 0 )); then
    log "Repos needing manual conflict resolution:"
    for r in "${NEEDS_MANUAL_RESOLVE[@]}"; do log "  - $r"; done
  fi
  if (( ${#CONFLICT_REPORTS[@]} > 0 )); then
    log "Conflict diff reports:"
    for entry in "${CONFLICT_REPORTS[@]}"; do
      log "  - $entry"
    done
  fi

  # Human-readable summary
  echo
  local ok=${#SUMMARY_OK[@]} fail=${#SUMMARY_FAIL[@]} need=${#NEEDS_MANUAL_RESOLVE[@]}
  echo "=== sync-git-auto summary ==="
  echo "Processed $((ok+fail+need)) repos: $ok succeeded, $fail failed/remote-issues, $need need manual merge."
  if (( need>0 )); then
    echo "Repos requiring manual resolution. Review conflict reports under logs, then in each:"
    echo "  cd <repo>"
    echo "  # fix conflicts in your editor:"
    echo "  git add <resolved files>"
    echo "  git commit"
    echo "  git push origin $MAIN_BRANCH"
  fi
  if (( ${#CONFLICT_REPORTS[@]} > 0 )); then
    echo "Conflict diff reports generated:"
    for entry in "${CONFLICT_REPORTS[@]}"; do
      # entry format: "/path/to/repo:/path/to/logs/repo-conflict-....diff"
      local repo_path="${entry%%:*}"
      local report_file="${entry#*:}"
      echo "  Repo: $repo_path → Report: $report_file"
    done
  fi
  echo "Log: $RUN_LOG"
  echo "Latest link: $LATEST_LOG"
}

main "$@"
Explanation of key refinements:

WIP branch & preserving local work

Before updating main, the script checks if there are uncommitted changes or local commits that diverge from remote. If so, it creates a timestamped WIP branch (sync-wip-YYYYMMDD-HHMMSS) to save that work.

Then it checks out main, fetches remote, and merges remote/main into local main (fast-forward or merge commit). If that merge yields conflicts, it captures state, saves a diff report, and—if AUTO_MERGE_STRATEGY is set—attempts git merge -X ours/theirs. If auto-merge fails or isn’t set, the repo is marked for manual resolution.

After updating main, it merges the WIP branch back. Again, on conflict, it saves a diff report and optionally tries the auto-merge strategy, otherwise stops for manual resolution.

Enhanced conflict logging & reports

On any merge conflict (remote/main or WIP merge), the script runs git diff and writes it to a file under logs/, named <repo-name>-conflict-*.diff. At the end, the summary prints paths to these reports so you can open and inspect exactly what conflicted.

Optional auto-merge strategy

If you set export AUTO_MERGE_STRATEGY=ours (to prefer local) or theirs (to prefer remote), the script will attempt git merge -Xours or -Xtheirs when a conflict arises. This can automatically resolve trivial conflicts according to that preference. If it still fails, it falls back to manual resolution.

Retry logic

retry_cmd wraps fetch, push, etc., with exponential backoff up to MAX_RETRIES. This helps transient network issues.

Sensitive files

As before, .gitignore is updated to include config/ and .env, and any staged sensitive files are unstaged.

Summary

At the end, the script logs which repos succeeded, which had remote issues, which need manual resolution, and paths to conflict diff reports. You can open those diffs to see exactly the conflicting hunks.

Usage

Run: bash -x ./sync-git-auto.sh sync "Your commit message".

To enable auto-merge strategy:

bash
Copy
Edit
export AUTO_MERGE_STRATEGY=theirs   # or "ours"
bash -x ./sync-git-auto.sh sync "Your commit message"
For merges across branches:
bash ./sync-git-auto.sh merge --auto-resolve feature1 feature2 plus AUTO_MERGE_STRATEGY if desired.

Manual resolution flow

If a repo appears under “need manual merge” in the summary, do:

bash
Copy
Edit
cd path/to/repo
# Inspect conflict diff: logs/<repo-name>-conflict-*.diff
# Open in VSCode, fix conflicts in the files
git add <resolved files>
git commit
git push origin main
After resolving, re-run the script; it will detect no divergence and simply push or fast-forward.

With these refinements, the script attempts to preserve and merge both local (your VSCode progress) and remote (Jules’s updates) sequentially, logs detailed conflict reports, retries operations, and only stops when genuine manual conflict resolution is required.

#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail
IFS=$'\n'

BASE_DIR="/c/Users/rehan/OneDrive/Desktop/github_repos"
LOG_DIR="$BASE_DIR/logs"
LOCKFILE="$BASE_DIR/sync-git-auto.lock"
MAX_RETRIES=5
RETRY_WAIT_BASE=5
GITHUB_REMOTE="origin"
MAIN_BRANCH="main"
SENSITIVE_PATHS=("config/" ".env")
AUTO_MERGE_STRATEGY="${AUTO_MERGE_STRATEGY:-theirs}"

declare -a SUMMARY_OK=()
declare -a SUMMARY_FAIL=()
declare -a NEEDS_MANUAL_RESOLVE=()
declare -a CONFLICT_REPORTS=()

trap cleanup EXIT

timestamp() { date '+%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S'; }

log() {
  echo "[$(timestamp)] $*" | tee -a "$RUN_LOG"
}

cleanup() {
  local code=$?
  [[ -f "$LOCKFILE" ]] && rm -f "$LOCKFILE"
  if [[ $code -ne 0 ]]; then
    log "Script exited with code $code"
  fi
  exit $code
}

acquire_lock() {
  if [[ -f "$LOCKFILE" ]]; then
    echo "Another sync is running. Exiting."
    exit 1
  fi
  echo $$ > "$LOCKFILE"
}

retry_cmd() {
  local retries=0 wait_sec=$RETRY_WAIT_BASE
  until "${@}"; do
    ((retries++))
    if ((retries >= MAX_RETRIES)); then
      log "Failed after $MAX_RETRIES attempts: ${*}"
      return 1
    fi
    log "Retrying in $wait_sec seconds..."
    sleep "$wait_sec"
    ((wait_sec *= 2))
  done
}

get_all_repos() {
  find "$BASE_DIR" -mindepth 1 -maxdepth 1 -type d -exec test -d '{}/.git' ';' -print
}

validate_remote() {
  local repo=$1
  cd "$repo"
  if ! git remote get-url "$GITHUB_REMOTE" &>/dev/null; then
    log "ERROR: Remote '$GITHUB_REMOTE' not set in $repo"
    cd - &>/dev/null
    return 1
  fi
  if ! git ls-remote "$GITHUB_REMOTE" &>/dev/null; then
    log "ERROR: Cannot connect to remote '$GITHUB_REMOTE' in $repo"
    cd - &>/dev/null
    return 1
  fi
  cd - &>/dev/null
  return 0
}

ensure_gitignore_and_unstage_sensitive() {
  local changed=0
  for pat in "${SENSITIVE_PATHS[@]}"; do
    grep -qxF "$pat" .gitignore || echo "$pat" >> .gitignore
  done
  local staged
  staged=$(git diff --cached --name-only)
  while IFS= read -r f; do
    for pat in "${SENSITIVE_PATHS[@]}"; do
      [[ "$f" == $pat* ]] && git reset "$f"
    done
  done <<< "$staged"
}

abort_rebase_merge_if_any() {
  [[ -d .git/rebase-apply || -d .git/rebase-merge || -f .git/MERGE_HEAD ]] && git rebase --abort || true
}

clean_empty_dirs() {
  log "Cleaning empty directories..."
  find . -type d -empty -not -path './.git*' -exec rm -rf '{}' +
}

prepare_and_pull_main() {
  abort_rebase_merge_if_any
  local need_wip=0
  [[ -n "$(git status --porcelain)" ]] && need_wip=1
  git rev-parse --verify HEAD &>/dev/null || return 0
  git rev-parse --verify "$GITHUB_REMOTE/$MAIN_BRANCH" &>/dev/null || return 0
  local LOCAL_HASH REMOTE_HASH
  LOCAL_HASH=$(git rev-parse HEAD)
  REMOTE_HASH=$(git rev-parse "$GITHUB_REMOTE/$MAIN_BRANCH")

  local wip_branch=""
  if [[ "$LOCAL_HASH" != "$REMOTE_HASH" ]]; then
    need_wip=1
  fi

  if (( need_wip )); then
    local ts
    ts=$(date +%Y%m%d-%H%M%S)
    wip_branch="sync-wip-$ts"
    git branch "$wip_branch"
    log "Created WIP branch '$wip_branch' to save local work"
  fi

  git checkout "$MAIN_BRANCH"
  retry_cmd git fetch "$GITHUB_REMOTE" "$MAIN_BRANCH"
  git merge --ff-only "$GITHUB_REMOTE/$MAIN_BRANCH" || true
  log "Fast-forwarded $MAIN_BRANCH to $GITHUB_REMOTE/$MAIN_BRANCH"

  if [[ -n "$wip_branch" ]]; then
    log "Merging WIP branch '$wip_branch' into $MAIN_BRANCH"
    git merge --no-ff "$wip_branch" -m "Merge local WIP ($wip_branch) into $MAIN_BRANCH" || {
      NEEDS_MANUAL_RESOLVE+=("$PWD ($wip_branch merge failed)")
      return 1
    }
    log "Merged WIP into $MAIN_BRANCH cleanly"
    git branch -d "$wip_branch"
    log "Deleted WIP branch '$wip_branch'"
  fi
}

sync_repo() {
  local repo=$1 commit_msg=$2
  log "=== Sync start: $repo ==="
  cd "$repo" || return 1

  validate_remote "$repo" || {
    SUMMARY_FAIL+=("$repo (remote issue)")
    return 1
  }

  if ! git diff --quiet || ! git diff --cached --quiet; then
    git add .
    git commit -m "$commit_msg" || true
    log "Committed local uncommitted changes on $MAIN_BRANCH"
  fi

  ensure_gitignore_and_unstage_sensitive
  prepare_and_pull_main || {
    SUMMARY_FAIL+=("$repo (merge issue)")
    return 1
  }

  ensure_gitignore_and_unstage_sensitive
  clean_empty_dirs
  retry_cmd git push "$GITHUB_REMOTE" "$MAIN_BRANCH" || {
    SUMMARY_FAIL+=("$repo (push failed)")
    return 1
  }

  SUMMARY_OK+=("$repo")
  log "Sync succeeded for $repo"
}

main() {
  mkdir -p "$LOG_DIR"
  RUN_TS=$(date +%Y%m%d-%H%M%S)
  RUN_LOG="$LOG_DIR/sync-git-auto-$RUN_TS.log"
  LATEST_LOG="$LOG_DIR/sync-git-auto-latest.log"
  touch "$RUN_LOG"
  ln -sf "$RUN_LOG" "$LATEST_LOG"

  acquire_lock
  local cmd=$1; shift
  mapfile -t repos < <(get_all_repos)

  [[ ${#repos[@]} -eq 0 ]] && echo "No Git repos found." && exit 1

  local commit_msg=${1:-"Auto-sync"}
  log "=== RUN $cmd; commit message: '$commit_msg' ==="

  for repo in "${repos[@]}"; do
    if ! sync_repo "$repo" "$commit_msg"; then
      log "Sync issues in $repo"
    fi
  done

  log "=== Summary ==="
  if (( ${#SUMMARY_OK[@]} > 0 )); then
    log "Succeeded in:"
    for r in "${SUMMARY_OK[@]}"; do log "  - $r"; done
  fi

  if (( ${#SUMMARY_FAIL[@]} > 0 )); then
    log "Failed or remote issues:"
    for r in "${SUMMARY_FAIL[@]}"; do log "  - $r"; done
  fi

  if (( ${#NEEDS_MANUAL_RESOLVE[@]} > 0 )); then
    log "Needs manual conflict resolution:"
    for r in "${NEEDS_MANUAL_RESOLVE[@]}"; do log "  - $r"; done
  fi
}

main "$@"

#!/usr/bin/env bash

# === CONFIG ===
REPOS=(
  "../QEP-MVP"
  "../Quran-recitation-mvp"
  "../Quran-recitation-platform"
)
ACTION=$1
COMMIT_MSG=$2
TIMESTAMP=$(date "+%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S")
WIP_BRANCH="sync-wip-$(date "+%Y%m%d-%H%M%S")"
MAX_RETRIES=4
LOG_PREFIX="[$(date '+%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S')]"

log() {
  echo "[$(date '+%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S')] $1"
}

retry_push() {
  local attempt=1
  local delay=5
  while [[ $attempt -le $MAX_RETRIES ]]; do
    log "Attempt $attempt: pushing to remote..."
    if git push origin main; then
      log "Push successful"
      return 0
    else
      log "Push failed - attempt $attempt"
      sleep $delay
      delay=$((delay * 2))  # exponential backoff
    fi
    ((attempt++))
  done
  log "ERROR: All push attempts failed."
  return 1
}

safe_git_pull() {
  if ! git pull --rebase --autostash; then
    log "WARNING: Pull failed - trying fallback"
    git pull --allow-unrelated-histories || {
      log "ERROR: Pull failed due to unrelated histories or merge conflict."
      return 1
    }
  fi
  return 0
}

handle_repo() {
  local repo_path="$1"
  log "=== Sync start: $repo_path ==="
  cd "$repo_path" || { log "ERROR: Cannot access $repo_path"; return 1; }

  if ! git rev-parse --is-inside-work-tree > /dev/null 2>&1; then
    log "ERROR: Not a valid Git repository: $repo_path"
    return 1
  fi

  local remote_url
  remote_url=$(git remote get-url origin 2>/dev/null)
  if [[ -z "$remote_url" ]]; then
    log "ERROR: Remote 'origin' not set in $repo_path"
    return 1
  fi

  git checkout main || git checkout -b main
  git status --porcelain | grep . && {
    log "Detected uncommitted changes - creating WIP branch"
    git add .
    git commit -m "${COMMIT_MSG:-WIP auto commit}"
    git branch "$WIP_BRANCH"
  }

  safe_git_pull || return 1

  if git show-ref --verify --quiet "refs/heads/$WIP_BRANCH"; then
    log "Merging $WIP_BRANCH into main..."
    git merge "$WIP_BRANCH" --no-edit || return 1
    git branch -d "$WIP_BRANCH"
  fi

  git clean -fdq
  log "Pushing changes to remote..."
  retry_push || return 1

  log "Sync succeeded for $repo_path"
  return 0
}

log "=== RUN $ACTION; commit message: '${COMMIT_MSG}' ==="

SUCCESS_REPOS=()
FAIL_REPOS=()

for repo in "${REPOS[@]}"; do
  if handle_repo "$repo"; then
    SUCCESS_REPOS+=("$repo")
  else
    FAIL_REPOS+=("$repo")
  fi
done

log "=== Summary ==="
log "Succeeded in:"
for r in "${SUCCESS_REPOS[@]}"; do
  log "  - $r"
done

if [[ ${#FAIL_REPOS[@]} -gt 0 ]]; then
  log "Failed or had issues:"
  for r in "${FAIL_REPOS[@]}"; do
    log "  - $r"
  done
fi

#!/usr/bin/env bash

# sync-git-auto.sh
# Consolidated, comprehensive Git synchronization script

set -euo pipefail

### === CONFIGURATION === ###
REPOS=(
  "$HOME/OneDrive/Desktop/github_repos/QEP-MVP"
  "$HOME/OneDrive/Desktop/github_repos/Quran-recitation-mvp"
  "$HOME/OneDrive/Desktop/github_repos/Quran-recitation-platform"
)

DEFAULT_BRANCH="main"
LOG_FILE="sync.log"
RETRY_LIMIT=4
RETRY_DELAYS=(5 10 20 40)

# === CONFIG ===
REPOS=(
  "../QEP-MVP"
  "../Quran-recitation-mvp"
  "../Quran-recitation-platform"
)
ACTION=$1
COMMIT_MSG=$2
TIMESTAMP=$(date "+%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S")
WIP_BRANCH="sync-wip-$(date "+%Y%m%d-%H%M%S")"
MAX_RETRIES=4
LOG_FILE="sync.log"

log() {
  local msg="[$(date '+%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S')] $1"
  echo "$msg" | tee -a "$LOG_FILE"
}

retry_push() {
  local attempt=1
  local delay=5
  while [[ $attempt -le $MAX_RETRIES ]]; do
    log "Attempt $attempt: pushing to remote..."
    if git push origin main; then
      log "Push successful"
      return 0
    else
      log "Push failed - attempt $attempt"
      sleep $delay
      delay=$((delay * 2))
    fi
    ((attempt++))
  done
  log "ERROR: All push attempts failed."
  return 1
}

safe_git_pull() {
  if ! git pull --rebase --autostash; then
    log "WARNING: Pull with rebase failed - trying merge fallback"
    git pull --allow-unrelated-histories || {
      log "ERROR: Pull failed due to unrelated histories or conflict"
      return 1
    }
  fi
  return 0
}

handle_repo() {
  local repo_path="$1"
  log "=== Sync start: $repo_path ==="
  cd "$repo_path" || { log "ERROR: Cannot access $repo_path"; return 1; }

  if ! git rev-parse --is-inside-work-tree > /dev/null 2>&1; then
    log "ERROR: Not a git repo: $repo_path"
    return 1
  fi

  local remote_url
  remote_url=$(git remote get-url origin 2>/dev/null)
  if [[ -z "$remote_url" ]]; then
    log "ERROR: Remote 'origin' not configured"
    return 1
  fi

  git checkout main || git checkout -b main
  git fetch origin

  if [[ -n $(git status --porcelain) ]]; then
    log "Detected local changes - committing and creating WIP branch"
    git add .
    git commit -m "${COMMIT_MSG:-Auto commit on sync}" || log "No changes staged"
    git branch "$WIP_BRANCH"
  fi

  safe_git_pull || return 1

  if git show-ref --verify --quiet "refs/heads/$WIP_BRANCH"; then
    log "Merging WIP branch into main"
    git merge "$WIP_BRANCH" --no-edit || return 1
    git branch -d "$WIP_BRANCH"
  fi

  git clean -fdq
  retry_push || return 1

  log "Sync succeeded: $repo_path"
  return 0
}

log "=== RUN $ACTION; Commit message: '${COMMIT_MSG}' ==="

SUCCESS_REPOS=()
FAIL_REPOS=()

for repo in "${REPOS[@]}"; do
  if handle_repo "$repo"; then
    SUCCESS_REPOS+=("$repo")
  else
    FAIL_REPOS+=("$repo")
  fi
  echo "" >> "$LOG_FILE"
done

log "=== Sync Summary ==="
log "Succeeded:"
for r in "${SUCCESS_REPOS[@]}"; do
  log "  - $r"
  done

if [[ ${#FAIL_REPOS[@]} -gt 0 ]]; then
  log "Failed/Issues:"
  for r in "${FAIL_REPOS[@]}"; do
    log "  - $r"
  done

# sync-git-auto.sh
# Consolidated, comprehensive Git synchronization script

set -euo pipefail

### === CONFIGURATION === ###
REPOS=(
  "$HOME/OneDrive/Desktop/github_repos/QEP-MVP"
  "$HOME/OneDrive/Desktop/github_repos/Quran-recitation-mvp"
  "$HOME/OneDrive/Desktop/github_repos/Quran-recitation-platform"
)

DEFAULT_BRANCH="main"
LOG_FILE="sync.log"
RETRY_LIMIT=4
RETRY_DELAYS=(5 10 20 40)


### === FUNCTIONS === ###

log() {
  local message="[$(date '+%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S')] $1"
  echo -e "$message" | tee -a "$LOG_FILE"
}

clean_empty_dirs() {
  find . -type d -empty -delete 2>/dev/null || true
}

check_git_repo() {
  if [ ! -d .git ]; then
    log "ERROR: Not a Git repository: $PWD"
    return 1
  fi
  if ! git remote get-url origin &>/dev/null; then
    log "ERROR: Remote 'origin' not set in $PWD"
    return 1
  fi
}

commit_local_changes() {
  if [ -n "$(git status --porcelain)" ]; then
    git add -A
    git commit -m "$1"
    log "Committed local uncommitted changes on $(git rev-parse --abbrev-ref HEAD)"
  fi
}

create_wip_branch() {
  local wip_branch="sync-wip-$(date '+%Y%m%d-%H%M%S')"
  git checkout -b "$wip_branch"
  log "Created WIP branch '$wip_branch' to save local work"
  echo "$wip_branch"
}

safe_checkout_main() {
  if [[ "$(git rev-parse --abbrev-ref HEAD)" != "$DEFAULT_BRANCH" ]]; then
    git checkout "$DEFAULT_BRANCH"
  fi
}

fast_forward_pull() {
  git fetch origin "$DEFAULT_BRANCH"
  if ! git merge --ff-only "origin/$DEFAULT_BRANCH"; then
    log "Non-fast-forward detected. Attempting merge."
    git merge "origin/$DEFAULT_BRANCH" || {
      log "Merge conflict occurred. Manual intervention may be required."
      return 1
    }
  fi
  log "Fast-forwarded $DEFAULT_BRANCH to origin/$DEFAULT_BRANCH"
}

attempt_push_with_retry() {
  local try=0
  until git push origin "$DEFAULT_BRANCH"; do
    if [ $try -ge $RETRY_LIMIT ]; then
      log "Final push attempt failed after $RETRY_LIMIT retries."
      return 1
    fi
    local delay=${RETRY_DELAYS[$try]}
    log "Push failed (non-fast-forward). Retrying in $delay seconds..."
    sleep "$delay"
    ((try++))
    git pull --rebase --autostash || git pull --no-rebase
  done
  log "Push succeeded after retry #$try"
}

sync_repo() {
  local repo_path="$1"
  local commit_message="$2"

  log "=== Sync start: $repo_path ==="
  cd "$repo_path" || { log "ERROR: Could not cd into $repo_path"; return 1; }

  if ! check_git_repo; then
    return 1
  fi

  safe_checkout_main
  commit_local_changes "$commit_message"

  local wip_branch="$(create_wip_branch)"
  safe_checkout_main
  fast_forward_pull || return 1

  log "Merging WIP branch '$wip_branch' into $DEFAULT_BRANCH"
  git merge "$wip_branch" || { log "Merge conflict from WIP. Manual resolution required."; return 1; }
  git branch -D "$wip_branch"
  log "Deleted WIP branch '$wip_branch'"

  clean_empty_dirs
  attempt_push_with_retry || return 1
  log "Sync succeeded for $repo_path"
}


### === MAIN === ###

ACTION=${1:-sync}
COMMIT_MSG=${2:-"Auto sync commit"}
log "=== RUN $ACTION; commit message: '$COMMIT_MSG' ==="

SUCCESSFUL=()
FAILED=()

for repo in "${REPOS[@]}"; do
  if sync_repo "$repo" "$COMMIT_MSG"; then
    SUCCESSFUL+=("$repo")
  else
    FAILED+=("$repo")
  fi
done

log "=== Summary ==="
if [ ${#SUCCESSFUL[@]} -gt 0 ]; then
  log "Succeeded in:"
  for path in "${SUCCESSFUL[@]}"; do
    log "  - $path"
  done
fi

if [ ${#FAILED[@]} -gt 0 ]; then
  log "Failed or had issues:"
  for path in "${FAILED[@]}"; do
    log "  - $path"
  done
fi

run_cmd() {
  local attempt=1
  local cmd="$*"
  until $cmd; do
    if (( attempt >= MAX_RETRIES )); then
      log "ERROR: Command failed after $attempt attempts: $cmd"
      return 1
    fi
    local wait_sec=$(( RETRY_WAIT_INITIAL * attempt ))
    log "WARN: Command failed (attempt $attempt): $cmd"
    log "Retrying in $wait_sec seconds..."
    sleep $wait_sec
    (( attempt++ ))
  done
  log "SUCCESS: Command succeeded: $cmd"
  return 0
}

check_node_pnpm_versions() {
  local required_node_version="18.0.0"
  local required_pnpm_version="7.0.0"

  local node_version
  node_version=$(node -v 2>/dev/null || echo "none")
  local pnpm_version
  pnpm_version=$(pnpm -v 2>/dev/null || echo "none")

  log "Detected Node.js version: $node_version"
  log "Detected pnpm version: $pnpm_version"

  if [[ "$node_version" == "none" ]]; then
    log "ERROR: Node.js is not installed or not in PATH."
    exit 1
  fi

  if [[ "$pnpm_version" == "none" ]]; then
    log "ERROR: pnpm is not installed or not in PATH."
    exit 1
  fi

  # Simple version check (major only)
  local node_major=${node_version#v}
  node_major=${node_major%%.*}

  local req_node_major=${required_node_version%%.*}

  if (( node_major < req_node_major )); then
    log "ERROR: Node.js version $required_node_version or higher required."
    exit 1
  fi

  local pnpm_major=${pnpm_version%%.*}
  local req_pnpm_major=${required_pnpm_version%%.*}

  if (( pnpm_major < req_pnpm_major )); then
    log "ERROR: pnpm version $required_pnpm_version or higher required."
    exit 1
  fi
}

clean_caches() {
  log "Cleaning node_modules and pnpm caches..."
  rm -rf frontend/node_modules backend/node_modules shared/node_modules
  pnpm store prune
  pnpm cache clean --all
}

build_all() {
  log "Starting build process for all projects..."

  run_cmd pnpm --filter frontend build || { log "Frontend build failed."; return 1; }
  run_cmd pnpm --filter backend build || { log "Backend build failed."; return 1; }

  log "Build process completed successfully."
}

  log "Starting development environment containers..."
  run_cmd docker-compose -f ./infra/docker/docker-compose-dev.yml up -d || { log "Failed to start dev environment"; return 1; }
}

  load_env_file
  check_node_pnpm_versions
  clean_caches
  build_all
  docker_up
  log "=== Script completed successfully ==="

#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail
IFS=$'\n\t'

# === CONFIGURATION ===
LOGFILE="setup.log"
ENV_PATH=".env"
MAX_RETRIES=5
RETRY_WAIT_INITIAL=3  # seconds, exponential backoff multiplier
REQUIRED_NODE_VERSION="18.0.0"
REQUIRED_PNPM_VERSION="7.0.0"

# === UTILITIES ===
timestamp() {
  date "+%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S"
}

log() {
  local msg="$*"
  echo -e "$(timestamp) $msg" | tee -a "$LOGFILE"
}

# Retry a command with exponential backoff
run_cmd() {
  local attempt=1
  local delay=$RETRY_WAIT_INITIAL
  local cmd="$*"
  until $cmd; do
    if (( attempt >= MAX_RETRIES )); then
      log "❌ ERROR: Command failed after $attempt attempts: $cmd"
      return 1
    fi
    log "⚠️ WARN: Command failed (attempt $attempt): $cmd"
    log "Retrying in $delay seconds..."
    sleep "$delay"
    delay=$(( delay * 2 ))
    ((attempt++))
  done
  log "✅ SUCCESS: Command succeeded: $cmd"
  return 0
}

# Load environment variables safely, export GOOGLE_APPLICATION_CREDENTIALS if set
load_env_file() {
  if [[ -f "$ENV_PATH" ]]; then
    log "📦 Loading environment variables from $ENV_PATH"
    set -a
    # shellcheck source=/dev/null
    source "$ENV_PATH"
    set +a
    if [[ -n "${GOOGLE_APPLICATION_CREDENTIALS:-}" ]]; then
      export GOOGLE_APPLICATION_CREDENTIALS
      log "🔐 Exported GOOGLE_APPLICATION_CREDENTIALS=$GOOGLE_APPLICATION_CREDENTIALS"
    fi
  else
    log "⚠️ WARNING: $ENV_PATH not found; skipping environment loading"
  fi
}

# Compare semantic versions (only major.minor.patch, simple numeric)
version_ge() {
  # returns 0 if $1 >= $2, else 1
  # usage: version_ge "18.2.0" "18.0.0"
  local IFS=.
  local i ver1=($1) ver2=($2)
  # fill empty fields with zeros
  for ((i=${#ver1[@]}; i<3; i++)); do ver1[i]=0; done
  for ((i=${#ver2[@]}; i<3; i++)); do ver2[i]=0; done
  for ((i=0; i<3; i++)); do
    if ((10#${ver1[i]} > 10#${ver2[i]})); then
      return 0
    elif ((10#${ver1[i]} < 10#${ver2[i]})); then
      return 1
    fi
  done
  return 0
}

# Check Node.js and pnpm versions with detailed semantic comparison
check_versions() {
  local node_version node_version_clean pnpm_version

  node_version=$(node -v 2>/dev/null || echo "none")
  pnpm_version=$(pnpm -v 2>/dev/null || echo "none")

  log "🧪 Detected Node.js version: $node_version"
  log "🧪 Detected pnpm version: $pnpm_version"

  if [[ "$node_version" == "none" ]]; then
    log "❌ ERROR: Node.js is not installed or not in PATH."
    exit 1
  fi

  if [[ "$pnpm_version" == "none" ]]; then
    log "❌ ERROR: pnpm is not installed or not in PATH."
    exit 1
  fi

  node_version_clean="${node_version#v}"
  if ! version_ge "$node_version_clean" "$REQUIRED_NODE_VERSION"; then
    log "❌ ERROR: Node.js version $REQUIRED_NODE_VERSION or higher required."
    exit 1
  fi

  if ! version_ge "$pnpm_version" "$REQUIRED_PNPM_VERSION"; then
    log "❌ ERROR: pnpm version $REQUIRED_PNPM_VERSION or higher required."
    exit 1
  fi

  log "✅ Node.js and pnpm version requirements satisfied."
}

# Clean caches and node_modules with error-tolerant approach
clean_caches() {
  log "🧹 Cleaning node_modules and pnpm caches..."
  local dirs=(frontend/node_modules backend/node_modules shared/node_modules)
  for d in "${dirs[@]}"; do
    if [[ -d "$d" ]]; then
      rm -rf "$d" && log "🗑️ Removed $d"
    else
      log "ℹ️ Directory $d does not exist, skipping"
    fi
  done
  run_cmd pnpm store prune || log "⚠️ pnpm store prune failed, continuing"
  run_cmd pnpm cache clean --all || log "⚠️ pnpm cache clean failed, continuing"
  log "✅ Cache cleanup complete."
}

# Build frontend, backend, shared packages with retries
build_all() {
  log "🏗️ Starting build process for all projects..."
  run_cmd pnpm --filter frontend build || { log "❌ Frontend build failed."; return 1; }
  run_cmd pnpm --filter backend build || { log "❌ Backend build failed."; return 1; }
  run_cmd pnpm --filter shared build || { log "❌ Shared build failed."; return 1; }
  log "✅ Build process completed successfully."
}

# Docker-compose startup with retries for both databases and dev environment
docker_up() {
  log "🐳 Starting Docker containers..."
  run_cmd docker-compose -f ./infra/docker/docker-compose-databases.yml up -d || { log "❌ Failed to start databases"; return 1; }
  run_cmd docker-compose -f ./infra/docker/docker-compose-dev.yml up -d || { log "❌ Failed to start dev environment"; return 1; }
  log "✅ Docker containers started successfully."
}

# Main execution sequence with error handling and summary logging
main() {
  log "🚀 === Setup Script Started ==="
  local start_time=$(date +%s)

  load_env_file
  check_versions
  clean_caches
  build_all
  docker_up

  local end_time=$(date +%s)

  date "+%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S"
}

log() {
  local msg="$*"
  echo "$(timestamp) $msg"
  echo "$(timestamp) $msg" >> "$LOGFILE"
}

load_env_file() {
  if [ -f "$ENV_PATH" ]; then
    log "Loading environment variables from $ENV_PATH"
    set -a
    source "$ENV_PATH"
    set +a
    if [[ -n "${GOOGLE_APPLICATION_CREDENTIALS:-}" ]]; then
      export GOOGLE_APPLICATION_CREDENTIALS
      log "Exported GOOGLE_APPLICATION_CREDENTIALS=$GOOGLE_APPLICATION_CREDENTIALS"
    fi
  else
    log "WARNING: $ENV_PATH not found. Skipping environment loading."
  fi
}

run_cmd() {
  local attempt=1
  local cmd="$*"
  until $cmd; do
    if (( attempt >= MAX_RETRIES )); then
      log "ERROR: Command failed after $attempt attempts: $cmd"
      return 1
    fi
    local wait_sec=$(( RETRY_WAIT_INITIAL * attempt ))
    log "WARN: Command failed (attempt $attempt): $cmd"
    log "Retrying in $wait_sec seconds..."
    sleep $wait_sec
    (( attempt++ ))
  done
  log "SUCCESS: Command succeeded: $cmd"
  return 0
}

check_node_pnpm_versions() {
  local required_node_version="18.0.0"
  local required_pnpm_version="7.0.0"

  local node_version
  node_version=$(node -v 2>/dev/null || echo "none")
  local pnpm_version
  pnpm_version=$(pnpm -v 2>/dev/null || echo "none")

  log "Detected Node.js version: $node_version"
  log "Detected pnpm version: $pnpm_version"

  if [[ "$node_version" == "none" ]]; then
    log "ERROR: Node.js is not installed or not in PATH."
    exit 1
  fi

  if [[ "$pnpm_version" == "none" ]]; then
    log "ERROR: pnpm is not installed or not in PATH."
    exit 1
  fi

  # Simple version check (major only)
  local node_major=${node_version#v}
  node_major=${node_major%%.*}

  local req_node_major=${required_node_version%%.*}

  if (( node_major < req_node_major )); then
    log "ERROR: Node.js version $required_node_version or higher required."
    exit 1
  fi

  local pnpm_major=${pnpm_version%%.*}
  local req_pnpm_major=${required_pnpm_version%%.*}

  if (( pnpm_major < req_pnpm_major )); then
    log "ERROR: pnpm version $required_pnpm_version or higher required."
    exit 1
  fi
}

clean_caches() {
  log "Cleaning node_modules and pnpm caches..."
  rm -rf frontend/node_modules backend/node_modules shared/node_modules
  pnpm store prune
  pnpm cache clean --all
}

  log "Starting build process for all projects..."

  run_cmd pnpm --filter frontend build || { log "Frontend build failed."; return 1; }
  run_cmd pnpm --filter backend build || { log "Backend build failed."; return 1; }
  run_cmd pnpm --filter shared build || { log "Shared build failed."; return 1; }

  log "Build process completed successfully."
}

  log "Starting database containers..."
  run_cmd docker-compose -f ./infra/docker/docker-compose-databases.yml up -d || { log "Failed to start databases"; return 1; }

  log "Starting development environment containers..."
  run_cmd docker-compose -f ./infra/docker/docker-compose-dev.yml up -d || { log "Failed to start dev environment"; return 1; }
}

  load_env_file
  check_node_pnpm_versions
  clean_caches
  build_all
  docker_up
  log "=== Script completed successfully ==="
}

#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail
IFS=$'\n\t'

# === CONFIGURATION ===
LOGFILE="setup.log"
ENV_PATH=".env"
MAX_RETRIES=5
RETRY_WAIT_INITIAL=3  # seconds, exponential backoff multiplier
REQUIRED_NODE_VERSION="18.0.0"
REQUIRED_PNPM_VERSION="7.0.0"

# === UTILITIES ===
timestamp() {
  date "+%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S"
}

log() {
  local msg="$*"
  echo -e "$(timestamp) $msg" | tee -a "$LOGFILE"
}

# Retry a command with exponential backoff
run_cmd() {
  local attempt=1
  local delay=$RETRY_WAIT_INITIAL
  local cmd="$*"
  until $cmd; do
    if (( attempt >= MAX_RETRIES )); then
      log "❌ ERROR: Command failed after $attempt attempts: $cmd"
      return 1
    fi
    log "⚠️ WARN: Command failed (attempt $attempt): $cmd"
    log "Retrying in $delay seconds..."
    sleep "$delay"
    delay=$(( delay * 2 ))
    ((attempt++))
  done
  log "✅ SUCCESS: Command succeeded: $cmd"
  return 0
}

# Load environment variables safely, export GOOGLE_APPLICATION_CREDENTIALS if set
load_env_file() {
  if [[ -f "$ENV_PATH" ]]; then
    log "📦 Loading environment variables from $ENV_PATH"
    set -a
    # shellcheck source=/dev/null
    source "$ENV_PATH"
    set +a
    if [[ -n "${GOOGLE_APPLICATION_CREDENTIALS:-}" ]]; then
      export GOOGLE_APPLICATION_CREDENTIALS
      log "🔐 Exported GOOGLE_APPLICATION_CREDENTIALS=$GOOGLE_APPLICATION_CREDENTIALS"
    fi
  else
    log "⚠️ WARNING: $ENV_PATH not found; skipping environment loading"
  fi
}

# Compare semantic versions (only major.minor.patch, simple numeric)
version_ge() {
  # returns 0 if $1 >= $2, else 1
  # usage: version_ge "18.2.0" "18.0.0"
  local IFS=.
  local i ver1=($1) ver2=($2)
  # fill empty fields with zeros
  for ((i=${#ver1[@]}; i<3; i++)); do ver1[i]=0; done
  for ((i=${#ver2[@]}; i<3; i++)); do ver2[i]=0; done
  for ((i=0; i<3; i++)); do
    if ((10#${ver1[i]} > 10#${ver2[i]})); then
      return 0
    elif ((10#${ver1[i]} < 10#${ver2[i]})); then
      return 1
    fi
  done
  return 0
}

# Check Node.js and pnpm versions with detailed semantic comparison
check_versions() {
  local node_version node_version_clean pnpm_version

  node_version=$(node -v 2>/dev/null || echo "none")
  pnpm_version=$(pnpm -v 2>/dev/null || echo "none")

  log "🧪 Detected Node.js version: $node_version"
  log "🧪 Detected pnpm version: $pnpm_version"

  if [[ "$node_version" == "none" ]]; then
    log "❌ ERROR: Node.js is not installed or not in PATH."
    exit 1
  fi

  if [[ "$pnpm_version" == "none" ]]; then
    log "❌ ERROR: pnpm is not installed or not in PATH."
    exit 1
  fi

  node_version_clean="${node_version#v}"
  if ! version_ge "$node_version_clean" "$REQUIRED_NODE_VERSION"; then
    log "❌ ERROR: Node.js version $REQUIRED_NODE_VERSION or higher required."
    exit 1
  fi

  if ! version_ge "$pnpm_version" "$REQUIRED_PNPM_VERSION"; then
    log "❌ ERROR: pnpm version $REQUIRED_PNPM_VERSION or higher required."
    exit 1
  fi

  log "✅ Node.js and pnpm version requirements satisfied."
}

# Clean caches and node_modules with error-tolerant approach
clean_caches() {
  log "🧹 Cleaning node_modules and pnpm caches..."
  local dirs=(frontend/node_modules backend/node_modules shared/node_modules)
  for d in "${dirs[@]}"; do
    if [[ -d "$d" ]]; then
      rm -rf "$d" && log "🗑️ Removed $d"
    else
      log "ℹ️ Directory $d does not exist, skipping"
    fi
  done
  run_cmd pnpm store prune || log "⚠️ pnpm store prune failed, continuing"
  run_cmd pnpm cache clean --all || log "⚠️ pnpm cache clean failed, continuing"
  log "✅ Cache cleanup complete."
}

# Build frontend, backend, shared packages with retries
build_all() {
  log "🏗️ Starting build process for all projects..."
  run_cmd pnpm --filter frontend build || { log "❌ Frontend build failed."; return 1; }
  run_cmd pnpm --filter backend build || { log "❌ Backend build failed."; return 1; }
  run_cmd pnpm --filter shared build || { log "❌ Shared build failed."; return 1; }
  log "✅ Build process completed successfully."
}

# Docker-compose startup with retries for both databases and dev environment
docker_up() {
  log "🐳 Starting Docker containers..."
  run_cmd docker-compose -f ./infra/docker/docker-compose-databases.yml up -d || { log "❌ Failed to start databases"; return 1; }
  run_cmd docker-compose -f ./infra/docker/docker-compose-dev.yml up -d || { log "❌ Failed to start dev environment"; return 1; }
  log "✅ Docker containers started successfully."
}

# Main execution sequence with error handling and summary logging
main() {
  log "🚀 === Setup Script Started ==="
  local start_time=$(date +%s)

  load_env_file
  check_versions
  clean_caches
  build_all
  docker_up

  local end_time=$(date +%s)
  local elapsed=$(( end_time - start_time ))

  log "🎉 === Setup Completed Successfully in ${elapsed}s ==="
}

main "$@"

  run_cmd pnpm --filter backend build || { log "Backend build failed."; return 1; }

  log "Build process completed successfully."

  log "Starting development environment containers..."

  run_cmd docker-compose -f ./infra/docker/docker-compose-dev.yml up -d || { log "Failed to start dev environment"; return 1; }

#!/usr/bin/env bash

set -euo pipefail

IFS=$'\n\t'



# === CONFIGURATION ===

LOGFILE="setup.log"

ENV_PATH=".env"

MAX_RETRIES=5

RETRY_WAIT_INITIAL=3  # seconds

REQUIRED_NODE_VERSION="18.0.0"

REQUIRED_PNPM_VERSION="7.0.0"



# === LOGGING ===

timestamp() {

  date "+%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S"

}



log() {

  local msg="$*"

  echo -e "$(timestamp) $msg" | tee -a "$LOGFILE"

}



# === RETRY WRAPPER ===

run_cmd() {

  local attempt=1

  local delay=$RETRY_WAIT_INITIAL

  local cmd="$*"

  until $cmd; do

    if (( attempt >= MAX_RETRIES )); then

      log "❌ ERROR: '$cmd' failed after $attempt attempts"

      return 1

    fi

    log "⚠️ WARN: Command failed (attempt $attempt): $cmd"

    log "Retrying in $delay seconds..."

    sleep "$delay"

    delay=$(( delay * 2 ))

    ((attempt++))

  done

  log "✅ SUCCESS: Command succeeded: $cmd"

  return 0

}



# === ENVIRONMENT SETUP ===

load_env_file() {

  if [ -f "$ENV_PATH" ]; then

    log "📦 Loading environment from $ENV_PATH"

    set -a

    source "$ENV_PATH"

    set +a

    if [[ -n "${GOOGLE_APPLICATION_CREDENTIALS:-}" ]]; then

      export GOOGLE_APPLICATION_CREDENTIALS

      log "🔐 Exported GOOGLE_APPLICATION_CREDENTIALS"

    fi

  else

    log "⚠️ WARNING: $ENV_PATH not found. Skipping."

  fi

}



# === VERSION CHECKS ===

check_versions() {

  local node_version=$(node -v 2>/dev/null || echo "none")

  local pnpm_version=$(pnpm -v 2>/dev/null || echo "none")



  log "🧪 Node.js version: $node_version"

  log "🧪 PNPM version: $pnpm_version"



  if [[ "$node_version" == "none" ]]; then

    log "❌ ERROR: Node.js is not installed."

    exit 1

  fi



  if [[ "$pnpm_version" == "none" ]]; then

    log "❌ ERROR: pnpm is not installed."

    exit 1

  fi



  # Compare major versions

  local node_major=${node_version#v}

  node_major=${node_major%%.*}

  local pnpm_major=${pnpm_version%%.*}



  if (( node_major < ${REQUIRED_NODE_VERSION%%.*} )); then

    log "❌ ERROR: Node.js $REQUIRED_NODE_VERSION or newer required."

    exit 1

  fi



  if (( pnpm_major < ${REQUIRED_PNPM_VERSION%%.*} )); then

    log "❌ ERROR: pnpm $REQUIRED_PNPM_VERSION or newer required."

    exit 1

  fi

}



# === CLEANUP ===

clean_caches() {

  log "🧹 Cleaning node_modules and pnpm caches..."

  rm -rf frontend/node_modules backend/node_modules shared/node_modules

  pnpm store prune || true

  pnpm cache clean --all || true

  log "✅ Cache cleanup complete."

}

}

#!/usr/bin/env bash

set -euo pipefail

IFS=$'\n\t'



# === CONFIGURATION ===

LOGFILE="setup.log"

ENV_PATH=".env"

MAX_RETRIES=5

RETRY_WAIT_INITIAL=3  # seconds, exponential backoff multiplier

REQUIRED_NODE_VERSION="18.0.0"

REQUIRED_PNPM_VERSION="7.0.0"



# === UTILITIES ===

timestamp() {

  date "+%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S"

}



log() {

  local msg="$*"

  echo -e "$(timestamp) $msg" | tee -a "$LOGFILE"

}



# Retry a command with exponential backoff

run_cmd() {

  local attempt=1

  local delay=$RETRY_WAIT_INITIAL

  local cmd="$*"

  until $cmd; do

    if (( attempt >= MAX_RETRIES )); then

      log "❌ ERROR: Command failed after $attempt attempts: $cmd"

      return 1

    fi

    log "⚠️ WARN: Command failed (attempt $attempt): $cmd"

    log "Retrying in $delay seconds..."

    sleep "$delay"

    delay=$(( delay * 2 ))

    ((attempt++))

  done

  log "✅ SUCCESS: Command succeeded: $cmd"

  return 0

}



# Load environment variables safely, export GOOGLE_APPLICATION_CREDENTIALS if set

load_env_file() {

  if [[ -f "$ENV_PATH" ]]; then

    log "📦 Loading environment variables from $ENV_PATH"

    set -a

    # shellcheck source=/dev/null

    source "$ENV_PATH"

    set +a

    if [[ -n "${GOOGLE_APPLICATION_CREDENTIALS:-}" ]]; then

      export GOOGLE_APPLICATION_CREDENTIALS

      log "🔐 Exported GOOGLE_APPLICATION_CREDENTIALS=$GOOGLE_APPLICATION_CREDENTIALS"

    fi

  else

    log "⚠️ WARNING: $ENV_PATH not found; skipping environment loading"

  fi

}



# Compare semantic versions (only major.minor.patch, simple numeric)

version_ge() {

  # returns 0 if $1 >= $2, else 1

  # usage: version_ge "18.2.0" "18.0.0"

  local IFS=.

  local i ver1=($1) ver2=($2)

  # fill empty fields with zeros

  for ((i=${#ver1[@]}; i<3; i++)); do ver1[i]=0; done

  for ((i=${#ver2[@]}; i<3; i++)); do ver2[i]=0; done

  for ((i=0; i<3; i++)); do

    if ((10#${ver1[i]} > 10#${ver2[i]})); then

      return 0

    elif ((10#${ver1[i]} < 10#${ver2[i]})); then

      return 1

    fi

  done

  return 0

}



# Check Node.js and pnpm versions with detailed semantic comparison

check_versions() {

  local node_version node_version_clean pnpm_version



  node_version=$(node -v 2>/dev/null || echo "none")

  pnpm_version=$(pnpm -v 2>/dev/null || echo "none")



  log "🧪 Detected Node.js version: $node_version"

  log "🧪 Detected pnpm version: $pnpm_version"



  if [[ "$node_version" == "none" ]]; then

    log "❌ ERROR: Node.js is not installed or not in PATH."

    exit 1

  fi



  if [[ "$pnpm_version" == "none" ]]; then

    log "❌ ERROR: pnpm is not installed or not in PATH."

    exit 1

  fi



  node_version_clean="${node_version#v}"

  if ! version_ge "$node_version_clean" "$REQUIRED_NODE_VERSION"; then

    log "❌ ERROR: Node.js version $REQUIRED_NODE_VERSION or higher required."

    exit 1

  fi



  if ! version_ge "$pnpm_version" "$REQUIRED_PNPM_VERSION"; then

    log "❌ ERROR: pnpm version $REQUIRED_PNPM_VERSION or higher required."

    exit 1

  fi



  log "✅ Node.js and pnpm version requirements satisfied."

}



# Clean caches and node_modules with error-tolerant approach

clean_caches() {

  log "🧹 Cleaning node_modules and pnpm caches..."

  local dirs=(frontend/node_modules backend/node_modules shared/node_modules)

  for d in "${dirs[@]}"; do

    if [[ -d "$d" ]]; then

      rm -rf "$d" && log "🗑️ Removed $d"

    else

      log "ℹ️ Directory $d does not exist, skipping"

    fi

  done

  run_cmd pnpm store prune || log "⚠️ pnpm store prune failed, continuing"

  run_cmd pnpm cache clean --all || log "⚠️ pnpm cache clean failed, continuing"

  log "✅ Cache cleanup complete."

}



# Build frontend, backend, shared packages with retries

build_all() {

  log "🏗️ Starting build process for all projects..."

  run_cmd pnpm --filter frontend build || { log "❌ Frontend build failed."; return 1; }

  run_cmd pnpm --filter backend build || { log "❌ Backend build failed."; return 1; }

  run_cmd pnpm --filter shared build || { log "❌ Shared build failed."; return 1; }

  log "✅ Build process completed successfully."

}



# Docker-compose startup with retries for both databases and dev environment

docker_up() {

  log "🐳 Starting Docker containers..."

  run_cmd docker-compose -f ./infra/docker/docker-compose-databases.yml up -d || { log "❌ Failed to start databases"; return 1; }

  run_cmd docker-compose -f ./infra/docker/docker-compose-dev.yml up -d || { log "❌ Failed to start dev environment"; return 1; }

  log "✅ Docker containers started successfully."

}



# Main execution sequence with error handling and summary logging

main() {

  log "🚀 === Setup Script Started ==="

  local start_time=$(date +%s)



  load_env_file

  check_versions

  clean_caches

  build_all

  docker_up



  local end_time=$(date +%s)

  local elapsed=$(( end_time - start_time ))



  log "🎉 === Setup Completed Successfully in ${elapsed}s ==="

}



main "$@"

REQUIRED_PNPM_VERSION="7.0.0"

timestamp() {

log() {

  echo -e "$(timestamp) $msg" | tee -a "$LOGFILE"

# === RETRY WRAPPER ===



run_cmd() {



  local attempt=1



  local delay=$RETRY_WAIT_INITIAL

  until $cmd; do



    if (( attempt >= MAX_RETRIES )); then



      log "❌ ERROR: '$cmd' failed after $attempt attempts"

    log "Retrying in $delay seconds..."



    sleep "$delay"

    ((attempt++))



  done



  log "✅ SUCCESS: Command succeeded: $cmd"



  return 0



}







# === ENVIRONMENT SETUP ===



load_env_file() {



  if [ -f "$ENV_PATH" ]; then



    log "📦 Loading environment from $ENV_PATH"



    set -a



    source "$ENV_PATH"



    set +a



    if [[ -n "${GOOGLE_APPLICATION_CREDENTIALS:-}" ]]; then



      export GOOGLE_APPLICATION_CREDENTIALS



      log "🔐 Exported GOOGLE_APPLICATION_CREDENTIALS"



    fi



  else



    log "⚠️ WARNING: $ENV_PATH not found. Skipping."



  fi



}







# === VERSION CHECKS ===



check_versions() {



  local node_version=$(node -v 2>/dev/null || echo "none")



  local pnpm_version=$(pnpm -v 2>/dev/null || echo "none")







  log "🧪 Node.js version: $node_version"



  log "🧪 PNPM version: $pnpm_version"







  if [[ "$node_version" == "none" ]]; then



    log "❌ ERROR: Node.js is not installed."



    exit 1



  fi







  if [[ "$pnpm_version" == "none" ]]; then



    log "❌ ERROR: pnpm is not installed."



    exit 1



  fi







  # Compare major versions



  local node_major=${node_version#v}



  node_major=${node_major%%.*}



  local pnpm_major=${pnpm_version%%.*}







  if (( node_major < ${REQUIRED_NODE_VERSION%%.*} )); then



    log "❌ ERROR: Node.js $REQUIRED_NODE_VERSION or newer required."



    exit 1



  fi







  if (( pnpm_major < ${REQUIRED_PNPM_VERSION%%.*} )); then



    log "❌ ERROR: pnpm $REQUIRED_PNPM_VERSION or newer required."



    exit 1



  fi



}







# === CLEANUP ===



clean_caches() {



  log "🧹 Cleaning node_modules and pnpm caches..."



  rm -rf frontend/node_modules backend/node_modules shared/node_modules



  pnpm store prune || true



  pnpm cache clean --all || true



  log "✅ Cache cleanup complete."



}

  run_cmd pnpm --filter backend build || return 1



  run_cmd pnpm --filter shared build || return 1

  log "🐳 Starting Docker containers..."







  run_cmd docker-compose -f ./infra/docker/docker-compose-databases.yml up -d || return 1



  run_cmd docker-compose -f ./infra/docker/docker-compose-dev.yml up -d || return 1







  log "✅ Docker containers started successfully."



}

  log "🚀 === Setup Script Started ==="







  load_env_file



  check_versions



  clean_caches

  docker_up







  log "🎉 === Setup Completed Successfully ==="

#!/usr/bin/env bash



set -euo pipefail



IFS=$'\n\t'







# === CONFIGURATION ===



LOGFILE="setup.log"



ENV_PATH=".env"



MAX_RETRIES=5



RETRY_WAIT_INITIAL=3  # seconds, exponential backoff multiplier



REQUIRED_NODE_VERSION="18.0.0"



REQUIRED_PNPM_VERSION="7.0.0"







# === UTILITIES ===



timestamp() {



  date "+%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S"



}







log() {



  local msg="$*"



  echo -e "$(timestamp) $msg" | tee -a "$LOGFILE"



}







# Retry a command with exponential backoff



run_cmd() {



  local attempt=1



  local delay=$RETRY_WAIT_INITIAL



  local cmd="$*"



  until $cmd; do



    if (( attempt >= MAX_RETRIES )); then



      log "❌ ERROR: Command failed after $attempt attempts: $cmd"



      return 1



    fi



    log "⚠️ WARN: Command failed (attempt $attempt): $cmd"



    log "Retrying in $delay seconds..."



    sleep "$delay"



    delay=$(( delay * 2 ))



    ((attempt++))



  done



  log "✅ SUCCESS: Command succeeded: $cmd"



  return 0



}







# Load environment variables safely, export GOOGLE_APPLICATION_CREDENTIALS if set



load_env_file() {



  if [[ -f "$ENV_PATH" ]]; then



    log "📦 Loading environment variables from $ENV_PATH"



    set -a



    # shellcheck source=/dev/null



    source "$ENV_PATH"



    set +a



    if [[ -n "${GOOGLE_APPLICATION_CREDENTIALS:-}" ]]; then



      export GOOGLE_APPLICATION_CREDENTIALS



      log "🔐 Exported GOOGLE_APPLICATION_CREDENTIALS=$GOOGLE_APPLICATION_CREDENTIALS"



    fi



  else



    log "⚠️ WARNING: $ENV_PATH not found; skipping environment loading"



  fi



}







# Compare semantic versions (only major.minor.patch, simple numeric)



version_ge() {



  # returns 0 if $1 >= $2, else 1



  # usage: version_ge "18.2.0" "18.0.0"



  local IFS=.



  local i ver1=($1) ver2=($2)



  # fill empty fields with zeros



  for ((i=${#ver1[@]}; i<3; i++)); do ver1[i]=0; done



  for ((i=${#ver2[@]}; i<3; i++)); do ver2[i]=0; done



  for ((i=0; i<3; i++)); do



    if ((10#${ver1[i]} > 10#${ver2[i]})); then



      return 0



    elif ((10#${ver1[i]} < 10#${ver2[i]})); then



      return 1



    fi



  done



  return 0



}







# Check Node.js and pnpm versions with detailed semantic comparison



check_versions() {



  local node_version node_version_clean pnpm_version







  node_version=$(node -v 2>/dev/null || echo "none")



  pnpm_version=$(pnpm -v 2>/dev/null || echo "none")







  log "🧪 Detected Node.js version: $node_version"



  log "🧪 Detected pnpm version: $pnpm_version"







  if [[ "$node_version" == "none" ]]; then



    log "❌ ERROR: Node.js is not installed or not in PATH."



    exit 1



  fi







  if [[ "$pnpm_version" == "none" ]]; then



    log "❌ ERROR: pnpm is not installed or not in PATH."



    exit 1



  fi







  node_version_clean="${node_version#v}"



  if ! version_ge "$node_version_clean" "$REQUIRED_NODE_VERSION"; then



    log "❌ ERROR: Node.js version $REQUIRED_NODE_VERSION or higher required."



    exit 1



  fi







  if ! version_ge "$pnpm_version" "$REQUIRED_PNPM_VERSION"; then



    log "❌ ERROR: pnpm version $REQUIRED_PNPM_VERSION or higher required."



    exit 1



  fi







  log "✅ Node.js and pnpm version requirements satisfied."



}







# Clean caches and node_modules with error-tolerant approach



clean_caches() {



  log "🧹 Cleaning node_modules and pnpm caches..."



  local dirs=(frontend/node_modules backend/node_modules shared/node_modules)



  for d in "${dirs[@]}"; do



    if [[ -d "$d" ]]; then



      rm -rf "$d" && log "🗑️ Removed $d"



    else



      log "ℹ️ Directory $d does not exist, skipping"



    fi



  done



  run_cmd pnpm store prune || log "⚠️ pnpm store prune failed, continuing"



  run_cmd pnpm cache clean --all || log "⚠️ pnpm cache clean failed, continuing"



  log "✅ Cache cleanup complete."



}







# Build frontend, backend, shared packages with retries



build_all() {



  log "🏗️ Starting build process for all projects..."



  run_cmd pnpm --filter frontend build || { log "❌ Frontend build failed."; return 1; }



  run_cmd pnpm --filter backend build || { log "❌ Backend build failed."; return 1; }



  run_cmd pnpm --filter shared build || { log "❌ Shared build failed."; return 1; }



  log "✅ Build process completed successfully."



}







# Docker-compose startup with retries for both databases and dev environment



docker_up() {



  log "🐳 Starting Docker containers..."



  run_cmd docker-compose -f ./infra/docker/docker-compose-databases.yml up -d || { log "❌ Failed to start databases"; return 1; }



  run_cmd docker-compose -f ./infra/docker/docker-compose-dev.yml up -d || { log "❌ Failed to start dev environment"; return 1; }



  log "✅ Docker containers started successfully."



}







# Main execution sequence with error handling and summary logging



main() {



  log "🚀 === Setup Script Started ==="



  local start_time=$(date +%s)







  load_env_file



  check_versions



  clean_caches



  build_all



  docker_up







  local end_time=$(date +%s)



  local elapsed=$(( end_time - start_time ))







  log "🎉 === Setup Completed Successfully in ${elapsed}s ==="



}







main "$@"

load_env_file() {
  if [ -f "$ENV_PATH" ]; then
    log "Loading environment variables from $ENV_PATH"
    set -a
    source "$ENV_PATH"
    set +a
    if [[ -n "${GOOGLE_APPLICATION_CREDENTIALS:-}" ]]; then

    fi
  else
    log "WARNING: $ENV_PATH not found. Skipping environment loading."
  fi
}

run_cmd() {
  local attempt=1
  local cmd="$*"
  until $cmd; do
    if (( attempt >= MAX_RETRIES )); then
      log "ERROR: Command failed after $attempt attempts: $cmd"
      return 1
    fi
    local wait_sec=$(( RETRY_WAIT_INITIAL * attempt ))
    log "WARN: Command failed (attempt $attempt): $cmd"
    log "Retrying in $wait_sec seconds..."
    sleep $wait_sec
    (( attempt++ ))
  done
  log "SUCCESS: Command succeeded: $cmd"
  return 0
}

check_node_pnpm_versions() {
  local required_node_version="18.0.0"
  local required_pnpm_version="7.0.0"

  local node_version
  node_version=$(node -v 2>/dev/null || echo "none")
  local pnpm_version
  pnpm_version=$(pnpm -v 2>/dev/null || echo "none")

  log "Detected Node.js version: $node_version"
  log "Detected pnpm version: $pnpm_version"

  if [[ "$node_version" == "none" ]]; then
    log "ERROR: Node.js is not installed or not in PATH."
    exit 1
  fi

  if [[ "$pnpm_version" == "none" ]]; then
    log "ERROR: pnpm is not installed or not in PATH."
    exit 1
  fi

  # Simple version check (major only)
  local node_major=${node_version#v}
  node_major=${node_major%%.*}

  local req_node_major=${required_node_version%%.*}

  if (( node_major < req_node_major )); then
    log "ERROR: Node.js version $required_node_version or higher required."
    exit 1
  fi

  local pnpm_major=${pnpm_version%%.*}
  local req_pnpm_major=${required_pnpm_version%%.*}

  if (( pnpm_major < req_pnpm_major )); then
    log "ERROR: pnpm version $required_pnpm_version or higher required."
    exit 1
  fi
}

  log "Cleaning node_modules and pnpm caches..."

#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail
IFS=$'\n\t'

# === CONFIGURATION ===
LOGFILE="setup.log"
ENV_PATH=".env"
MAX_RETRIES=5
RETRY_WAIT_INITIAL=3  # seconds, exponential backoff multiplier
REQUIRED_NODE_VERSION="18.0.0"
REQUIRED_PNPM_VERSION="7.0.0"

# === UTILITIES ===
timestamp() {
  date "+%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S"
}

log() {
  local msg="$*"
  echo -e "$(timestamp) $msg" | tee -a "$LOGFILE"
}

# Retry a command with exponential backoff
run_cmd() {
  local attempt=1
  local delay=$RETRY_WAIT_INITIAL
  local cmd="$*"
  until $cmd; do
    if (( attempt >= MAX_RETRIES )); then
      log "❌ ERROR: Command failed after $attempt attempts: $cmd"
      return 1
    fi
    log "⚠️ WARN: Command failed (attempt $attempt): $cmd"
    log "Retrying in $delay seconds..."
    sleep "$delay"
    delay=$(( delay * 2 ))
    ((attempt++))
  done
  log "✅ SUCCESS: Command succeeded: $cmd"
  return 0
}

# Load environment variables safely, export GOOGLE_APPLICATION_CREDENTIALS if set
load_env_file() {
  if [[ -f "$ENV_PATH" ]]; then
    log "📦 Loading environment variables from $ENV_PATH"
    set -a
    # shellcheck source=/dev/null
    source "$ENV_PATH"
    set +a
    if [[ -n "${GOOGLE_APPLICATION_CREDENTIALS:-}" ]]; then
      export GOOGLE_APPLICATION_CREDENTIALS
      log "🔐 Exported GOOGLE_APPLICATION_CREDENTIALS=$GOOGLE_APPLICATION_CREDENTIALS"
    fi
  else
    log "⚠️ WARNING: $ENV_PATH not found; skipping environment loading"
  fi
}

# Compare semantic versions (only major.minor.patch, simple numeric)
version_ge() {
  # returns 0 if $1 >= $2, else 1
  # usage: version_ge "18.2.0" "18.0.0"
  local IFS=.
  local i ver1=($1) ver2=($2)
  # fill empty fields with zeros
  for ((i=${#ver1[@]}; i<3; i++)); do ver1[i]=0; done
  for ((i=${#ver2[@]}; i<3; i++)); do ver2[i]=0; done
  for ((i=0; i<3; i++)); do
    if ((10#${ver1[i]} > 10#${ver2[i]})); then
      return 0
    elif ((10#${ver1[i]} < 10#${ver2[i]})); then
      return 1
    fi
  done
  return 0
}

# Check Node.js and pnpm versions with detailed semantic comparison
check_versions() {
  local node_version node_version_clean pnpm_version

  node_version=$(node -v 2>/dev/null || echo "none")
  pnpm_version=$(pnpm -v 2>/dev/null || echo "none")

  log "🧪 Detected Node.js version: $node_version"
  log "🧪 Detected pnpm version: $pnpm_version"

  if [[ "$node_version" == "none" ]]; then
    log "❌ ERROR: Node.js is not installed or not in PATH."
    exit 1
  fi

  if [[ "$pnpm_version" == "none" ]]; then
    log "❌ ERROR: pnpm is not installed or not in PATH."
    exit 1
  fi

  node_version_clean="${node_version#v}"
  if ! version_ge "$node_version_clean" "$REQUIRED_NODE_VERSION"; then
    log "❌ ERROR: Node.js version $REQUIRED_NODE_VERSION or higher required."
    exit 1
  fi

  if ! version_ge "$pnpm_version" "$REQUIRED_PNPM_VERSION"; then
    log "❌ ERROR: pnpm version $REQUIRED_PNPM_VERSION or higher required."
    exit 1
  fi

  log "✅ Node.js and pnpm version requirements satisfied."
}

# Clean caches and node_modules with error-tolerant approach
clean_caches() {
  log "🧹 Cleaning node_modules and pnpm caches..."
  local dirs=(frontend/node_modules backend/node_modules shared/node_modules)
  for d in "${dirs[@]}"; do
    if [[ -d "$d" ]]; then
      rm -rf "$d" && log "🗑️ Removed $d"
    else
      log "ℹ️ Directory $d does not exist, skipping"
    fi
  done
  run_cmd pnpm store prune || log "⚠️ pnpm store prune failed, continuing"
  run_cmd pnpm cache clean --all || log "⚠️ pnpm cache clean failed, continuing"
  log "✅ Cache cleanup complete."
}

# Build frontend, backend, shared packages with retries
build_all() {
  log "🏗️ Starting build process for all projects..."
  run_cmd pnpm --filter frontend build || { log "❌ Frontend build failed."; return 1; }
  run_cmd pnpm --filter backend build || { log "❌ Backend build failed."; return 1; }
  run_cmd pnpm --filter shared build || { log "❌ Shared build failed."; return 1; }
  log "✅ Build process completed successfully."
}

# Docker-compose startup with retries for both databases and dev environment
docker_up() {
  log "🐳 Starting Docker containers..."
  run_cmd docker-compose -f ./infra/docker/docker-compose-databases.yml up -d || { log "❌ Failed to start databases"; return 1; }
  run_cmd docker-compose -f ./infra/docker/docker-compose-dev.yml up -d || { log "❌ Failed to start dev environment"; return 1; }
  log "✅ Docker containers started successfully."
}

# Main execution sequence with error handling and summary logging
main() {
  log "🚀 === Setup Script Started ==="
  local start_time=$(date +%s)

  load_env_file
  check_versions
  clean_caches
  build_all
  docker_up

  local end_time=$(date +%s)
  local elapsed=$(( end_time - start_time ))

  log "🎉 === Setup Completed Successfully in ${elapsed}s ==="
}

#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail
IFS=$'\n\t'

# === CONFIGURATION ===
LOGFILE="setup.log"
ENV_PATH=".env"
MAX_RETRIES=5
RETRY_WAIT_INITIAL=3  # seconds, exponential backoff base delay
REQUIRED_NODE_VERSION="18.0.0"
REQUIRED_PNPM_VERSION="7.0.0"

# === LOGGING ===
timestamp() {
  date "+%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S"
}

log() {
  local msg="$*"
  echo -e "$(timestamp) $msg" | tee -a "$LOGFILE"
}

# === RETRY WRAPPER ===
run_cmd() {
  local attempt=1
  local delay=$RETRY_WAIT_INITIAL
  local cmd="$*"

  until $cmd; do
    if (( attempt >= MAX_RETRIES )); then
      log "❌ ERROR: Command failed after $attempt attempts: $cmd"
      return 1
    fi
    log "⚠️ WARN: Command failed (attempt $attempt): $cmd"
    log "Retrying in $delay seconds..."
    sleep "$delay"
    delay=$(( delay * 2 ))
    ((attempt++))
  done

  log "✅ SUCCESS: Command succeeded: $cmd"
  return 0
}

# === ENVIRONMENT SETUP ===
load_env_file() {
  if [[ -f "$ENV_PATH" ]]; then
    log "📦 Loading environment variables from $ENV_PATH"
    set -a
    # shellcheck source=/dev/null
    source "$ENV_PATH"
    set +a
    if [[ -n "${GOOGLE_APPLICATION_CREDENTIALS:-}" ]]; then
      export GOOGLE_APPLICATION_CREDENTIALS
      log "🔐 Exported GOOGLE_APPLICATION_CREDENTIALS=$GOOGLE_APPLICATION_CREDENTIALS"
    fi
  else
    log "⚠️ WARNING: $ENV_PATH not found. Skipping environment loading."
  fi
}

# === SEMANTIC VERSION COMPARISON ===
version_ge() {
  # returns 0 if $1 >= $2 else 1
  # usage: version_ge "18.2.0" "18.0.0"
  local IFS=.
  local i ver1=($1) ver2=($2)
  for ((i=${#ver1[@]}; i<3; i++)); do ver1[i]=0; done
  for ((i=${#ver2[@]}; i<3; i++)); do ver2[i]=0; done
  for ((i=0; i<3; i++)); do
    if ((10#${ver1[i]} > 10#${ver2[i]})); then return 0; fi
    if ((10#${ver1[i]} < 10#${ver2[i]})); then return 1; fi
  done
  return 0
}

# === VERSION CHECKS ===
check_versions() {
  local node_version node_ver_clean pnpm_version

  node_version=$(node -v 2>/dev/null || echo "none")
  pnpm_version=$(pnpm -v 2>/dev/null || echo "none")

  log "🧪 Detected Node.js version: $node_version"
  log "🧪 Detected pnpm version: $pnpm_version"

  if [[ "$node_version" == "none" ]]; then
    log "❌ ERROR: Node.js is not installed or not in PATH."
    exit 1
  fi

  if [[ "$pnpm_version" == "none" ]]; then
    log "❌ ERROR: pnpm is not installed or not in PATH."
    exit 1
  fi

  node_ver_clean="${node_version#v}"

  if ! version_ge "$node_ver_clean" "$REQUIRED_NODE_VERSION"; then
    log "❌ ERROR: Node.js version $REQUIRED_NODE_VERSION or higher required."
    exit 1
  fi

  if ! version_ge "$pnpm_version" "$REQUIRED_PNPM_VERSION"; then
    log "❌ ERROR: pnpm version $REQUIRED_PNPM_VERSION or higher required."
    exit 1
  fi

  log "✅ Node.js and pnpm versions meet requirements."
}

# === CLEANUP ===
clean_caches() {
  log "🧹 Cleaning node_modules and pnpm caches..."
  local dirs=(frontend/node_modules backend/node_modules shared/node_modules)
  for d in "${dirs[@]}"; do
    if [[ -d "$d" ]]; then
      rm -rf "$d" && log "🗑️ Removed directory: $d"
    else
      log "ℹ️ Directory not found, skipping: $d"
    fi
  done

  run_cmd pnpm store prune || log "⚠️ pnpm store prune failed, continuing"
  run_cmd pnpm cache clean --all || log "⚠️ pnpm cache clean failed, continuing"
  log "✅ Cache cleanup completed."
}

# === BUILD ===
build_all() {
  log "🏗️ Starting build for frontend..."
  run_cmd pnpm --filter frontend build || { log "❌ Frontend build failed."; return 1; }

  log "🏗️ Starting build for backend..."
  run_cmd pnpm --filter backend build || { log "❌ Backend build failed."; return 1; }

  log "🏗️ Starting build for shared..."
  run_cmd pnpm --filter shared build || { log "❌ Shared build failed."; return 1; }

  log "✅ All builds completed successfully."
}

# === DOCKER ===
docker_up() {
  log "🐳 Starting database containers..."
  run_cmd docker-compose -f ./infra/docker/docker-compose-databases.yml up -d || { log "❌ Failed to start database containers."; return 1; }

  log "🐳 Starting development environment containers..."
  run_cmd docker-compose -f ./infra/docker/docker-compose-dev.yml up -d || { log "❌ Failed to start dev environment containers."; return 1; }

  log "✅ Docker containers started successfully."
}

# === MAIN ===
main() {
  log "🚀 === Setup Script Started ==="
  local start_ts=$(date +%s)

  load_env_file
  check_versions
  clean_caches
  build_all
  docker_up

  local end_ts=$(date +%s)
  local duration=$((end_ts - start_ts))

  log "🎉 === Setup Completed Successfully in ${duration}s ==="
}

main "$@"
