    if (( attempt >= MAX_RETRIES )); then

      log "ERROR: Command failed after $attempt attempts: $cmd"

      return 1

    fi

    local wait_sec=$(( RETRY_WAIT_INITIAL * attempt ))

  local required_pnpm_version="7.0.0"

  local pnpm_version

  local node_major=${node_version#v}

    exit 1

#!/usr/bin/env bash

set -euo pipefail

IFS=$'\n\t'



# === CONFIGURATION ===

LOGFILE="setup.log"

ENV_PATH=".env"

MAX_RETRIES=5

RETRY_WAIT_INITIAL=3  # seconds, exponential backoff multiplier

REQUIRED_NODE_VERSION="18.0.0"

REQUIRED_PNPM_VERSION="7.0.0"



# === UTILITIES ===

timestamp() {

  date "+%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S"

}



log() {

  local msg="$*"

  echo -e "$(timestamp) $msg" | tee -a "$LOGFILE"

}



# Retry a command with exponential backoff

run_cmd() {

  local attempt=1

  local delay=$RETRY_WAIT_INITIAL

  local cmd="$*"

  until $cmd; do

    if (( attempt >= MAX_RETRIES )); then

      log "❌ ERROR: Command failed after $attempt attempts: $cmd"

      return 1

    fi

    log "⚠️ WARN: Command failed (attempt $attempt): $cmd"

    log "Retrying in $delay seconds..."

    sleep "$delay"

    delay=$(( delay * 2 ))

    ((attempt++))

  done

  log "✅ SUCCESS: Command succeeded: $cmd"

  return 0

}



# Load environment variables safely, export GOOGLE_APPLICATION_CREDENTIALS if set

load_env_file() {

  if [[ -f "$ENV_PATH" ]]; then

    log "📦 Loading environment variables from $ENV_PATH"

    set -a

    # shellcheck source=/dev/null

    source "$ENV_PATH"

    set +a

    if [[ -n "${GOOGLE_APPLICATION_CREDENTIALS:-}" ]]; then

      export GOOGLE_APPLICATION_CREDENTIALS

      log "🔐 Exported GOOGLE_APPLICATION_CREDENTIALS=$GOOGLE_APPLICATION_CREDENTIALS"

    fi

  else

    log "⚠️ WARNING: $ENV_PATH not found; skipping environment loading"

  fi

}



# Compare semantic versions (only major.minor.patch, simple numeric)

version_ge() {

  # returns 0 if $1 >= $2, else 1

  # usage: version_ge "18.2.0" "18.0.0"

  local IFS=.

  local i ver1=($1) ver2=($2)

  # fill empty fields with zeros

  for ((i=${#ver1[@]}; i<3; i++)); do ver1[i]=0; done

  for ((i=${#ver2[@]}; i<3; i++)); do ver2[i]=0; done

  for ((i=0; i<3; i++)); do

    if ((10#${ver1[i]} > 10#${ver2[i]})); then

      return 0

    elif ((10#${ver1[i]} < 10#${ver2[i]})); then

      return 1

    fi

  done

  return 0

}



# Check Node.js and pnpm versions with detailed semantic comparison

check_versions() {

  local node_version node_version_clean pnpm_version



  node_version=$(node -v 2>/dev/null || echo "none")

  pnpm_version=$(pnpm -v 2>/dev/null || echo "none")



  log "🧪 Detected Node.js version: $node_version"

  log "🧪 Detected pnpm version: $pnpm_version"



  if [[ "$node_version" == "none" ]]; then

    log "❌ ERROR: Node.js is not installed or not in PATH."

    exit 1

  fi



  if [[ "$pnpm_version" == "none" ]]; then

    log "❌ ERROR: pnpm is not installed or not in PATH."

    exit 1

  fi



  node_version_clean="${node_version#v}"

  if ! version_ge "$node_version_clean" "$REQUIRED_NODE_VERSION"; then

    log "❌ ERROR: Node.js version $REQUIRED_NODE_VERSION or higher required."

    exit 1

  fi



  if ! version_ge "$pnpm_version" "$REQUIRED_PNPM_VERSION"; then

    log "❌ ERROR: pnpm version $REQUIRED_PNPM_VERSION or higher required."

    exit 1

  fi



  log "✅ Node.js and pnpm version requirements satisfied."

}



# Clean caches and node_modules with error-tolerant approach

clean_caches() {

  log "🧹 Cleaning node_modules and pnpm caches..."

  local dirs=(frontend/node_modules backend/node_modules shared/node_modules)

  for d in "${dirs[@]}"; do

    if [[ -d "$d" ]]; then

      rm -rf "$d" && log "🗑️ Removed $d"

    else

      log "ℹ️ Directory $d does not exist, skipping"

    fi

  done

  run_cmd pnpm store prune || log "⚠️ pnpm store prune failed, continuing"

  run_cmd pnpm cache clean --all || log "⚠️ pnpm cache clean failed, continuing"

  log "✅ Cache cleanup complete."

}



# Build frontend, backend, shared packages with retries

build_all() {

  log "🏗️ Starting build process for all projects..."

  run_cmd pnpm --filter frontend build || { log "❌ Frontend build failed."; return 1; }

  run_cmd pnpm --filter backend build || { log "❌ Backend build failed."; return 1; }

  run_cmd pnpm --filter shared build || { log "❌ Shared build failed."; return 1; }

  log "✅ Build process completed successfully."

}



# Docker-compose startup with retries for both databases and dev environment

docker_up() {

  log "🐳 Starting Docker containers..."

  run_cmd docker-compose -f ./infra/docker/docker-compose-databases.yml up -d || { log "❌ Failed to start databases"; return 1; }

  run_cmd docker-compose -f ./infra/docker/docker-compose-dev.yml up -d || { log "❌ Failed to start dev environment"; return 1; }

  log "✅ Docker containers started successfully."

}



# Main execution sequence with error handling and summary logging

main() {

  log "🚀 === Setup Script Started ==="

  local start_time=$(date +%s)



  load_env_file

  check_versions

  clean_caches

  build_all

  docker_up



  local end_time=$(date +%s)

  local elapsed=$(( end_time - start_time ))



  log "🎉 === Setup Completed Successfully in ${elapsed}s ==="

}



main "$@"

rehan@LAPTOP-KTJEL1I2 MINGW64 ~/OneDrive/Desktop/github_repos/Quran-recitation-mvp/mvp (sync-wip-20250619-073918) $ maybe useful for you going forward ; #!/usr/bin/env bash set -euo pipefail IFS=$'\n\t'

=== Configuration === REPOS=( "/c/Users/rehan/OneDrive/Desktop/github_repos/QEP-MVP" "/c/Users/rehan/OneDrive/Desktop/github_repos/Quran-recitation-mvp" "/c/Users/rehan/OneDrive/Desktop/github_repos/Quran-recitation-platform" ) DEFAULT_BRANCH="main" LOG_FILE="sync-git-auto.log" MAX_RETRIES=4 RETRY_DELAYS=(5 10 20 40) SENSITIVE_PATHS=(".env" "config/" "secrets/" "*.key") AUTO_MERGE_STRATEGY="${AUTO_MERGE_STRATEGY:-}" # Optional: "ours" or "theirs"

Arrays for summary declare -a SUCCESSFUL declare -a FAILED declare -a NEEDS_MANUAL_RESOLVE

=== Helper Functions === Log messages to stderr and append to log file log() { local level="$1" local message="[$(date '+%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S')] [$level] $2" echo "$message" >&2 # Send to stderr for console visibility echo "$message" >> "$LOG_FILE" # Append to log file }

Verify that the current directory is a valid Git repository with a remote check_git_repo() { if [ ! -d .git ]; then log "ERROR" "Not a Git repository: $PWD" return 1 fi if ! git remote get-url origin &>/dev/null; then log "ERROR" "Remote 'origin' not set in $PWD" return 1 fi }

Commit changes in submodules commit_submodules() { local commit_message="$1" log "INFO" "Checking for changes in submodules" export COMMIT_MSG="$commit_message" git submodule foreach --recursive ' if [ -n "$(git status --porcelain)" ]; then echo "[INFO] Committing changes in submodule $(pwd)" git add -A git commit -m "$COMMIT_MSG" || echo "[WARNING] No changes to commit in submodule $(pwd)" fi ' | while read -r line; do log "INFO" "$line"; done unset COMMIT_MSG }

Update .gitignore to exclude sensitive paths update_gitignore() { local updated=false for path in "${SENSITIVE_PATHS[@]}"; do if ! grep -q "^$path$" .gitignore 2>/dev/null; then echo "$path" >> .gitignore log "INFO" "Added '$path' to .gitignore" updated=true fi done if [ "$updated" = true ] && [ -f .gitignore ]; then git add .gitignore git commit -m "Update .gitignore to exclude sensitive paths" || true log "INFO" "Committed updated .gitignore" fi }

Unstage sensitive files from the index unstage_sensitive() { for path in "${SENSITIVE_PATHS[@]}"; do git reset HEAD "$path" 2>/dev/null || true if git ls-files --error-unmatch "$path" &>/dev/null; then log "WARNING" "Sensitive path '$path' detected in staging; unstaged it" fi done }

Commit all local changes, including submodules commit_local_changes() { local commit_message="$1" commit_submodules "$commit_message" git add -A unstage_sensitive if [ -n "$(git status --porcelain --untracked-files=no)" ]; then git commit -m "$commit_message" || { log "ERROR" "Failed to commit changes in $PWD" return 1 } log "INFO" "Committed local changes with message: '$commit_message'" else log "INFO" "No changes to commit after unstaging sensitive files" fi }

Create a WIP branch and return its name create_wip_branch() { local wip_branch="sync-wip-$(date '+%Y%m%d-%H%M%S')" git checkout -b "$wip_branch" || { log "ERROR" "Failed to create WIP branch in $PWD" return 1 } log "INFO" "Created WIP branch '$wip_branch'" echo "$wip_branch" }

Safely checkout the default branch, creating it if necessary safe_checkout_main() { if ! git rev-parse --verify "$DEFAULT_BRANCH" &>/dev/null; then log "INFO" "Creating branch '$DEFAULT_BRANCH'" git checkout -b "$DEFAULT_BRANCH" || return 1 elif [[ "$(git rev-parse --abbrev-ref HEAD)" != "$DEFAULT_BRANCH" ]]; then git checkout "$DEFAULT_BRANCH" || return 1 fi log "INFO" "Checked out $DEFAULT_BRANCH" }

Pull remote changes with fast-forward, falling back to merge if needed fast_forward_pull() { git fetch origin || { log "ERROR" "Failed to fetch from origin" return 1 } if git rev-parse --verify "origin/$DEFAULT_BRANCH" &>/dev/null; then if ! git merge --ff-only "origin/$DEFAULT_BRANCH" 2>/dev/null; then log "INFO" "Non-fast-forward update detected. Attempting merge." if ! git merge "origin/$DEFAULT_BRANCH" 2>/dev/null; then log "WARNING" "Merge conflict occurred" if [ -n "$AUTO_MERGE_STRATEGY" ]; then log "INFO" "Applying auto-merge strategy: $AUTO_MERGE_STRATEGY" git merge -X "$AUTO_MERGE_STRATEGY" "origin/$DEFAULT_BRANCH" || { log "ERROR" "Auto-merge failed" return 1 } else log "WARNING" "Manual intervention required for merge conflict" return 1 fi fi fi log "INFO" "Updated $DEFAULT_BRANCH to match origin/$DEFAULT_BRANCH" else log "INFO" "Remote branch '$DEFAULT_BRANCH' does not exist. Nothing to pull." fi }

Merge the WIP branch into the default branch merge_wip_branch() { local wip_branch="$1" log "INFO" "Merging WIP branch '$wip_branch' into $DEFAULT_BRANCH" if ! git merge "$wip_branch" 2>/dev/null; then log "WARNING" "Merge conflict when merging WIP branch" if [ -n "$AUTO_MERGE_STRATEGY" ]; then log "INFO" "Applying auto-merge strategy: $AUTO_MERGE_STRATEGY" git merge -X "$AUTO_MERGE_STRATEGY" "$wip_branch" || { log "ERROR" "Auto-merge of WIP branch failed" return 1 } else log "WARNING" "Manual intervention required for WIP merge conflict" NEEDS_MANUAL_RESOLVE+=("$PWD (WIP merge conflict)") return 1 fi fi git branch -d "$wip_branch" || log "WARNING" "Failed to delete WIP branch '$wip_branch'" log "INFO" "Merged and deleted WIP branch '$wip_branch'" }

Push changes to remote with retries attempt_push_with_retry() { local try=0 while ! git push origin "$DEFAULT_BRANCH" 2>/dev/null; do if [ $try -ge $MAX_RETRIES ]; then log "ERROR" "Push failed after $MAX_RETRIES retries" return 1 fi local delay=${RETRY_DELAYS[$try]} log "WARNING" "Push failed. Retrying in $delay seconds (Attempt $((try + 1))/$MAX_RETRIES)" sleep "$delay" ((try++)) git fetch origin || continue if ! git pull --rebase --autostash 2>/dev/null; then git pull --no-rebase || { log "ERROR" "Pull failed during retry" return 1 } fi done log "INFO" "Push succeeded after $try retries" }

Remove empty directories clean_empty_dirs() { find . -type d -empty -delete 2>/dev/null || log "WARNING" "Failed to clean empty directories" log "INFO" "Cleaned up empty directories" }

=== Main Sync Function === Synchronize a single repository with retry logic sync_repo() { local repo_path="$1" local commit_message="$2" local max_attempts=3 local attempt=1 local success=false

cd "$repo_path" || { log "ERROR" "Cannot access $repo_path"; return 1; } log "INFO" "=== Syncing repository: $repo_path ==="

if ! check_git_repo; then FAILED+=("$repo_path") return 1 fi

git submodule update --init --recursive || log "WARNING" "Failed to initialize submodules"

while [ $attempt -le $max_attempts ] && [ "$success" = false ]; do log "INFO" "Attempt $attempt of $max_attempts"

update_gitignore safe_checkout_main || continue commit_local_changes "$commit_message" || continue

local wip_branch="" if [ -n "$(git status --porcelain)" ] || (git rev-parse "origin/$DEFAULT_BRANCH" &>/dev/null && ! git diff --quiet "origin/$DEFAULT_BRANCH"); then wip_branch=$(create_wip_branch) || continue fi

fast_forward_pull || continue

if [ -n "$wip_branch" ]; then merge_wip_branch "$wip_branch" || continue fi

clean_empty_dirs attempt_push_with_retry && success=true || log "ERROR" "Push failed"

if [ "$success" = false ]; then log "WARNING" "Sync attempt $attempt failed, resetting changes" git reset --hard git checkout "$DEFAULT_BRANCH" sleep 2 fi ((attempt++)) done

if [ "$success" = true ]; then log "INFO" "Successfully synced $repo_path" SUCCESSFUL+=("$repo_path") else log "ERROR" "Failed to sync $repo_path after $max_attempts attempts" FAILED+=("$repo_path") fi }

=== Main Execution === ACTION=${1:-sync} COMMIT_MSG=${2:-"Auto sync commit $(date '+%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S')"} log "INFO" "=== Starting $ACTION operation with message: '$COMMIT_MSG' ==="

SUCCESSFUL=() FAILED=() NEEDS_MANUAL_RESOLVE=()

for repo in "${REPOS[@]}"; do if [ ! -d "$repo" ]; then log "ERROR" "Repository path does not exist: $repo" FAILED+=("$repo") continue fi sync_repo "$repo" "$COMMIT_MSG" done

log "INFO" "=== Synchronization Summary ===" log "INFO" "Successful syncs (${#SUCCESSFUL[@]}):" for repo in "${SUCCESSFUL[@]}"; do log "INFO" " - $repo" done log "INFO" "Failed syncs (${#FAILED[@]}):" for repo in "${FAILED[@]}"; do log "INFO" " - $repo" done if [ ${#NEEDS_MANUAL_RESOLVE[@]} -gt 0 ]; then log "WARNING" "Repositories needing manual resolution (${#NEEDS_MANUAL_RESOLVE[@]}):" for repo in "${NEEDS_MANUAL_RESOLVE[@]}"; do log "WARNING" " - $repo" done fi

if [ ${#FAILED[@]} -gt 0 ] || [ ${#NEEDS_MANUAL_RESOLVE[@]} -gt 0 ]; then log "ERROR" "Operation completed with issues. Check log for details." exit 1 else log "INFO" "Operation completed successfully." exit 0 fi rehan@LAPTOP-KTJEL1I2 MINGW64 ~/OneDrive/Desktop/github_repos/Quran-recitation-mvp/mvp (main) $ ./sync-git-auto.sh sync "Update sync auto" [2025-06-19 07:03:40] === RUN sync; commit message: 'Update sync auto' === [2025-06-19 07:03:40] === Sync start: /c/Users/rehan/OneDrive/Desktop/github_repos/QEP-MVP === Already on 'main' From https://github.com/Rehan719/QEP-MVP

=== Configuration === REPOS=( "/c/Users/rehan/OneDrive/Desktop/github_repos/QEP-MVP" "/c/Users/rehan/OneDrive/Desktop/github_repos/Quran-recitation-mvp" "/c/Users/rehan/OneDrive/Desktop/github_repos/Quran-recitation-platform" ) DEFAULT_BRANCH="main" LOG_FILE="sync-git-auto.log" MAX_RETRIES=4 RETRY_DELAYS=(5 10 20 40) SENSITIVE_PATHS=(".env" "config/" "secrets/" "*.key") AUTO_MERGE_STRATEGY="${AUTO_MERGE_STRATEGY:-}" # Optional: "ours" or "theirs"

Arrays for summary declare -a SUCCESSFUL declare -a FAILED declare -a NEEDS_MANUAL_RESOLVE

=== Helper Functions === Log messages to stderr and append to log file log() { local level="$1" local message="[$(date '+%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S')] [$level] $2" echo "$message" >&2 # Send to stderr for console visibility echo "$message" >> "$LOG_FILE" # Append to log file }

Verify that the current directory is a valid Git repository with a remote check_git_repo() { if [ ! -d .git ]; then log "ERROR" "Not a Git repository: $PWD" return 1 fi if ! git remote get-url origin &>/dev/null; then log "ERROR" "Remote 'origin' not set in $PWD" return 1 fi }

Commit changes in submodules commit_submodules() { local commit_message="$1" log "INFO" "Checking for changes in submodules" export COMMIT_MSG="$commit_message" git submodule foreach --recursive ' if [ -n "$(git status --porcelain)" ]; then echo "[INFO] Committing changes in submodule $(pwd)" git add -A git commit -m "$COMMIT_MSG" || echo "[WARNING] No changes to commit in submodule $(pwd)" fi ' | while read -r line; do log "INFO" "$line"; done unset COMMIT_MSG }

Update .gitignore to exclude sensitive paths update_gitignore() { local updated=false for path in "${SENSITIVE_PATHS[@]}"; do if ! grep -q "^$path$" .gitignore 2>/dev/null; then echo "$path" >> .gitignore log "INFO" "Added '$path' to .gitignore" updated=true fi done if [ "$updated" = true ] && [ -f .gitignore ]; then git add .gitignore git commit -m "Update .gitignore to exclude sensitive paths" || true log "INFO" "Committed updated .gitignore" fi }

Unstage sensitive files from the index unstage_sensitive() { for path in "${SENSITIVE_PATHS[@]}"; do git reset HEAD "$path" 2>/dev/null || true if git ls-files --error-unmatch "$path" &>/dev/null; then log "WARNING" "Sensitive path '$path' detected in staging; unstaged it" fi done }

Commit all local changes, including submodules commit_local_changes() { local commit_message="$1" commit_submodules "$commit_message" git add -A unstage_sensitive if [ -n "$(git status --porcelain --untracked-files=no)" ]; then git commit -m "$commit_message" || { log "ERROR" "Failed to commit changes in $PWD" return 1 } log "INFO" "Committed local changes with message: '$commit_message'" else log "INFO" "No changes to commit after unstaging sensitive files" fi }

Create a WIP branch and return its name create_wip_branch() { local wip_branch="sync-wip-$(date '+%Y%m%d-%H%M%S')" git checkout -b "$wip_branch" || { log "ERROR" "Failed to create WIP branch in $PWD" return 1 } log "INFO" "Created WIP branch '$wip_branch'" echo "$wip_branch" }

Safely checkout the default branch, creating it if necessary safe_checkout_main() { if ! git rev-parse --verify "$DEFAULT_BRANCH" &>/dev/null; then log "INFO" "Creating branch '$DEFAULT_BRANCH'" git checkout -b "$DEFAULT_BRANCH" || return 1 elif [[ "$(git rev-parse --abbrev-ref HEAD)" != "$DEFAULT_BRANCH" ]]; then git checkout "$DEFAULT_BRANCH" || return 1 fi log "INFO" "Checked out $DEFAULT_BRANCH" }

Pull remote changes with fast-forward, falling back to merge if needed fast_forward_pull() { git fetch origin || { log "ERROR" "Failed to fetch from origin" return 1 } if git rev-parse --verify "origin/$DEFAULT_BRANCH" &>/dev/null; then if ! git merge --ff-only "origin/$DEFAULT_BRANCH" 2>/dev/null; then log "INFO" "Non-fast-forward update detected. Attempting merge." if ! git merge "origin/$DEFAULT_BRANCH" 2>/dev/null; then log "WARNING" "Merge conflict occurred" if [ -n "$AUTO_MERGE_STRATEGY" ]; then log "INFO" "Applying auto-merge strategy: $AUTO_MERGE_STRATEGY" git merge -X "$AUTO_MERGE_STRATEGY" "origin/$DEFAULT_BRANCH" || { log "ERROR" "Auto-merge failed" return 1 } else log "WARNING" "Manual intervention required for merge conflict" return 1 fi fi fi log "INFO" "Updated $DEFAULT_BRANCH to match origin/$DEFAULT_BRANCH" else log "INFO" "Remote branch '$DEFAULT_BRANCH' does not exist. Nothing to pull." fi }

Merge the WIP branch into the default branch merge_wip_branch() { local wip_branch="$1" log "INFO" "Merging WIP branch '$wip_branch' into $DEFAULT_BRANCH" if ! git merge "$wip_branch" 2>/dev/null; then log "WARNING" "Merge conflict when merging WIP branch" if [ -n "$AUTO_MERGE_STRATEGY" ]; then log "INFO" "Applying auto-merge strategy: $AUTO_MERGE_STRATEGY" git merge -X "$AUTO_MERGE_STRATEGY" "$wip_branch" || { log "ERROR" "Auto-merge of WIP branch failed" return 1 } else log "WARNING" "Manual intervention required for WIP merge conflict" NEEDS_MANUAL_RESOLVE+=("$PWD (WIP merge conflict)") return 1 fi fi git branch -d "$wip_branch" || log "WARNING" "Failed to delete WIP branch '$wip_branch'" log "INFO" "Merged and deleted WIP branch '$wip_branch'" }

Push changes to remote with retries attempt_push_with_retry() { local try=0 while ! git push origin "$DEFAULT_BRANCH" 2>/dev/null; do if [ $try -ge $MAX_RETRIES ]; then log "ERROR" "Push failed after $MAX_RETRIES retries" return 1 fi local delay=${RETRY_DELAYS[$try]} log "WARNING" "Push failed. Retrying in $delay seconds (Attempt $((try + 1))/$MAX_RETRIES)" sleep "$delay" ((try++)) git fetch origin || continue if ! git pull --rebase --autostash 2>/dev/null; then git pull --no-rebase || { log "ERROR" "Pull failed during retry" return 1 } fi done log "INFO" "Push succeeded after $try retries" }

Remove empty directories clean_empty_dirs() { find . -type d -empty -delete 2>/dev/null || log "WARNING" "Failed to clean empty directories" log "INFO" "Cleaned up empty directories" }

=== Main Sync Function === Synchronize a single repository with retry logic sync_repo() { local repo_path="$1" local commit_message="$2" local max_attempts=3 local attempt=1 local success=false

cd "$repo_path" || { log "ERROR" "Cannot access $repo_path"; return 1; } log "INFO" "=== Syncing repository: $repo_path ==="

if ! check_git_repo; then FAILED+=("$repo_path") return 1 fi

git submodule update --init --recursive || log "WARNING" "Failed to initialize submodules"

while [ $attempt -le $max_attempts ] && [ "$success" = false ]; do log "INFO" "Attempt $attempt of $max_attempts"

update_gitignore safe_checkout_main || continue commit_local_changes "$commit_message" || continue

local wip_branch="" if [ -n "$(git status --porcelain)" ] || (git rev-parse "origin/$DEFAULT_BRANCH" &>/dev/null && ! git diff --quiet "origin/$DEFAULT_BRANCH"); then wip_branch=$(create_wip_branch) || continue fi

fast_forward_pull || continue

if [ -n "$wip_branch" ]; then merge_wip_branch "$wip_branch" || continue fi

clean_empty_dirs attempt_push_with_retry && success=true || log "ERROR" "Push failed"

if [ "$success" = false ]; then log "WARNING" "Sync attempt $attempt failed, resetting changes" git reset --hard git checkout "$DEFAULT_BRANCH" sleep 2 fi ((attempt++)) done

if [ "$success" = true ]; then log "INFO" "Successfully synced $repo_path" SUCCESSFUL+=("$repo_path") else log "ERROR" "Failed to sync $repo_path after $max_attempts attempts" FAILED+=("$repo_path") fi }

=== Main Execution === ACTION=${1:-sync} COMMIT_MSG=${2:-"Auto sync commit $(date '+%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S')"} log "INFO" "=== Starting $ACTION operation with message: '$COMMIT_MSG' ==="

SUCCESSFUL=() FAILED=() NEEDS_MANUAL_RESOLVE=()

for repo in "${REPOS[@]}"; do if [ ! -d "$repo" ]; then log "ERROR" "Repository path does not exist: $repo" FAILED+=("$repo") continue fi sync_repo "$repo" "$COMMIT_MSG" done

log "INFO" "=== Synchronization Summary ===" log "INFO" "Successful syncs (${#SUCCESSFUL[@]}):" for repo in "${SUCCESSFUL[@]}"; do log "INFO" " - $repo" done log "INFO" "Failed syncs (${#FAILED[@]}):" for repo in "${FAILED[@]}"; do log "INFO" " - $repo" done if [ ${#NEEDS_MANUAL_RESOLVE[@]} -gt 0 ]; then log "WARNING" "Repositories needing manual resolution (${#NEEDS_MANUAL_RESOLVE[@]}):" for repo in "${NEEDS_MANUAL_RESOLVE[@]}"; do log "WARNING" " - $repo" done fi

if [ ${#FAILED[@]} -gt 0 ] || [ ${#NEEDS_MANUAL_RESOLVE[@]} -gt 0 ]; then log "ERROR" "Operation completed with issues. Check log for details." exit 1 else log "INFO" "Operation completed successfully." exit 0 fi #!/usr/bin/env bash set -euo pipefail IFS=$'\n\t'

Arrays for summary declare -a SUCCESSFUL declare -a FAILED declare -a NEEDS_MANUAL_RESOLVE

=== Helper Functions === log() { local level="$1" local message="[$(date '+%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S')] [$level] $2" echo "$message" | tee -a "$LOG_FILE" }

prompt_user() { if [ "$INTERACTIVE_MODE" != "true" ]; then return 0 fi local message="$1" local response read -p "$message (y/n): " response [[ "$response" =~ ^[Yy] ]] && return 0 || return 1 }

check_git_repo() { if [ ! -d .git ]; then log "ERROR" "Not a Git repository: $PWD" return 1 fi if ! git remote get-url origin &>/dev/null; then log "ERROR" "Remote 'origin' not set in $PWD" return 1 fi }

update_gitignore() { local updated=false for path in "${SENSITIVE_PATHS[@]}"; do if ! grep -q "^$path$" .gitignore 2>/dev/null; then echo "$path" >> .gitignore log "INFO" "Added '$path' to .gitignore" updated=true fi done if [ "$updated" = true ] && [ -f .gitignore ]; then git add .gitignore git commit -m "Update .gitignore to exclude sensitive paths" || true log "INFO" "Committed updated .gitignore" fi }

unstage_sensitive() { for path in "${SENSITIVE_PATHS[@]}"; do git reset HEAD "$path" 2>/dev/null || true if git ls-files --error-unmatch "$path" &>/dev/null; then log "WARNING" "Sensitive path '$path' detected in staging; unstaged it" fi done }

commit_local_changes() { if [ -n "$(git status --porcelain)" ]; then git add -A unstage_sensitive if [ -n "$(git status --porcelain --untracked-files=no)" ]; then git commit -m "$1" || { log "ERROR" "Failed to commit changes in $PWD" return 1 } log "INFO" "Committed local changes with message: '$1'" else log "INFO" "No changes to commit after unstaging sensitive files" fi else log "INFO" "No local changes to commit" fi }

create_wip_branch() { local wip_branch="sync-wip-$(date '+%Y%m%d-%H%M%S')" git checkout -b "$wip_branch" || { log "ERROR" "Failed to create WIP branch in $PWD" return 1 } log "INFO" "Created WIP branch '$wip_branch'" echo "$wip_branch" }

safe_checkout_main() { if ! git rev-parse --verify "$DEFAULT_BRANCH" &>/dev/null; then log "INFO" "Creating branch '$DEFAULT_BRANCH' as it does not exist" git checkout -b "$DEFAULT_BRANCH" || return 1 elif [[ "$(git rev-parse --abbrev-ref HEAD)" != "$DEFAULT_BRANCH" ]]; then git checkout "$DEFAULT_BRANCH" || { log "ERROR" "Failed to checkout $DEFAULT_BRANCH" return 1 } fi log "INFO" "Checked out $DEFAULT_BRANCH" }

fast_forward_pull() { git fetch origin || { log "ERROR" "Failed to fetch from origin" return 1 } if git rev-parse --verify "origin/$DEFAULT_BRANCH" &>/dev/null; then if ! git merge --ff-only "origin/$DEFAULT_BRANCH" 2>/dev/null; then log "INFO" "Non-fast-forward update detected. Attempting merge." if ! git merge "origin/$DEFAULT_BRANCH" 2>/dev/null; then log "WARNING" "Merge conflict occurred" if [ -n "$AUTO_MERGE_STRATEGY" ]; then log "INFO" "Applying auto-merge strategy: $AUTO_MERGE_STRATEGY" git merge -X "$AUTO_MERGE_STRATEGY" "origin/$DEFAULT_BRANCH" || { log "ERROR" "Auto-merge failed" return 1 } else log "WARNING" "Manual intervention required for merge conflict" return 1 fi fi fi log "INFO" "Updated $DEFAULT_BRANCH to match origin/$DEFAULT_BRANCH" else log "INFO" "Remote branch '$DEFAULT_BRANCH' does not exist. Nothing to pull." fi }

merge_wip_branch() { local wip_branch="$1" log "INFO" "Merging WIP branch '$wip_branch' into $DEFAULT_BRANCH" if ! git merge "$wip_branch" 2>/dev/null; then log "WARNING" "Merge conflict when merging WIP branch" if [ -n "$AUTO_MERGE_STRATEGY" ]; then log "INFO" "Applying auto-merge strategy: $AUTO_MERGE_STRATEGY" git merge -X "$AUTO_MERGE_STRATEGY" "$wip_branch" || { log "ERROR" "Auto-merge of WIP branch failed" return 1 } else log "WARNING" "Manual intervention required for WIP merge conflict" NEEDS_MANUAL_RESOLVE+=("$PWD (WIP merge conflict)") return 1 fi fi git branch -d "$wip_branch" || log "WARNING" "Failed to delete WIP branch '$wip_branch'" log "INFO" "Merged and deleted WIP branch '$wip_branch'" }

attempt_push_with_retry() { local try=0 while ! git push origin "$DEFAULT_BRANCH" 2>/dev/null; do if [ $try -ge $MAX_RETRIES ]; then log "ERROR" "Push failed after $MAX_RETRIES retries" return 1 fi local delay=${RETRY_DELAYS[$try]} log "WARNING" "Push failed. Retrying in $delay seconds (Attempt $((try + 1))/$MAX_RETRIES)" sleep "$delay" ((try++)) git fetch origin || continue if ! git pull --rebase --autostash 2>/dev/null; then git pull --no-rebase || { log "ERROR" "Pull failed during retry" return 1 } fi done log "INFO" "Push succeeded after $try retries" }

clean_empty_dirs() { find . -type d -empty -delete 2>/dev/null || log "WARNING" "Failed to clean empty directories" log "INFO" "Cleaned up empty directories" }

=== Main Sync Function === sync_repo() { local repo_path="$1" local commit_message="$2" log "INFO" "=== Syncing repository: $repo_path ===" cd "$repo_path" || { log "ERROR" "Could not cd into $repo_path" return 1 }

if ! check_git_repo; then return 1 fi

update_gitignore safe_checkout_main || return 1 commit_local_changes "$commit_message" || return 1

local wip_branch="" if [ -n "$(git status --porcelain)" ] || (git rev-parse "origin/$DEFAULT_BRANCH" &>/dev/null && ! git diff --quiet "origin/$DEFAULT_BRANCH"); then wip_branch=$(create_wip_branch) || return 1 if [ "$INTERACTIVE_MODE" = "true" ]; then prompt_user "Proceed with WIP branch '$wip_branch'?" || { log "INFO" "User aborted WIP branch operation" git checkout "$DEFAULT_BRANCH" git branch -d "$wip_branch" 2>/dev/null return 1 } fi fi

fast_forward_pull || return 1

if [ -n "$wip_branch" ]; then merge_wip_branch "$wip_branch" || return 1 fi

clean_empty_dirs attempt_push_with_retry || return 1

log "INFO" "Sync completed successfully for $repo_path" }

=== Main Execution === ACTION=${1:-sync} COMMIT_MSG=${2:-"Auto sync commit $(date '+%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S')"} log "INFO" "=== Starting $ACTION operation with message: '$COMMIT_MSG' ==="

SUCCESSFUL=() FAILED=() NEEDS_MANUAL_RESOLVE=()

for repo in "${REPOS[@]}"; do if [ ! -d "$repo" ]; then log "ERROR" "Repository path does not exist: $repo" FAILED+=("$repo") continue fi if sync_repo "$repo" "$COMMIT_MSG"; then SUCCESSFUL+=("$repo") else FAILED+=("$repo") fi done

log "INFO" "=== Synchronization Summary ===" log "INFO" "Successful syncs (${#SUCCESSFUL[@]}):" for repo in "${SUCCESSFUL[@]}"; do log "INFO" " - $repo" done log "INFO" "Failed syncs (${#FAILED[@]}):" for repo in "${FAILED[@]}"; do log "INFO" " - $repo" done if [ ${#NEEDS_MANUAL_RESOLVE[@]} -gt 0 ]; then log "WARNING" "Repositories needing manual resolution (${#NEEDS_MANUAL_RESOLVE[@]}):" for repo in "${NEEDS_MANUAL_RESOLVE[@]}"; do log "WARNING" " - $repo" done fi

Exit with appropriate status if [ ${#FAILED[@]} -gt 0 ] || [ ${#NEEDS_MANUAL_RESOLVE[@]} -gt 0 ]; then log "ERROR" "Operation completed with issues. Check log for details." exit 1 else log "INFO" "Operation completed successfully." exit 0 fi #!/usr/bin/env bash set -euo pipefail IFS=$'\n'

BASE_DIR="/c/Users/rehan/OneDrive/Desktop/github_repos" LOG_DIR="$BASE_DIR/logs" LOCKFILE="$BASE_DIR/sync-git-auto.lock" MAX_RETRIES=5 RETRY_WAIT_BASE=5 GITHUB_REMOTE="origin" MAIN_BRANCH="main" SENSITIVE_PATHS=("config/" ".env") AUTO_MERGE_STRATEGY="${AUTO_MERGE_STRATEGY:-theirs}"

declare -a SUMMARY_OK=() declare -a SUMMARY_FAIL=() declare -a NEEDS_MANUAL_RESOLVE=() declare -a CONFLICT_REPORTS=()

trap cleanup EXIT

timestamp() { date '+%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S'; }

log() { echo "[$(timestamp)] $*" | tee -a "$RUN_LOG" }

cleanup() { local code=$? [[ -f "$LOCKFILE" ]] && rm -f "$LOCKFILE" if [[ $code -ne 0 ]]; then log "Script exited with code $code" fi exit $code }

acquire_lock() { if [[ -f "$LOCKFILE" ]]; then echo "Another sync is running. Exiting." exit 1 fi echo $$ > "$LOCKFILE" }

retry_cmd() { local retries=0 wait_sec=$RETRY_WAIT_BASE until "${@}"; do ((retries++)) if ((retries >= MAX_RETRIES)); then log "Failed after $MAX_RETRIES attempts: ${*}" return 1 fi log "Retrying in $wait_sec seconds..." sleep "$wait_sec" ((wait_sec *= 2)) done }

get_all_repos() { find "$BASE_DIR" -mindepth 1 -maxdepth 1 -type d -exec test -d '{}/.git' ';' -print }

validate_remote() { local repo=$1 cd "$repo" if ! git remote get-url "$GITHUB_REMOTE" &>/dev/null; then log "ERROR: Remote '$GITHUB_REMOTE' not set in $repo" cd - &>/dev/null return 1 fi if ! git ls-remote "$GITHUB_REMOTE" &>/dev/null; then log "ERROR: Cannot connect to remote '$GITHUB_REMOTE' in $repo" cd - &>/dev/null return 1 fi cd - &>/dev/null return 0 }

ensure_gitignore_and_unstage_sensitive() { local changed=0 for pat in "${SENSITIVE_PATHS[@]}"; do grep -qxF "$pat" .gitignore || echo "$pat" >> .gitignore done local staged staged=$(git diff --cached --name-only) while IFS= read -r f; do for pat in "${SENSITIVE_PATHS[@]}"; do [[ "$f" == $pat* ]] && git reset "$f" done done <<< "$staged" }

abort_rebase_merge_if_any() { [[ -d .git/rebase-apply || -d .git/rebase-merge || -f .git/MERGE_HEAD ]] && git rebase --abort || true }

clean_empty_dirs() { log "Cleaning empty directories..." find . -type d -empty -not -path './.git*' -exec rm -rf '{}' + }

prepare_and_pull_main() { abort_rebase_merge_if_any local need_wip=0 [[ -n "$(git status --porcelain)" ]] && need_wip=1 git rev-parse --verify HEAD &>/dev/null || return 0 git rev-parse --verify "$GITHUB_REMOTE/$MAIN_BRANCH" &>/dev/null || return 0 local LOCAL_HASH REMOTE_HASH LOCAL_HASH=$(git rev-parse HEAD) REMOTE_HASH=$(git rev-parse "$GITHUB_REMOTE/$MAIN_BRANCH")

local wip_branch="" if [[ "$LOCAL_HASH" != "$REMOTE_HASH" ]]; then need_wip=1 fi

if (( need_wip )); then local ts ts=$(date +%Y%m%d-%H%M%S) wip_branch="sync-wip-$ts" git branch "$wip_branch" log "Created WIP branch '$wip_branch' to save local work" fi

git checkout "$MAIN_BRANCH" retry_cmd git fetch "$GITHUB_REMOTE" "$MAIN_BRANCH" git merge --ff-only "$GITHUB_REMOTE/$MAIN_BRANCH" || true log "Fast-forwarded $MAIN_BRANCH to $GITHUB_REMOTE/$MAIN_BRANCH"

if [[ -n "$wip_branch" ]]; then log "Merging WIP branch '$wip_branch' into $MAIN_BRANCH" git merge --no-ff "$wip_branch" -m "Merge local WIP ($wip_branch) into $MAIN_BRANCH" || { NEEDS_MANUAL_RESOLVE+=("$PWD ($wip_branch merge failed)") return 1 } log "Merged WIP into $MAIN_BRANCH cleanly" git branch -d "$wip_branch" log "Deleted WIP branch '$wip_branch'" fi }

sync_repo() { local repo=$1 commit_msg=$2 log "=== Sync start: $repo ===" cd "$repo" || return 1

validate_remote "$repo" || { SUMMARY_FAIL+=("$repo (remote issue)") return 1 }

if ! git diff --quiet || ! git diff --cached --quiet; then git add . git commit -m "$commit_msg" || true log "Committed local uncommitted changes on $MAIN_BRANCH" fi

ensure_gitignore_and_unstage_sensitive prepare_and_pull_main || { SUMMARY_FAIL+=("$repo (merge issue)") return 1 }

ensure_gitignore_and_unstage_sensitive clean_empty_dirs retry_cmd git push "$GITHUB_REMOTE" "$MAIN_BRANCH" || { SUMMARY_FAIL+=("$repo (push failed)") return 1 }

SUMMARY_OK+=("$repo") log "Sync succeeded for $repo" }

main() { mkdir -p "$LOG_DIR" RUN_TS=$(date +%Y%m%d-%H%M%S) RUN_LOG="$LOG_DIR/sync-git-auto-$RUN_TS.log" LATEST_LOG="$LOG_DIR/sync-git-auto-latest.log" touch "$RUN_LOG" ln -sf "$RUN_LOG" "$LATEST_LOG"

acquire_lock local cmd=$1; shift mapfile -t repos < <(get_all_repos)

[[ ${#repos[@]} -eq 0 ]] && echo "No Git repos found." && exit 1

local commit_msg=${1:-"Auto-sync"} log "=== RUN $cmd; commit message: '$commit_msg' ==="

for repo in "${repos[@]}"; do if ! sync_repo "$repo" "$commit_msg"; then log "Sync issues in $repo" fi done

log "=== Summary ===" if (( ${#SUMMARY_OK[@]} > 0 )); then log "Succeeded in:" for r in "${SUMMARY_OK[@]}"; do log " - $r"; done fi

if (( ${#SUMMARY_FAIL[@]} > 0 )); then log "Failed or remote issues:" for r in "${SUMMARY_FAIL[@]}"; do log " - $r"; done fi

if (( ${#NEEDS_MANUAL_RESOLVE[@]} > 0 )); then log "Needs manual conflict resolution:" for r in "${NEEDS_MANUAL_RESOLVE[@]}"; do log " - $r"; done fi }

main "$@" #!/usr/bin/env bash set -euo pipefail IFS=$'\n\t'

=== Configuration === BASE_DIR="${BASE_DIR:-/c/Users/rehan/OneDrive/Desktop/github_repos}" LOG_DIR="$BASE_DIR/logs" LOCKFILE="$BASE_DIR/sync-git-auto.lock" MAX_RETRIES=5 RETRY_WAIT_BASE=5 GITHUB_REMOTE="${GITHUB_REMOTE:-origin}" MAIN_BRANCH="${MAIN_BRANCH:-main}" SENSITIVE_PATHS=("config/" ".env")

Arrays for summary declare -a SUMMARY_OK declare -a SUMMARY_FAIL declare -a NEEDS_MANUAL_RESOLVE

timestamp() { date "+%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S"; }

log() { echo "[$(timestamp)] $*" | tee -a "$RUN_LOG" }

cleanup() { local code=$? [[ -f "$LOCKFILE" ]] && rm -f "$LOCKFILE" if (( code != 0 )); then log "Script exited with code $code" else log "Script completed successfully" fi } trap cleanup EXIT

acquire_lock() { if [[ -f "$LOCKFILE" ]]; then local pid; pid=$(<"$LOCKFILE") if kill -0 "$pid" &>/dev/null; then echo "Another instance (PID $pid) running. Exiting." >&2 exit 1 else log "Stale lockfile detected (PID $pid not running). Overwriting." fi fi echo $$ > "$LOCKFILE" }

retry_cmd() { local retries=0 wait_sec=$RETRY_WAIT_BASE local cmd=( "$@" ) until "${cmd[@]}"; do ((retries++)) if (( retries >= MAX_RETRIES )); then log "ERROR: Command failed after $retries attempts: ${cmd[]}" return 1 fi log "WARN: Command failed, retry $retries/$MAX_RETRIES: ${cmd[]}" sleep "$wait_sec" wait_sec=$(( wait_sec * 2 )) done }

check_connectivity() { if ! git ls-remote "$GITHUB_REMOTE" &>/dev/null; then log "ERROR: Cannot reach remote '$GITHUB_REMOTE' for $(pwd)." return 1 fi return 0 }

abort_rebase_merge_if_any() { if [[ -d ".git/rebase-apply" || -d ".git/rebase-merge" ]]; then log "Detected in-progress rebase in $(pwd). Aborting..." git rebase --abort &>/dev/null || log "Warning: rebase abort failed" fi if [[ -f ".git/MERGE_HEAD" ]]; then log "Detected in-progress merge in $(pwd). Aborting..." git merge --abort &>/dev/null || log "Warning: merge abort failed" fi }

stash_uncommitted() { STASHED=0 if ! git diff --quiet || ! git diff --cached --quiet || [[ -n "$(git ls-files --others --exclude-standard)" ]]; then if git stash push --include-untracked -m "sync-git-auto stash" &>/dev/null; then log "Stashed local changes."; STASHED=1 else log "Warning: Failed to stash local changes." fi fi }

pop_stash_if_any() { if [[ "${STASHED:-0}" -eq 1 ]]; then if git stash list | grep -q "sync-git-auto stash"; then git stash pop &>/dev/null && log "Re-applied stashed changes." || log "Warning: Failed to reapply stash." fi fi }

clean_empty_dirs() { log "Cleaning empty directories..." find . -type d -empty -not -path "./.git*" -exec rm -rf {} + 2>/dev/null || true }

get_all_repos() { find "$BASE_DIR" -mindepth 1 -maxdepth 1 -type d -exec test -d "{}/.git" ; -print || true }

validate_remote() { local repo="$1"; cd "$repo" if ! git remote get-url "$GITHUB_REMOTE" &>/dev/null; then log "ERROR: Remote '$GITHUB_REMOTE' not set in $repo"; cd - >/dev/null; return 1 fi if ! check_connectivity; then log "ERROR: Cannot reach remote in $repo"; cd - >/dev/null; return 1 fi cd - >/dev/null; return 0 }

capture_repo_state() { log "Capturing state in $(pwd):" log "-> git status:" git status | tee -a "$RUN_LOG" log "-> Unmerged/conflicts:" local conflicts conflicts=$(git diff --name-only --diff-filter=U || true) if [[ -n "$conflicts" ]]; then while IFS= read -r f; do log " - $f"; done <<<"$conflicts" else log " (none)" fi log "-> Recent reflog:" git reflog -n 5 | tee -a "$RUN_LOG" }

ensure_gitignore_and_unstage_sensitive() { # At repo root: append to .gitignore and unstage any sensitive local changed=0 for pat in "${SENSITIVE_PATHS[@]}"; do if ! grep -qxF "$pat" .gitignore 2>/dev/null; then echo "$pat" >> .gitignore changed=1 log "Appended '$pat' to .gitignore" fi done if (( changed )); then git add .gitignore git commit -m "chore: update .gitignore to exclude sensitive files" || log "Warn: .gitignore commit failed" fi # Unstage any staged sensitive files local staged staged=$(git diff --cached --name-only || true) while IFS= read -r f; do for pat in "${SENSITIVE_PATHS[@]}"; do if [[ "$f" == "$pat"* || "$f" == "$pat" ]]; then git rm --cached --ignore-unmatch "$f" &>/dev/null && log "Unstaged sensitive file: $f" fi done done <<<"$staged" }

Pull remote main (fast-forward or merge), but preserve local via WIP branch prepare_and_pull_main() { abort_rebase_merge_if_any

Determine if there are local commits not yet on remote, or uncommitted changes local need_wip=0 # Check uncommitted: if ! git diff --quiet || ! git diff --cached --quiet || [[ -n "$(git ls-files --others --exclude-standard)" ]]; then need_wip=1 else # Check if local main diverged: if HEAD not equal to origin/main if git rev-parse --verify HEAD &>/dev/null && git rev-parse --verify "$GITHUB_REMOTE/$MAIN_BRANCH" &>/dev/null; then local LOCAL_HASH REMOTE_HASH LOCAL_HASH=$(git rev-parse HEAD) REMOTE_HASH=$(git rev-parse "$GITHUB_REMOTE/$MAIN_BRANCH") if [[ "$LOCAL_HASH" != "$REMOTE_HASH" ]]; then # They differ; but maybe local behind or ahead. To preserve local, mark need_wip. need_wip=1 fi fi fi
local wip_branch="" if (( need_wip )); then # Create a unique WIP branch local ts=$(date +'%Y%m%d-%H%M%S') wip_branch="sync-wip-$ts" git branch "$wip_branch" || { log "ERROR: Could not create WIP branch $wip_branch"; return 1; } log "Created WIP branch '$wip_branch' to save local work" fi

Now ensure main is up-to-date with remote # Checkout main if ! git checkout "$MAIN_BRANCH"; then log "ERROR: Cannot checkout $MAIN_BRANCH in $(pwd)"; capture_repo_state; return 1 fi
Pull remote. Use fetch+merge to preserve history rather than reset. if ! retry_cmd git fetch "$GITHUB_REMOTE" "$MAIN_BRANCH"; then log "ERROR: fetch failed for $GITHUB_REMOTE/$MAIN_BRANCH"; return 1 fi
If local main has diverged, this merge may produce conflicts, but we'll handle after merging WIP if ! git merge --ff-only "$GITHUB_REMOTE/$MAIN_BRANCH" &>/dev/null; then # Cannot fast-forward; perform a merge commit log "Local main not fast-forwardable; merging remote into main" if ! git merge "$GITHUB_REMOTE/$MAIN_BRANCH" -m "Merge remote $GITHUB_REMOTE/$MAIN_BRANCH into main"; then log "ERROR: Merge remote/main into local main failed. Manual resolution needed." capture_repo_state # If WIP branch exists, leave state so user can resolve NEEDS_MANUAL_RESOLVE+=("$(pwd) (merge remote/main into main)") return 1 fi else log "Fast-forwarded main to $GITHUB_REMOTE/$MAIN_BRANCH" fi
If we created a WIP branch, now merge it back into main if [[ -n "$wip_branch" ]]; then log "Merging WIP branch '$wip_branch' into main" if git merge --no-ff "$wip_branch" -m "Merge local WIP ($wip_branch) into main"; then log "Merged WIP into main cleanly" # Delete WIP branch git branch -d "$wip_branch" &>/dev/null && log "Deleted WIP branch '$wip_branch'" else log "Conflict merging WIP branch '$wip_branch' into main. Manual resolution required." capture_repo_state NEEDS_MANUAL_RESOLVE+=("$(pwd) (conflict merging WIP)") # leave WIP branch intact for manual resolution return 1 fi fi
return 0 }

sync_repo() { local repo="$1"; shift local commit_msg="$1" log "=== Sync start: $repo ===" cd "$repo"

if ! validate_remote "$repo"; then SUMMARY_FAIL+=("$repo (remote issue)"); cd - >/dev/null; return 1 fi

Stage & commit uncommitted changes to avoid losing them if ! git diff --quiet || ! git diff --cached --quiet || [[ -n "$(git ls-files --others --exclude-standard)" ]]; then git add . if git commit -m "$commit_msg"; then log "Committed local uncommitted changes on main" else log "WARN: Commit of local changes failed" fi fi
ensure_gitignore_and_unstage_sensitive

Fetch & merge remote main, preserving local via WIP if needed if ! prepare_and_pull_main; then log "ERROR: Could not integrate remote/main with local in $repo" SUMMARY_FAIL+=("$repo (needs manual merge)") cd - >/dev/null; return 1 fi
ensure_gitignore_and_unstage_sensitive

clean_empty_dirs

Finally push merged main if ! retry_cmd git push "$GITHUB_REMOTE" "$MAIN_BRANCH"; then log "ERROR: Push failed in $repo" SUMMARY_FAIL+=("$repo (push failed)"); cd - >/dev/null; return 1 fi
SUMMARY_OK+=("$repo") log "Sync succeeded for $repo" cd - >/dev/null; return 0 }

merge_branches() { local repo="$1"; shift local auto_resolve="$1"; shift local branches=( "$@" ) log "=== Merge start: $repo branches: ${branches[*]} ===" cd "$repo" if ! validate_remote "$repo"; then SUMMARY_FAIL+=("$repo (remote issue)"); cd - >/dev/null; return 1 fi

First ensure sync with remote if ! sync_repo "$repo" "WIP before merge"; then log "ERROR: Pre-merge sync failed in $repo" cd - >/dev/null; return 1 fi
for br in "${branches[@]}"; do log "Merging branch '$br' into main in $repo" if ! retry_cmd git fetch "$GITHUB_REMOTE" "$br:$br"; then log "WARN: Failed to fetch $br"; SUMMARY_FAIL+=("$repo (fetch $br failed)"); continue fi if git merge --no-ff "$br" -m "Merge $br into main"; then log "Merged $br cleanly" else log "Conflict merging $br in $repo" if [[ "$auto_resolve" == "true" ]]; then log "Auto-resolving by accepting theirs for $br" git checkout --theirs . &>/dev/null git add . &>/dev/null git commit -m "Auto-resolved conflict: accepted theirs from $br" &>/dev/null && log "Auto-resolve commit succeeded" else capture_repo_state SUMMARY_FAIL+=("$repo (conflict on $br)") cd - >/dev/null; return 1 fi fi ensure_gitignore_and_unstage_sensitive done

clean_empty_dirs

if ! retry_cmd git push "$GITHUB_REMOTE" "$MAIN_BRANCH"; then SUMMARY_FAIL+=("$repo (push after merge failed)"); cd - >/dev/null; return 1 fi

SUMMARY_OK+=("$repo") log "Merge succeeded for $repo" cd - >/dev/null; return 0 }

clean_repo() { local repo="$1" log "=== Clean start: $repo ===" cd "$repo" if git filter-repo --force --invert-paths --path config/firebase-credendials.json --path config/google-credendials.json --path .env; then log "Filter-repo succeeded" if git remote | grep -q "^$GITHUB_REMOTE$"; then retry_cmd git push --force "$GITHUB_REMOTE" "$MAIN_BRANCH" && log "Force-pushed cleaned history" || SUMMARY_FAIL+=("$repo (clean push failed)") else log "No remote; skipping push"; SUMMARY_FAIL+=("$repo (no origin for clean)") fi else SUMMARY_FAIL+=("$repo (filter-repo failed)"); log "ERROR: filter-repo failed" fi cd - >/dev/null }

send_alert() { :; }

usage() { cat <<EOF Usage: $0 sync [commit message] # Commit local changes, merge remote changes, push $0 merge [--auto-resolve] <branches...> # Merge given branches into main after syncing $0 clean # Remove sensitive files from history EOF exit 1 }

main() { mkdir -p "$LOG_DIR" RUN_TS="$(date +'%Y%m%d-%H%M%S')" RUN_LOG="$LOG_DIR/sync-git-auto-$RUN_TS.log" LATEST_LOG="$LOG_DIR/sync-git-auto-latest.log" touch "$RUN_LOG" ln -sf "$RUN_LOG" "$LATEST_LOG" 2>/dev/null || cp -f "$RUN_LOG" "$LATEST_LOG"

sync_repo() { local repo_path="$1" local commit_msg="$2"

if [ ! -d "$repo_path" ]; then log "Repo not found: $repo_path" return 1 fi

log "Starting sync for repo: $repo_path" cd "$repo_path"

Add all except config/ and .env git add --all -- ":(exclude)config/" ":(exclude).env"

clean_empty_dirs

if ! retry_cmd git pull --rebase origin main; then log "ERROR: Pull failed in $repo_path" return 1 fi

if ! retry_cmd git push origin main; then log "ERROR: Push failed in $repo_path" return 1 fi

log "Sync completed for $repo_path" cd - > /dev/null }

merge_branches() { local repo_path="$1" local auto_resolve="$2" shift 2 local branches=("$@")

if [ ! -d "$repo_path" ]; then log "Repo not found: $repo_path" return 1 fi

log "Starting merge into main for repo: $repo_path" cd "$repo_path"

retry_cmd git checkout main retry_cmd git pull --rebase origin main

for branch in "${branches[@]}"; do log "Merging branch $branch into main" if ! git fetch origin "$branch:$branch"; then log "WARN: Failed to fetch branch $branch" continue fi

if ! git merge --no-ff "$branch" -m "Merged $branch into main"; then if [ "$auto_resolve" == "true" ]; then log "Conflict detected, auto-resolving by accepting theirs for $branch" git checkout --theirs . git add . git commit -m "Auto-resolved conflict: accepted theirs from $branch" else log "Conflict in $branch, manual resolution required. Exiting." exit 1 fi fi done

clean_empty_dirs

if ! retry_cmd git push origin main; then log "ERROR: Push failed after merge in $repo_path" return 1 fi

log "Merge complete for $repo_path" cd - > /dev/null }

usage() { cat <<EOF Usage: $0 sync [commit message] # Commit and push local changes $0 merge [--auto-resolve] <branches...> # Merge branches into main, optionally auto-resolving conflicts $0 clean # Clean repos from sensitive files (git filter-repo) EOF exit 1 }

main() { if [ "$#" -lt 1 ]; then usage fi

local command="$1" shift

case "$command" in sync) local commit_msg="${1:-Auto commit}" local repos repos=$(get_all_repos) for repo in $repos; do if ! sync_repo "$repo" "$commit_msg"; then send_alert log "Error syncing $repo" fi done ;; merge) local auto_resolve="false" if [ "${1:-}" == "--auto-resolve" ]; then auto_resolve="true" shift fi if [ "$#" -lt 1 ]; then usage fi local branches=("$@") local repos repos=$(get_all_repos) for repo in $repos; do if ! merge_branches "$repo" "$auto_resolve" "${branches[@]}"; then send_alert log "Error merging in $repo" fi done ;; clean) local repos repos=$(get_all_repos) for repo in $repos; do log "Cleaning repo $repo (filter-repo)..." cd "$repo" git filter-repo --force --invert-paths --path config/firebase-credentials.json --path config/google-credentials.json --path .env || log "Filter-repo failed for $repo" git push --force origin main || log "Force push failed for $repo" cd - > /dev/null done ;; *) usage ;; esac

log "Script execution completed" }

Complete setup-and-run.sh Script
Below is the regenerated and optimized setup-and-run.sh script, designed for copy-pasting into Visual Studio Code (VS Code). It maximizes functionality, captures current state, planning, progress, recent changes, GitHub updates, and issues/errors, while facilitating collaboration between you (the developer), Grok (LLM), and Jules (AI agent) on GitHub and VS Code. The script is POSIX-compliant, Windows-compatible (MINGW64/Git Bash), and focuses on robust logging, state management, and error recovery.
bash

#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail
IFS=$'\n\t'

# === CONFIGURATION ===
# Script root directory and output paths
SCRIPT_DIR=$(cd "$(dirname "$0")" && pwd)
LOG_DIR="$SCRIPT_DIR/collaboration/logs"
mkdir -p "$LOG_DIR"

# Output files for collaboration and tracking
LOG_FILE="$LOG_DIR/setup.log"
STATE_FILE="$LOG_DIR/state.json"
SUMMARY_FILE="$LOG_DIR/summary.json"
TROUBLESHOOTING_GUIDE="$LOG_DIR/troubleshooting_guide.txt"
EXPERIENCE_DB="$LOG_DIR/experience.json"

# Project-specific paths
ENV_PATH="$SCRIPT_DIR/config/.env"
COMPOSE_FILES=(
  "$SCRIPT_DIR/infra/docker/docker-compose-databases.yml"
  "$SCRIPT_DIR/infra/docker/docker-compose-dev.yml"
)
PROJECT_DIRS=("src/shared" "src/frontend" "src/backend")

# Required versions and environment variables
REQUIRED_NODE_VERSION="18.0.0"
REQUIRED_PNPM_VERSION="8.0.0"
REQUIRED_ENV_VARS=("GOOGLE_APPLICATION_CREDENTIALS")

# Command-line flags for customization
VERBOSE=false
DEBUG=false
DRY_RUN=false
RESUME=false
NO_PARALLEL=false
CHECK_GIT=false
TIMEOUT=600

# Tracking arrays and associative array for state
declare -a SUCCESSFUL_STEPS
declare -a FAILED_STEPS
declare -a DEPRECATED_DEPS
declare -A STATE

# === UTILITY FUNCTIONS ===
# Generate timestamp for logging
timestamp() {
  date "+%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S"
}

# Log messages to terminal and file with levels and emojis
log() {
  local level="$1"
  local msg="$2"
  local emoji=""
  case "$level" in
    "INFO") emoji="ℹ️ " ;;
    "WARNING") emoji="⚠️ " ;;
    "ERROR") emoji="❌ " ;;
    "SUCCESS") emoji="✅ " ;;
    "DEBUG") emoji="🐛 " ;;
  esac
  if [[ "$level" != "DEBUG" || "$VERBOSE" = true || "$DEBUG" = true ]]; then
    echo -e "$(timestamp) $emoji[$level] $msg" >&2 | tee -a "$LOG_FILE"
  else
    echo -e "$(timestamp) $emoji[$level] $msg" >> "$LOG_FILE"
  fi
}

# Run command with timeout, logging, and dry-run support
run_cmd() {
  local cmd="$*"
  local cmd_display="${cmd//[^[:print:]]/ }"
  if [ "$DRY_RUN" = true ]; then
    log "INFO" "Dry-run: $cmd_display"
    return 0
  fi
  log "INFO" "Executing: $cmd_display"
  local output exit_code=0
  if ! output=$(timeout "$TIMEOUT" bash -c "$cmd" 2>&1); then
    exit_code=$?
    log "ERROR" "Command failed: $cmd_display"
    log "ERROR" "Output: $output"
    update_experience_db "command_failed" "$cmd_display" "$output" "Check $LOG_FILE and $TROUBLESHOOTING_GUIDE"
    return $exit_code
  fi
  log "SUCCESS" "Command succeeded: $cmd_display"
  echo "$output" >> "$LOG_FILE"
  return 0
}

# Compare version numbers (e.g., 1.2.3 >= 1.2.0)
version_ge() {
  local v1="$1"
  local v2="$2"
  v1=${v1#v}
  v2=${v2#v}
  IFS='.' read -ra ver1 <<< "$v1"
  IFS='.' read -ra ver2 <<< "$v2"
  for ((i=${#ver1[@]}; i<3; i++)); do ver1[i]=0; done
  for ((i=${#ver2[@]}; i<3; i++)); do ver2[i]=0; done
  for ((i=0; i<3; i++)); do
    local num1=${ver1[i]:-0}
    local num2=${ver2[i]:-0}
    num1=$((10#$num1))
    num2=$((10#$num2))
    if (( num1 > num2 )); then return 0; fi
    if (( num1 < num2 )); then return 1; fi
  done
  return 0
}

# Update experience database with error details
update_experience_db() {
  local error_type="$1"
  local context="$2"
  local output="$3"
  local resolution="$4"
  if ! command -v jq >/dev/null 2>&1; then
    log "WARNING" "jq not installed. Cannot update $EXPERIENCE_DB. Install with: sudo apt-get install jq"
    return 1
  fi
  local entry
  entry=$(jq -n \
    --arg type "$error_type" \
    --arg ctx "$context" \
    --arg out "$output" \
    --arg res "$resolution" \
    --arg ts "$(timestamp)" \
    --arg success_rate "0" \
    '{type: $type, context: $ctx, output: $out, resolution: $res, timestamp: $ts, success_rate: $success_rate}')
  if [ -f "$EXPERIENCE_DB" ]; then
    jq ". + [$entry] | sort_by(.timestamp) | reverse | .[:100]" "$EXPERIENCE_DB" > "${EXPERIENCE_DB}.tmp" && mv "${EXPERIENCE_DB}.tmp" "$EXPERIENCE_DB"
  else
    echo "[$entry]" > "$EXPERIENCE_DB"
  fi
  log "DEBUG" "Updated $EXPERIENCE_DB with $error_type"
}

# Check experience database for known fixes
check_experience_db() {
  local error_type="$1"
  local context="$2"
  if [ -f "$EXPERIENCE_DB" ] && command -v jq >/dev/null 2>&1; then
    local resolution
    resolution=$(jq -r ".[] | select(.type==\"$error_type\" and .context | contains(\"$context\")) | .resolution" "$EXPERIENCE_DB" | head -n 1)
    if [ -n "$resolution" ]; then
      log "INFO" "Applying known fix: $resolution"
      if eval "$resolution"; then
        log "SUCCESS" "Fix applied successfully"
        return 0
      else
        log "ERROR" "Failed to apply fix: $resolution"
        return 1
      fi
    fi
  fi
  return 1
}

# Save state to file
update_state() {
  local step="$1"
  local status="$2"
  STATE["$step"]="$status"
  if command -v jq >/dev/null 2>&1; then
    local json="{"
    local first=true
    for key in "${!STATE[@]}"; do
      if [ "$first" = true ]; then
        first=false
      else
        json+=","
      fi
      json+="\"$key\":\"${STATE[$key]}\""
    done
    json+="}"
    echo "$json" | jq . > "$STATE_FILE"
    log "DEBUG" "Saved state: $step -> $status"
  else
    log "WARNING" "jq not installed. State not saved to $STATE_FILE."
  fi
}

# Generate troubleshooting guide for collaboration
generate_troubleshooting_guide() {
  log "INFO" "Generating $TROUBLESHOOTING_GUIDE"
  {
    echo "Troubleshooting Guide for setup-and-run.sh ($(timestamp))"
    echo ""
    echo "1. Workspace Configuration:"
    echo "   - Verify pnpm-workspace.yaml contains:"
    echo "     packages:"
    echo "       - src/shared"
    echo "       - src/frontend"
    echo "       - src/backend"
    echo "   - Fix: echo -e \"packages:\n  - src/shared\n  - src/frontend\n  - src/backend\" > pnpm-workspace.yaml"
    echo ""
    echo "2. Postinstall Script:"
    echo "   - Check package.json scripts:"
    echo "     \"postinstall\": \"pnpm --filter src/shared install && pnpm --filter src/frontend install && pnpm --filter src/backend install\""
    echo "   - Fix: jq '.scripts.postinstall = \"pnpm --filter src/shared install && pnpm --filter src/frontend install && pnpm --filter src/backend install\"' package.json > tmp.json && mv tmp.json package.json"
    echo ""
    echo "3. Missing Exports:"
    echo "   - Check src/shared/src/index.ts for:"
    echo "     export type UserRole = 'admin' | 'user' | 'guest';"
    echo "   - Fix: echo \"export type UserRole = 'admin' | 'user' | 'guest';\" >> src/shared/src/index.ts"
    echo "   - Rebuild shared: pnpm --filter src/shared build"
    echo ""
    echo "4. TypeScript Configuration:"
    echo "   - Verify src/shared/tsconfig.json:"
    echo "     { \"compilerOptions\": { \"outDir\": \"./dist\", \"declaration\": true } }"
    echo "   - Verify src/frontend/tsconfig.json:"
    echo "     { \"compilerOptions\": { \"types\": [\"vite/client\", \"node\"], \"paths\": {\"@quran-platform-mvp/shared\": [\"../shared/src\"]} } }"
    echo "   - Fix: Update tsconfig.json with correct paths and types"
    echo ""
    echo "5. Vite Configuration:"
    echo "   - Check src/frontend/vite.config.ts for:"
    echo "     resolve: { alias: {'@quran-platform-mvp/shared': path.resolve(__dirname, '../shared/src')} }"
    echo "   - Fix: Add alias to vite.config.ts"
    echo ""
    echo "6. Missing Dependencies:"
    echo "   - Ensure frontend/package.json includes: react, react-dom, vite"
    echo "   - Run: pnpm --filter src/frontend add react react-dom vite"
    echo ""
    echo "7. Build Failures:"
    echo "   - Review: $LOG_FILE, $STATE_FILE, $SUMMARY_FILE"
    echo "   - Retry: ./setup-and-run.sh --verbose --resume"
    echo ""
    echo "8. Docker Issues:"
    echo "   - Verify Docker is running and files exist: ${COMPOSE_FILES[*]}"
    echo "   - Run: docker-compose -f <file> up -d"
    echo ""
    echo "9. Debug Mode:"
    echo "   - Run: ./setup-and-run.sh --debug"
    echo "   - Review: $LOG_FILE, $EXPERIENCE_DB, $SUMMARY_FILE"
    echo ""
    echo "10. GitHub Collaboration:"
    echo "   - Check for uncommitted changes: git status"
    echo "   - Push updates: git push"
    echo "   - Share logs and outputs via GitHub issues or PRs"
    echo ""
    echo "For further assistance, share $LOG_FILE and $EXPERIENCE_DB with collaborators."
  } > "$TROUBLESHOOTING_GUIDE"
}

# === CORE FUNCTIONS ===
# Check Node.js and pnpm versions
check_versions() {
  log "INFO" "Checking version requirements"
  local node_version pnpm_version
  node_version=$(node -v 2>/dev/null || echo "none")
  pnpm_version=$(pnpm -v 2>/dev/null || echo "none")
  log "INFO" "Detected Node.js: $node_version, pnpm: $pnpm_version"
  if [[ "$node_version" = "none" || "$pnpm_version" = "none" ]]; then
    log "ERROR" "Node.js or pnpm not installed. Install Node.js >= $REQUIRED_NODE_VERSION and pnpm >= $REQUIRED_PNPM_VERSION."
    return 1
  fi
  if ! version_ge "${node_version#v}" "$REQUIRED_NODE_VERSION"; then
    log "ERROR" "Node.js version ${node_version#v} is below required $REQUIRED_NODE_VERSION"
    return 1
  fi
  if ! version_ge "$pnpm_version" "$REQUIRED_PNPM_VERSION"; then
    log "ERROR" "pnpm version $pnpm_version is below required $REQUIRED_PNPM_VERSION"
    return 1
  fi
  if ! command -v docker >/dev/null 2>&1; then
    log "WARNING" "Docker not installed. Docker steps may fail."
  fi
  log "SUCCESS" "Version requirements met"
}

# Load environment variables from .env file
load_env_file() {
  log "INFO" "Loading environment variables"
  if [ -f "$ENV_PATH" ]; then
    log "INFO" "Found $ENV_PATH"
    set -a
    # shellcheck source=/dev/null
    source "$ENV_PATH"
    set +a
    for var in "${REQUIRED_ENV_VARS[@]}"; do
      if [ -z "${!var:-}" ]; then
        log "ERROR" "Required environment variable $var not set"
        return 1
      fi
    done
    log "SUCCESS" "Environment variables loaded"
  else
    log "WARNING" "$ENV_PATH not found. Some features may not work."
  fi
}

# Clean caches and node_modules
clean_caches() {
  log "INFO" "Cleaning caches and node_modules"
  for dir in "${PROJECT_DIRS[@]}"; do
    local node_modules="$dir/node_modules"
    local cache="$dir/.cache"
    if [ -d "$node_modules" ]; then
      run_cmd rm -rf "$node_modules"
      log "INFO" "Removed $node_modules"
    fi
    if [ -d "$cache" ]; then
      run_cmd rm -rf "$cache"
      log "INFO" "Removed $cache"
    fi
  done
  run_cmd pnpm store prune || log "WARNING" "pnpm store prune failed, continuing"
  log "SUCCESS" "Cache cleanup completed"
}

# Install dependencies with pnpm
install_dependencies() {
  log "INFO" "Installing dependencies"
  if ! run_cmd pnpm install --prefer-offline; then
    log "ERROR" "pnpm install failed"
    check_experience_db "install_failed" "pnpm"
    return 1
  fi
  log "SUCCESS" "Dependencies installed"
}

# Build all projects in monorepo
build_all() {
  log "INFO" "Building all projects"
  for project in "${PROJECT_DIRS[@]}"; do
    log "INFO" "Building $project"
    if ! run_cmd pnpm --filter "./$project" build; then
      log "ERROR" "Build failed for $project"
      check_experience_db "build_failed" "$project"
      return 1
    fi
    log "SUCCESS" "Build succeeded for $project"
  done
  log "SUCCESS" "All projects built"
}

# Start Docker containers
docker_all() {
  log "INFO" "Starting Docker services"
  if ! command -v docker >/dev/null 2>&1; then
    log "ERROR" "Docker not installed. Skipping Docker steps."
    return 1
  fi
  if ! docker info >/dev/null 2>&1; then
    log "ERROR" "Docker daemon not running. Start Docker and retry."
    return 1
  fi
  for compose_file in "${COMPOSE_FILES[@]}"; do
    if [ ! -f "$compose_file" ]; then
      log "ERROR" "Docker compose file $compose_file not found"
      return 1
    fi
    if ! run_cmd docker-compose -f "$compose_file" up -d; then
      log "ERROR" "Failed to start Docker with $compose_file"
      check_experience_db "docker_failed" "$compose_file"
      return 1
    fi
    log "SUCCESS" "Docker started with $compose_file"
  done
  log "SUCCESS" "Docker services started"
}

# Check GitHub repository status
check_git_status() {
  if [ "$CHECK_GIT" = true ]; then
    log "INFO" "Checking GitHub repository status"
    if [ -d ".git" ]; then
      local git_status git_log git_branch
      git_status=$(git status --porcelain 2>/dev/null)
      git_branch=$(git rev-parse --abbrev-ref HEAD 2>/dev/null || echo "unknown")
      git_log=$(git log -1 --pretty=format:"%h - %s (%an, %ad)" 2>/dev/null || echo "none")
      log "INFO" "Current branch: $git_branch"
      log "INFO" "Latest commit: $git_log"
      if [ -n "$git_status" ]; then
        log "WARNING" "Uncommitted changes detected:"
        echo "$git_status" | tee -a "$LOG_FILE"
      else
        log "SUCCESS" "No uncommitted changes"
      fi
      if git remote -v | grep -q origin; then
        log "INFO" "Checking for unpushed commits"
        if git log "origin/$git_branch..HEAD" --oneline | grep -q .; then
          log "WARNING" "Unpushed commits detected. Consider: git push"
        else
          log "SUCCESS" "No unpushed commits"
        fi
      else
        log "WARNING" "No remote repository configured"
      fi
    else
      log "WARNING" "Not a git repository"
    fi
  else
    log "INFO" "Skipping GitHub status check (use --check-git to enable)"
  fi
}

# Generate summary for collaboration
generate_summary() {
  local elapsed="$1"
  local status="success"
  if [ ${#FAILED_STEPS[@]} -gt 0 ]; then
    status="failed"
  fi
  log "INFO" "Generating summary"
  {
    echo "Setup Summary ($(timestamp))"
    echo "Status: $status"
    echo "Elapsed Time: $elapsed seconds"
    echo "Successful Steps: ${SUCCESSFUL_STEPS[*]:-None}"
    echo "Failed Steps: ${FAILED_STEPS[*]:-None}"
    if [ ${#DEPRECATED_DEPS[@]} -gt 0 ]; then
      echo "Deprecated Dependencies: ${DEPRECATED_DEPS[*]}"
    fi
    echo ""
    echo "Output Files:"
    echo "- Log: $LOG_FILE"
    echo "- State: $STATE_FILE"
    echo "- Summary: $SUMMARY_FILE"
    echo "- Troubleshooting Guide: $TROUBLESHOOTING_GUIDE"
    echo "- Experience Database: $EXPERIENCE_DB"
    echo ""
    echo "Next Steps:"
    if [ "$status" = "failed" ]; then
      echo "- Review $LOG_FILE and $TROUBLESHOOTING_GUIDE"
      echo "- Retry with: ./setup-and-run.sh --verbose --resume"
    else
      echo "- Start development: pnpm --filter src/frontend dev"
      echo "- Monitor Docker: docker ps"
      echo "- Share progress via GitHub"
    fi
  } | tee "$SUMMARY_FILE"
  cat "$SUMMARY_FILE" >&2
}

# === MAIN EXECUTION ===
main() {
  # Parse command-line arguments
  while [[ $# -gt 0 ]]; do
    case "$1" in
      --verbose) VERBOSE=true; shift ;;
      --debug) DEBUG=true; VERBOSE=true; shift ;;
      --dry-run) DRY_RUN=true; shift ;;
      --resume) RESUME=true; shift ;;
      --no-parallel) NO_PARALLEL=true; shift ;;
      --check-git) CHECK_GIT=true; shift ;;
      --timeout=*) TIMEOUT="${1#*=}"; shift ;;
      --help)
        echo "Usage: ./setup-and-run.sh [options]"
        echo "Options:"
        echo "  --verbose       Show detailed logs"
        echo "  --debug         Enable debug mode (implies --verbose)"
        echo "  --dry-run       Simulate execution without changes"
        echo "  --resume        Resume from last failed step"
        echo "  --no-parallel   Disable parallel execution"
        echo "  --check-git     Check GitHub repository status"
        echo "  --timeout=<sec> Set command timeout (default: 600)"
        exit 0
        ;;
      *) log "WARNING" "Unknown argument: $1"; shift ;;
    esac
  done

  # Initialize script
  log "INFO" "=== Setup Script Started ==="
  local start_time=$(date +%s)

  # Check for jq
  if ! command -v jq >/dev/null 2>&1; then
    log "WARNING" "jq not installed. State and experience database functionality limited. Install with: sudo apt-get install jq"
  fi

  # Load state if resuming
  if [ "$RESUME" = true ] && [ -f "$STATE_FILE" ] && command -v jq >/dev/null 2>&1; then
    log "INFO" "Loading state from $STATE_FILE"
    while IFS=':' read -r key value; do
      key=$(echo "$key" | tr -d ' "')
      value=$(echo "$value" | tr -d ' ",\n')
      STATE["$key"]="$value"
    done < <(jq -r 'to_entries[] | "\(.key):\(.value)"' "$STATE_FILE")
  fi

  # Define execution steps
  STEPS=(
    check_versions
    load_env_file
    clean_caches
    install_dependencies
    build_all
    docker_all
    check_git_status
  )

  # Execute steps with state tracking
  for step in "${STEPS[@]}"; do
    if [ "${STATE[$step]}" != "success" ] || [ "$step" = "check_git_status" ]; then
      log "INFO" "Executing step: $step"
      if ! "$step"; then
        log "ERROR" "Step $step failed"
        FAILED_STEPS+=("$step")
        update_state "$step" "failed"
        generate_troubleshooting_guide
        generate_summary "$(( $(date +%s) - start_time ))"
        exit 1
      fi
      SUCCESSFUL_STEPS+=("$step")
      update_state "$step" "success"
    else
      log "INFO" "Skipping step: $step (already successful)"
    fi
  done

  # Finalize execution
  local end_time=$(date +%s)
  local elapsed=$((end_time - start_time))
  generate_summary "$elapsed"
  log "SUCCESS" "Setup completed in ${elapsed} seconds"
  exit 0
}

# Trap interruptions to save state and generate summary
trap 'log "ERROR" "Script interrupted"; generate_summary "$(( $(date +%s) - start_time ))"; exit 1' INT TERM

# Start the script
main "$@"

Summary of What the Script Does
This script automates the setup and execution of a monorepo project (e.g., Quran-recitation-mvp) with frontend, backend, and shared components, using tools like pnpm, TypeScript, Vite, and Docker. It performs the following tasks:
Version Checks: Verifies Node.js (>= 18.0.0), pnpm (>= 8.0.0), and Docker installations.

Environment Setup: Loads variables from config/.env, ensuring required variables (e.g., GOOGLE_APPLICATION_CREDENTIALS) are set.

Cache Cleaning: Removes node_modules and project caches, prunes pnpm store.

Dependency Installation: Installs dependencies using pnpm install --prefer-offline for offline support.

Project Building: Builds src/shared, src/frontend, and src/backend in sequence using pnpm --filter.

Docker Services: Starts Docker containers using docker-compose files (docker-compose-databases.yml, docker-compose-dev.yml).

GitHub Status Check: Optionally (with --check-git) checks for uncommitted changes, unpushed commits, and logs the latest commit.

State Management: Tracks step progress in memory and state.json, allowing resumption with --resume.

Error Handling: Captures command failures, logs outputs, and records issues in experience.json with suggested resolutions.

Troubleshooting: Generates a guide (troubleshooting_guide.txt) with fixes for common issues (e.g., TypeScript configs, Vite aliases).

Summary Generation: Produces a summary (summary.json and terminal output) of status, steps, and output file paths.

The script supports collaboration by:
Producing detailed logs and structured outputs (JSON files) for sharing via GitHub.

Providing clear terminal feedback for real-time progress.

Including troubleshooting tips for VS Code development (e.g., TypeScript paths, Vite aliases).

Enabling Grok and Jules to analyze logs and errors for further assistance.

Summary of Outputs and Locations
Output Files and Their Locations
All outputs are stored in the collaboration/logs/ directory within the repository root (e.g., C:\Users\rehan\OneDrive\Desktop\github_repos\Quran-recitation-mvp\collaboration\logs\).
setup.log
Content: Detailed log of all script actions, including INFO, SUCCESS, ERROR, WARNING, and DEBUG messages with timestamps and emojis.

Purpose: Records every step, command output, and error for debugging and collaboration.

Example Path: collaboration/logs/setup.log

state.json
Content: JSON object mapping each step (e.g., check_versions) to its status (success or failed).

Purpose: Tracks progress to enable resumption with --resume.

Example Content:
json

{
  "check_versions": "success",
  "load_env_file": "success",
  "install_dependencies": "failed"
}

Example Path: collaboration/logs/state.json

summary.json
Content: Summary of script execution, including status, elapsed time, successful/failed steps, deprecated dependencies (if any), output file paths, and next steps.

Purpose: Provides a quick overview for collaborators, shareable via GitHub.

Example Content:
json

Setup Summary (2025-06-20 08:17:00)
Status: success
Elapsed Time: 120 seconds
Successful Steps: check_versions load_env_file clean_caches install_dependencies build_all docker_all check_git_status
Failed Steps: None
Output Files:
- Log: collaboration/logs/setup.log
- State: collaboration/logs/state.json
- Summary: collaboration/logs/summary.json
- Troubleshooting Guide: collaboration/logs/troubleshooting_guide.txt
- Experience Database: collaboration/logs/experience.json
Next Steps:
- Start development: pnpm --filter src/frontend dev
- Monitor Docker: docker ps
- Share progress via GitHub

Example Path: collaboration/logs/summary.json

troubleshooting_guide.txt
Content: Actionable fixes for common issues, such as workspace configuration, TypeScript settings, Vite aliases, Docker problems, and GitHub collaboration tips.

Purpose: Assists developers, Grok, and Jules in resolving errors, especially during VS Code development.

Example Path: collaboration/logs/troubleshooting_guide.txt

experience.json
Content: JSON array of error records, each with type (e.g., command_failed), context, output, resolution, timestamp, and success rate.

Purpose: Stores known issues and fixes for automated recovery and sharing with collaborators.

Example Content:
json

[
  {
    "type": "command_failed",
    "context": "pnpm install",
    "output": "ERR_PNPM_NO_OFFLINE...",
    "resolution": "Run: pnpm install --no-offline",
    "timestamp": "2025-06-20 08:15:00",
    "success_rate": "0"
  }
]

Example Path: collaboration/logs/experience.json

Terminal Output
Real-Time Progress: Displays INFO, SUCCESS, ERROR, and WARNING messages during execution, with timestamps and emojis (e.g., 2025-06-20 08:15:00  [INFO] Installing dependencies...).

Final Summary: At completion or failure, prints the same content as summary.json to the terminal, including status, steps, output file paths, and next steps.

Example Terminal Output:

...

Status: success

Output Files:

- State: C:\Users\rehan\OneDrive\Desktop\github_repos\Quran-recitation-mvp\collaboration\logs\state.json

- Monitor Docker: docker ps
