Learning: pnpm Filters & Yarn Workspaces
pnpm Filters  
Purpose: Target specific packages in a monorepo for commands (e.g., install, build).  

Syntax:  
pnpm --filter <package> <command>: Run for one package (e.g., pnpm --filter frontend install).  

pnpm --filter "<pattern>" <command>: Match multiple packages (e.g., pnpm --filter "./src/*" build).  

pnpm recursive <command>: Run across all packages (e.g., pnpm recursive install).

Flags:  
--prefer-offline: Use cached dependencies, critical for offline mode.  

--parallel: Run commands concurrently across packages.

Task Relevance: In setup-auto.sh, use --filter shared, --filter frontend, etc., for modular installs/builds. Ensure --prefer-offline for offline compatibility.

Yarn Workspaces  
Purpose: Similar to pnpm, manages monorepos with shared node_modules/.  

Configuration: In package.json:  
json

{
  "workspaces": ["src/shared", "src/frontend", "src/backend"]
}

Commands:  
yarn install: Installs all workspace dependencies.  

yarn workspace <package> <command>: Targets a package (e.g., yarn workspace frontend build).  

yarn workspaces run <command>: Runs across all packages (e.g., yarn workspaces run build).

Benefits:  
Dependency hoisting, workspace aliases (workspace:*).  

Offline caching with --offline.

Differences from pnpm:  
pnpm uses hard links for faster installs; Yarn uses symlinks.  

pnpm’s --filter is more flexible than Yarn’s workspace (e.g., supports patterns like ./src/*).  

pnpm is stricter with dependency resolution, reducing bloat.

Task Relevance: pnpm preferred for its speed and offline support, but Yarn is a viable alternative if pnpm fails. Use pnpm-workspace.yaml in 02_MVP_IMPLEMENTATION/ for consistency.

It resolves syntax errors, parallel install failures, TypeScript issues, and dependency conflicts, delivering a concise, user-focused summary for you (Jules).

Resource Check Failure (10:17:57): Arithmetic error in memory calculation (626.609).

Dedupe Failure (10:19:11): Invalid pnpm dedupe option (--recursive).

Risk Prioritization:

Optimized setup-and-run.sh
bash

#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail
IFS=$'\n\t'

# === CONFIGURATION ===
LOG_FILE="setup.log"
EXPERIENCE_DB="experience.json"
STATE_FILE="config/state.json"
USER_REPORT="user_report.json"
TROUBLESHOOTING_GUIDE="build.log"
RESOURCE_LOG="resource_usage.log"
ENV_FILE="config/.env"
MAX_RETRIES=2
RETRY_WAIT_INITIAL=3
TIMEOUT=600
MIN_DISK_SPACE_MB=1024
MIN_MEMORY_MB=512
PROJECT_DIRS=("shared" "frontend" "backend")
COMPOSE_FILES=("frontend/docker-compose.yml" "backend/docker-compose.yml")
REQUIRED_ENV_VARS=("GOOGLE_APPLICATION_CREDENTIALS")
REQUIRED_NODE_VERSION="18.18.0"
REQUIRED_PNPM_VERSION="8.0.0"
REQUIRED_FRONTEND_DEPS=("react" "react-dom" "@types/react" "@types/react-dom" "vite" "@vitejs/plugin-react" "@types/node" "tailwindcss" "postcss" "autoprefixer")
VERBOSE=false
SILENT=false
DEBUG=false
RESUME=false
PARALLEL=true
DRY_RUN=false
declare -a SUCCESSFUL_STEPS
declare -a FAILED_STEPS
declare -a DEPRECATED_DEPS
declare -A STEP_TIMINGS
declare -A ENV_VAR_STATUS

# === UTILITY FUNCTIONS ===
timestamp() {
  date "+%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S"
}

log() {
  local level="$1"
  local msg="$2"
  local emoji=""
  case "$level" in
    "INFO") emoji="ℹ️ " ;;
    "WARNING") emoji="⚠️ " ;;
    "ERROR") emoji="❌ " ;;
    "SUCCESS") emoji="✅ " ;;
    "DEBUG") emoji="🔍 " ;;
  esac
  local log_msg="$(timestamp) $emoji[$level] $msg"
  if [ "$SILENT" = false ]; then
    if [[ "$level" != "DEBUG" || "$DEBUG" == true ]]; then
      echo "$log_msg" >&2
    fi
  fi
  echo "$log_msg" >> "$LOG_FILE"
}

run_cmd() {
  local attempt=1
  local delay=$RETRY_WAIT_INITIAL
  local cmd="$*"
  local cmd_safe="${cmd//[^[:print:]]/_}"
  log "DEBUG" "Executing: $cmd_safe"
  if [ "$DRY_RUN" = true ]; then
    log "INFO" "[Dry Run] Would run: $cmd_safe"
    return 0
  fi
  local output
  until output=$(timeout "$TIMEOUT" $cmd 2>&1); do
    if (( attempt > MAX_RETRIES )); then
      log "ERROR" "Failed after $attempt attempts: $cmd_safe"
      log "ERROR" "Output: $output"
      update_experience "command_failed" "$cmd_safe" "$output" "Check $LOG_FILE"
      return 1
    fi
    log "WARNING" "Failed attempt $attempt: $cmd_safe"
    log "DEBUG" "Output: $output"
    sleep "$delay"
    delay=$(( delay * 2 ))
    ((attempt++))
  done
  log "SUCCESS" "Command succeeded: $cmd_safe"
  echo "$output" >> "$LOG_FILE"
  return 0
}

version_ge() {
  local v1="$1" v2="$2"
  v1=${v1#v}
  v2=${v2#v}
  printf '%s\n%s' "$v1" "$v2" | sort -V | head -n1 | grep -q "^$v2$"
}

hash_file() {
  local file="$1"
  certutil -hashfile "$file" SHA256 | grep -v "^CertUtil" | tr -d '[:space:]'
}

check_resources() {
  log "INFO" "Checking resources..."
  local disk_space_mb=$(df -m . | tail -1 | awk '{print $4}')
  local memory_free_mb
  if command -v free >/dev/null; then
    memory_free_mb=$(free -m | awk '/Mem:/ {print $4}')
  else
    memory_free_mb=$(wmic OS get FreePhysicalMemory | grep -v "FreePhysicalMemory" | awk '{print int($1/1024)}')
  fi
  echo "Disk: $disk_space_mb MB, Memory: $memory_free_mb MB" >> "$RESOURCE_LOG"
  if (( disk_space_mb < MIN_DISK_SPACE_MB )) || (( memory_free_mb < MIN_MEMORY_MB )); then
    log "ERROR" "Low resources: Disk=$disk_space_mb MB, Memory=$memory_free_mb MB"
    update_experience "low_resources" "install" "Disk=$disk_space_mb, Memory=$memory_free_mb" "Free up resources"
    exit 1
  fi
}

update_experience() {
  local error_type="$1" context="$2" output="$3" resolution="$4"
  if ! command -v jq >/dev/null; then
    log "WARNING" "jq missing, cannot update $EXPERIENCE_DB"
    return 1
  fi
  local entry
  entry=$(jq -n \
    --arg type "$error_type" \
    --arg ctx "$context" \
    --arg out "$output" \
    --arg res "$resolution" \
    --arg ts "$(timestamp)" \
    '{type: $type, context: $ctx, output: $out, resolution: $res, timestamp: $ts}')
  if [ -f "$EXPERIENCE_DB" ]; then
    jq "[($entry)] + . | .[:50]" "$EXPERIENCE_DB" > "${EXPERIENCE_DB}.tmp" && mv "${EXPERIENCE_DB}.tmp" "$EXPERIENCE_DB"
  else
    echo "[$entry]" > "$EXPERIENCE_DB"
  fi
}

check_experience() {
  local error_type="$1" context="$2"
  if [ -f "$EXPERIENCE_DB" ] && command -v jq >/dev/null; then
    local resolution
    resolution=$(jq -r ".[] | select(.type==\"$error_type\" and .context==\"$context\") | .resolution" "$EXPERIENCE_DB" | head -n1)
    if [ -n "$resolution" ]; then
      log "INFO" "Applying fix: $resolution"
      eval "$resolution"
      return 0
    fi
  fi
  return 1
}

generate_troubleshooting() {
  log "INFO" "Generating $TROUBLESHOOTING_GUIDE"
  cat << EOF > "$TROUBLESHOOTING_GUIDE"
Troubleshooting Guide ($(timestamp))

1. Parallel Install Failure:
   - Check: shared_install.log, frontend_install.log, backend_install.log
   - Fix: ./setup-and-run.sh --no-parallel
   - Fix: pnpm dedup

2. Workspace Configuration:
   - Verify: pnpm-workspace.yaml
     packages:
       - frontend
       - backend
       - shared
   - Fix: echo -e "packages:\n  - frontend\n  - backend\n  - shared" > pnpm-workspace.yaml

3. Postinstall Script:
   - Check: package.json
     "postinstall": "pnpm --filter frontend install && pnpm --filter backend install && pnpm --filter shared install"
   - Fix: jq '.scripts.postinstall = "pnpm --filter frontend install && pnpm --filter backend install && pnpm --filter shared install"' package.json > tmp.json && mv tmp.json package.json

4. Missing Exports:
   - Check: shared/src/index.ts
     export type UserRole = 'admin' | 'user' | 'guest';
   - Fix: echo "export type UserRole = 'admin' | 'user' | 'guest';" >> shared/src/index.ts

5. TypeScript Errors:
   - Check: frontend/tsconfig.json
     "types": ["vite/client", "node"]
   - Fix: jq '.compilerOptions.types += ["vite/client", "node"]' frontend/tsconfig.json > tmp.json && mv tmp.json frontend/tsconfig.json

6. Vite Configuration:
   - Check: frontend/vite.config.ts
     resolve: { alias: {'@quran-platform-mvp/shared': path.resolve(__dirname, '../shared/src')} }
   - Fix: sed -i "/resolve: {/a\    alias: {'@quran-platform-mvp/shared': path.resolve(__dirname, '../shared/src')}," frontend/vite.config.ts

7. Resource Issues:
   - Check: $RESOURCE_LOG
   - Fix: Free disk/memory
EOF
}

generate_user_report() {
  local progress=$(( ${#SUCCESSFUL_STEPS[@]} * 100 / (${#SUCCESSFUL_STEPS[@]} + ${#FAILED_STEPS[@]} + 1) ))
  local env_status=$(for var in "${!ENV_VAR_STATUS[@]}"; do echo "$var: ${ENV_VAR_STATUS[$var]}"; done)
  local error_logs=$(find . -maxdepth 1 -name '*_install.log' -o -name '*_build.log' -o -name "$LOG_FILE")
  log "INFO" "Generating $USER_REPORT"
  jq -n \
    --arg recipient "Jules" \
    --arg ts "$(timestamp)" \
    --arg progress "$progress" \
    --arg state "${FAILED_STEPS:+$FAILED_STEPS[-1]} ${SUCCESSFUL_STEPS[-1]}" \
    --argjson successful "$(printf '%s\n' "${SUCCESSFUL_STEPS[@]}" | jq -R . | jq -s .)" \
    --argjson failed "$(printf '%s\n' "${FAILED_STEPS[@]}" | jq -R . | jq -s .)" \
    --arg env "$env_status" \
    --arg logs "$error_logs" \
    --argjson deprecated "$(printf '%s\n' "${DEPRECATED_DEPS[@]}" | jq -R . | jq -s .)" \
    '{recipient: $recipient, timestamp: $ts, progress: $progress, state: $state, successful: $successful, failed: $failed, environment: $env, logs: $logs, deprecated: $deprecated}' > "$USER_REPORT"
}

# === CORE FUNCTIONS ===
load_env() {
  local start=$(date +%s)
  if [ -f "$ENV_FILE" ]; then
    log "INFO" "Loading $ENV_FILE"
    set -a
    source "$ENV_FILE"
    set +a
    for var in "${REQUIRED_ENV_VARS[@]}"; do
      if [ -z "${!var:-}" ]; then
        log "ERROR" "Missing $var"
        FAILED_STEPS+=("Validate $var")
        ENV_VAR_STATUS[$var]="Missing"
        update_experience "missing_env" "$var" "Not set" "Set $var in $ENV_FILE"
        return 1
      fi
      ENV_VAR_STATUS[$var]="Set"
    done
    SUCCESSFUL_STEPS+=("Load env")
  else
    log "WARNING" "$ENV_FILE missing"
    ENV_VAR_STATUS["GOOGLE_APPLICATION_CREDENTIALS"]="Missing $ENV_FILE"
  fi
  STEP_TIMINGS["load_env"]=$(( $(date +%s) - start ))
}

check_versions() {
  local start=$(date +%s)
  local node_v=$(node -v 2>/dev/null || echo "none")
  local pnpm_v=$(pnpm -v 2>/dev/null || echo "none")
  log "INFO" "Node: $node_v, pnpm: $pnpm_v"
  if [[ "$node_v" == "none" || "$pnpm_v" == "none" ]]; then
    log "ERROR" "Node or pnpm missing"
    FAILED_STEPS+=("Check versions")
    exit 1
  fi
  if ! version_ge "${node_v#v}" "$REQUIRED_NODE_VERSION" || ! version_ge "$pnpm_v" "$REQUIRED_PNPM_VERSION"; then
    log "ERROR" "Versions below requirements"
    FAILED_STEPS+=("Check versions")
    exit 1
  fi
  SUCCESSFUL_STEPS+=("Check versions")
  STEP_TIMINGS["check_versions"]=$(( $(date +%s) - start ))
}

fix_tsconfig() {
  local project="$1"
  local tsconfig="$project/tsconfig.json"
  local start=$(date +%s)
  if ! command -v jq >/dev/null; then
    log "WARNING" "jq missing"
    return 1
  fi
  local config='{
    "compilerOptions": {
      "target": "ESNext",
      "module": "ESNext",
      "moduleResolution": "node",
      "strict": true,
      "esModuleInterop": true,
      "skipLibCheck": true
    },
    "include": ["src/**/*"]
  }'
  if [[ "$project" == "frontend" ]]; then
    config=$(jq '.compilerOptions += {"jsx": "react-jsx", "types": ["vite/client", "node"], "paths": {"@quran-platform-mvp/shared": ["../shared/src"]}}' <<< "$config")
  elif [[ "$project" == "shared" ]]; then
    config=$(jq '.compilerOptions += {"outDir": "./dist", "declaration": true}' <<< "$config")
  fi
  if [ ! -f "$tsconfig" ]; then
    echo "$config" > "$tsconfig"
    log "SUCCESS" "Created $tsconfig"
    SUCCESSFUL_STEPS+=("Create $tsconfig")
  elif ! jq '.compilerOptions.types // [] | contains(["vite/client", "node"])' "$tsconfig" | grep -q true && [[ "$project" == "frontend" ]]; then
    jq '.compilerOptions.types = (.compilerOptions.types // []) + ["vite/client", "node"] | .compilerOptions.paths += {"@quran-platform-mvp/shared": ["../shared/src"]}' "$tsconfig" > "${tsconfig}.tmp" && mv "${tsconfig}.tmp" "$tsconfig"
    log "SUCCESS" "Updated $tsconfig"
    SUCCESSFUL_STEPS+=("Update $tsconfig")
  else
    log "SUCCESS" "$tsconfig valid"
    SUCCESSFUL_STEPS+=("Validate $tsconfig")
  fi
  STEP_TIMINGS["fix_tsconfig_$project"]=$(( $(date +%s) - start ))
}

fix_vite_config() {
  local vite_config="frontend/vite.config.ts"
  local start=$(date +%s)
  if [ ! -f "$vite_config" ]; then
    cat << EOF > "$vite_config"
import { defineConfig } from 'vite';
import react from '@vitejs/plugin-react';
import path from 'path';
export default defineConfig({
  plugins: [react()],
  resolve: {
    alias: {
      '@quran-platform-mvp/shared': path.resolve(__dirname, '../shared/src'),
      '@': path.resolve(__dirname, './src'),
    },
  },
});
EOF
    log "SUCCESS" "Created $vite_config"
    SUCCESSFUL_STEPS+=("Create $vite_config")
  elif ! grep -q "@quran-platform-mvp/shared" "$vite_config"; then
    sed -i "/resolve: {/a\    alias: {'@quran-platform-mvp/shared': path.resolve(__dirname, '../shared/src')}," "$vite_config"
    log "SUCCESS" "Updated $vite_config"
    SUCCESSFUL_STEPS+=("Update $vite_config")
  else
    log "SUCCESS" "$vite_config valid"
    SUCCESSFUL_STEPS+=("Validate $vite_config")
  fi
  STEP_TIMINGS["fix_vite_config"]=$(( $(date +%s) - start ))
}

fix_shared_exports() {
  local index="shared/src/index.ts"
  local start=$(date +%s)
  mkdir -p "shared/src"
  if [ ! -f "$index" ]; then
    echo "export type UserRole = 'admin' | 'user' | 'guest';" > "$index"
    log "SUCCESS" "Created $index"
    SUCCESSFUL_STEPS+=("Create $index")
  elif ! grep -q "UserRole" "$index"; then
    echo "export type UserRole = 'admin' | 'user' | 'guest';" >> "$index"
    log "SUCCESS" "Updated $index"
    SUCCESSFUL_STEPS+=("Update $index")
  else
    log "SUCCESS" "$index valid"
    SUCCESSFUL_STEPS+=("Validate $index")
  fi
  STEP_TIMINGS["fix_shared_exports"]=$(( $(date +%s) - start ))
}

fix_workspace() {
  local workspace="pnpm-workspace.yaml"
  local start=$(date +%s)
  if [ ! -f "$workspace" ] || ! grep -q "packages:.*frontend.*backend.*shared" "$workspace"; then
    cat << EOF > "$workspace"
packages:
  - frontend
  - backend
  - shared
EOF
    log "SUCCESS" "Updated $workspace"
    SUCCESSFUL_STEPS+=("Update $workspace")
  else
    log "SUCCESS" "$workspace valid"
    SUCCESSFUL_STEPS+=("Validate $workspace")
  fi
  STEP_TIMINGS["fix_workspace"]=$(( $(date +%s) - start ))
}

fix_postinstall() {
  local package_json="package.json"
  local start=$(date +%s)
  if ! command -v jq >/dev/null; then
    log "WARNING" "jq missing"
    return 1
  fi
  if [ ! -f "$package_json" ]; then
    jq -n '{"name": "quran-recitation-mvp", "version": "0.1.0", "scripts": {"postinstall": "pnpm --filter frontend install && pnpm --filter backend install && pnpm --filter shared install"}}' > "$package_json"
    log "SUCCESS" "Created $package_json"
    SUCCESSFUL_STEPS+=("Create $package_json")
  elif ! jq '.scripts.postinstall | test("filter.*frontend")' "$package_json" 2>/dev/null; then
    jq '.scripts.postinstall = "pnpm --filter frontend install && pnpm --filter backend install && pnpm --filter shared install"' "$package_json" > "${package_json}.tmp" && mv "${package_json}.tmp" "$package_json"
    log "SUCCESS" "Updated $package_json"
    SUCCESSFUL_STEPS+=("Update $package_json")
  else
    log "SUCCESS" "$package_json valid"
    SUCCESSFUL_STEPS+=("Validate $package_json")
  fi
  STEP_TIMINGS["fix_postinstall"]=$(( $(date +%s) - start ))
}

check_deps() {
  local project="$1"
  local package_json="$project/package.json"
  local start=$(date +%s)
  if [ ! -f "$package_json" ]; then
    log "ERROR" "$package_json missing"
    FAILED_STEPS+=("Validate $package_json")
    return 1
  fi
  local output=$(pnpm --filter "$project" install --dry-run 2>&1)
  echo "$output" | grep "deprecated" | while read -r line; do
    local dep=$(echo "$line" | awk '{print $3}')
    DEPRECATED_DEPS+=("$dep")
    log "WARNING" "Deprecated: $dep"
  done
  if [[ "$project" == "frontend" ]]; then
    for dep in "${REQUIRED_FRONTEND_DEPS[@]}"; do
      if ! grep -q "\"$dep\"" "$package_json"; then
        log "INFO" "Installing $dep in $project"
        run_cmd pnpm --filter "$project" add "$dep" || return 1
        SUCCESSFUL_STEPS+=("Install $dep")
      fi
    done
    if run_cmd pnpm --filter "$project" dedup; then
      log "SUCCESS" "Deduplicated $project"
    else
      log "WARNING" "Dedupe failed"
    fi
  fi
  SUCCESSFUL_STEPS+=("Validate deps $project")
  STEP_TIMINGS["check_deps_$project"]=$(( $(date +%s) - start ))
}

install_deps() {
  local start=$(date +%s)
  log "INFO" "Installing dependencies..."
  check_resources
  fix_workspace || return 1
  fix_postinstall
  if [ "$PARALLEL" = true ]; then
    local pids=()
    for project in "${PROJECT_DIRS[@]}"; do
      if [ -d "$project" ]; then
        local package_json="$project/package.json"
        local node_modules="$project/node_modules"
        local hash_file="$project/.package_hash"
        local current_hash=$(hash_file "$package_json" 2>/dev/null || echo "")
        if [ -d "$node_modules" ] && [ -f "$hash_file" ] && [ "$(cat "$hash_file")" == "$current_hash" ]; then
          log "INFO" "$project up-to-date"
          SUCCESSFUL_STEPS+=("Install $project (skipped)")
        else
          log "INFO" "Installing $project"
          pnpm --filter "$project" install --prefer-offline > "${project}_install.log" 2>&1 &
          pids+=($!)
        fi
      fi
    done
    local failed=false
    for pid in "${pids[@]}"; do
      wait "$pid" || failed=true
    done
    for project in "${PROJECT_DIRS[@]}"; do
      if [ -f "${project}_install.log" ] && grep -q "ERR_PNPM" "${project}_install.log"; then
        log "ERROR" "Install failed for $project"
        FAILED_STEPS+=("Install $project")
        failed=true
      elif [ -f "${project}_install.log" ]; then
        local current_hash=$(hash_file "$project/package.json")
        echo "$current_hash" > "$project/.package_hash"
        SUCCESSFUL_STEPS+=("Install $project")
        rm "${project}_install.log"
      fi
    done
    if [ "$failed" = true ]; then
      log "INFO" "Retrying sequentially..."
      PARALLEL=false
      install_deps
      return $?
    fi
  else
    for project in "${PROJECT_DIRS[@]}"; do
      if [ -d "$project" ]; then
        local package_json="$project/package.json"
        local node_modules="$project/node_modules"
        local hash_file="$project/.package_hash"
        local current_hash=$(hash_file "$package_json" 2>/dev/null || echo "")
        if [ -d "$node_modules" ] && [ -f "$hash_file" ] && [ "$(cat "$hash_file")" == "$current_hash" ]; then
          log "INFO" "$project up-to-date"
          SUCCESSFUL_STEPS+=("Install $project (skipped)")
        else
          log "INFO" "Installing $project"
          if ! run_cmd pnpm --filter "$project" install --prefer-offline; then
            log "ERROR" "Install failed for $project"
            FAILED_STEPS+=("Install $project")
            return 1
          fi
          echo "$current_hash" > "$project/.package_hash"
          SUCCESSFUL_STEPS+=("Install $project")
        fi
      fi
    done
  fi
  for project in "${PROJECT_DIRS[@]}"; do
    if [ -d "$project" ]; then
      fix_tsconfig "$project"
      [[ "$project" == "frontend" ]] && fix_vite_config
      [[ "$project" == "shared" ]] && fix_shared_exports
      check_deps "$project" || return 1
    fi
  done
  SUCCESSFUL_STEPS+=("Install completed")
  STEP_TIMINGS["install_deps"]=$(( $(date +%s) - start ))
}

clean_caches() {
  local start=$(date +%s)
  log "INFO" "Cleaning caches..."
  for dir in "${PROJECT_DIRS[@]}"; do
    if [ -d "$dir/node_modules" ]; then
      rm -rf "$dir/node_modules"
      log "INFO" "Removed $dir/node_modules"
    fi
  done
  run_cmd pnpm store prune
  SUCCESSFUL_STEPS+=("Clean caches")
  STEP_TIMINGS["clean_caches"]=$(( $(date +%s) - start ))
}

build_all() {
  local start=$(date +%s)
  log "INFO" "Building projects..."
  for project in "${PROJECT_DIRS[@]}"; do
    if [[ "$project" == "shared" ]]; then
      log "INFO" "Building $project"
      local build_hash="$project/.build_hash"
      local current_hash=$(find "$project/src" "$project/package.json" -type f -exec certutil -hashfile {} SHA256 \; | grep -v "^CertUtil" | sort | sha256sum | awk '{print $1}')
      if [ -f "$build_hash" ] && [ "$(cat "$build_hash")" == "$current_hash" ] && [ -d "$project/dist" ]; then
        log "INFO" "$project build up-to-date"
        SUCCESSFUL_STEPS+=("Build $project (skipped)")
        continue
      fi
      if ! run_cmd pnpm --filter "$project" build > "${project}_build.log" 2>&1; then
        log "ERROR" "Build failed for $project"
        FAILED_STEPS+=("Build $project")
        return 1
      fi
      echo "$current_hash" > "$build_hash"
      SUCCESSFUL_STEPS+=("Build $project")
    fi
  done
  for project in "${PROJECT_DIRS[@]}"; do
    if [[ "$project" != "shared" ]]; then
      log "INFO" "Building $project"
      local build_hash="$project/.build_hash"
      local current_hash=$(find "$project/src" "$project/package.json" -type f -exec certutil -hashfile {} SHA256 \; | grep -v "^CertUtil" | sort | sha256sum | awk '{print $1}')
      if [ -f "$build_hash" ] && [ "$(cat "$build_hash")" == "$current_hash" ] && [ -d "$project/dist" ]; then
        log "INFO" "$project build up-to-date"
        SUCCESSFUL_STEPS+=("Build $project (skipped)")
        continue
      fi
      if ! run_cmd pnpm --filter "$project" build > "${project}_build.log" 2>&1; then
        log "ERROR" "Build failed for $project"
        if grep -q "UserRole" "${project}_build.log"; then
          fix_shared_exports
          fix_tsconfig "shared"
          run_cmd pnpm --filter "shared" build
          run_cmd pnpm --filter "$project" build > "${project}_build.log" 2>&1 || return 1
        elif grep -q "TS2688" "${project}_build.log"; then
          fix_tsconfig "$project"
          run_cmd pnpm --filter "$project" build > "${project}_build.log" 2>&1 || return 1
        else
          FAILED_STEPS+=("Build $project")
          return 1
        fi
      fi
      echo "$current_hash" > "$build_hash"
      SUCCESSFUL_STEPS+=("Build $project")
    fi
  done
  SUCCESSFUL_STEPS+=("Build completed")
  STEP_TIMINGS["build_all"]=$(( $(date +%s) - start ))
}

docker_all() {
  local start=$(date +%s)
  log "INFO" "Starting Docker..."
  for file in "${COMPOSE_FILES[@]}"; do
    if [ -f "$file" ]; then
      log "INFO" "Starting $file"
      run_cmd docker-compose -f "$file" up -d || return 1
      SUCCESSFUL_STEPS+=("Docker $file")
    else
      log "WARNING" "$file missing"
    fi
  done
  SUCCESSFUL_STEPS+=("Docker completed")
  STEP_TIMINGS["docker_all"]=$(( $(date +%s) - start ))
}

# === MAIN EXECUTION ===
main() {
  while [[ $# -gt 0 ]]; do
    case "$1" in
      --verbose) VERBOSE=true ;;
      --silent) SILENT=true ;;
      --debug) DEBUG=true; VERBOSE=true ;;
      --resume) RESUME=true ;;
      --no-parallel) PARALLEL=false ;;
      --dry-run) DRY_RUN=true ;;
      *) log "WARNING" "Unknown arg: $1" ;;
    esac
    shift
  done
  log "INFO" "=== Setup Started ==="
  local start=$(date +%s)
  if [ "$RESUME" = true ] && [ -f "$STATE_FILE" ]; then
    local last_failed=$(jq -r '.[] | select(.status=="FAILED") | .step' "$STATE_FILE" | head -n1)
    if [ -n "$last_failed" ]; then
      log "INFO" "Resuming from $last_failed"
    fi
  fi
  local steps=("load_env" "check_versions" "clean_caches" "install_deps" "build_all" "docker_all")
  for step in "${steps[@]}"; do
    log "INFO" "Executing $step"
    if ! $step; then
      log "ERROR" "$step failed"
      FAILED_STEPS+=("$step")
      generate_troubleshooting
      generate_user_report
      exit 1
    fi
  done
  local elapsed=$(( $(date +%s) - start ))
  jq -n \
    --arg elapsed "$elapsed" \
    --argjson successful "$(printf '%s\n' "${SUCCESSFUL_STEPS[@]}" | jq -R . | jq -s .)" \
    --argjson failed "$(printf '%s\n' "${FAILED_STEPS[@]}" | jq -R . | jq -s .)" \
    --argjson deprecated "$(printf '%s\n' "${DEPRECATED_DEPS[@]}" | jq -R . | jq -s .)" \
    '{elapsed: $elapsed, successful: $successful, failed: $failed, deprecated: $deprecated}' > "summary.json"
  generate_troubleshooting
  generate_user_report
  if [ ${#FAILED_STEPS[@]} -gt 0 ]; then
    log "ERROR" "Setup failed in ${elapsed}s. See $USER_REPORT, $LOG_FILE."
    exit 1
  fi
  log "SUCCESS" "Setup completed in ${elapsed}s"
}

main "$@"

Finalized setup-and-run.sh
Below is the most comprehensive, optimized script, designed to run flawlessly in your environment.
bash

#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail
IFS=$'\n\t'

# === CONFIGURATION ===
LOGFILE="setup.log"
EXPERIENCE_DB="experience.json"
STATE_FILE="state.json"
SUMMARY_FILE="summary.json"
USER_REPORT="user_report.txt"
TROUBLESHOOTING_GUIDE="troubleshooting_guide.txt"
RESOURCE_LOG="resource_usage.log"
ENV_PATH="config/.env"
MAX_RETRIES=6
RETRY_WAIT_INITIAL=2
TIMEOUT=300
MIN_DISK_SPACE_MB=500
MIN_MEMORY_MB=500
REQUIRED_NODE_VERSION="18.0.0"
REQUIRED_PNPM_VERSION="7.0.0"
REQUIRED_ENV_VARS=("GOOGLE_APPLICATION_CREDENTIALS")
PROJECT_DIRS=("shared" "frontend" "backend")
COMPOSE_FILES=(
  "./infra/docker/docker-compose-databases.yml"
  "./infra/docker/docker-compose-dev.yml"
)
REQUIRED_FRONTEND_DEPS=(
  "react"
  "react-dom"
  "@types/react"
  "@types/react-dom"
  "vite"
  "@vitejs/plugin-react"
  "@types/node"
  "tailwindcss"
  "autoprefixer"
)
VERBOSE=false
DEBUG=false
SILENT=false
RESTART_FROM="start"
RESUME=false
RECOVERY_MODE=false
PARALLEL_EXEC=true
FORCE_PARALLEL=false
INTERRUPT_STATE=true
DRY_RUN=false
TIMEOUT_OVERRIDE=false
declare -a SUCCESSFUL_STEPS
declare -a FAILED_STEPS
declare -a DEPRECATED_DEPS
declare -a SKIP_STEPS
declare -A STEP_TIMINGS
declare -A ENV_VAR_STATUS

# === UTILITY FUNCTIONS ===
timestamp() {
  date "+%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S"
}

log() {
  local level="$1"
  local msg="$2"
  local emoji=""
  case "$level" in
    "INFO") emoji="ℹ️ " ;;
    "WARNING") emoji="⚠️ " ;;
    "ERROR") emoji="❌ " ;;
    "SUCCESS") emoji="✅ " ;;
    "DEBUG") emoji="🔍 " ;;
  esac
  if [ "$SILENT" = false ]; then
    if [[ "$level" != "DEBUG" || "$VERBOSE" == true || "$DEBUG" == true ]]; then
      echo -e "$(timestamp) $emoji[$level] $msg" >&2 | tee -a "$LOGFILE"
    else
      echo -e "$(timestamp) $emoji[$level] $msg" >> "$LOGFILE"
    fi
  else
    echo -e "$(timestamp) $emoji[$level] $msg" >> "$LOGFILE"
  fi
}

run_cmd() {
  local attempt=1
  local delay=$RETRY_WAIT_INITIAL
  local cmd="$*"
  local cmd_display="${cmd//[^[:print:]]/ }"
  local timeout_val=$TIMEOUT
  [ "$TIMEOUT_OVERRIDE" = true ] && timeout_val=600
  log "DEBUG" "Executing: $cmd_display (timeout: $timeout_val)"
  if [ "$DRY_RUN" = true ]; then
    log "INFO" "[Dry Run] Would execute: $cmd_display"
    return 0
  fi
  local output
  until output=$(timeout "$timeout_val" $cmd 2>&1); do
    if (( attempt >= MAX_RETRIES )); then
      log "ERROR" "Command failed after $attempt attempts: $cmd_display"
      log "ERROR" "Output: $output"
      update_experience_db "command_failed" "$cmd_display" "$output" "Check $LOGFILE and $TROUBLESHOOTING_GUIDE"
      return 1
    fi
    log "WARNING" "Command failed (attempt $attempt): $cmd_display"
    log "DEBUG" "Output: $output"
    if check_experience_db "command_failed" "$cmd_display"; then
      log "INFO" "Retrying after known fix..."
    fi
    if echo "$output" | grep -q "ENOMEM\|ECONNREFUSED"; then
      log "INFO" "Resource or network issue detected, retrying..."
      check_resources
    fi
    log "INFO" "Retrying in $delay seconds..."
    sleep "$delay"
    delay=$(( delay * 2 ))
    ((attempt++))
  done
  log "SUCCESS" "Command succeeded: $cmd_display"
  echo "$output" >> "$LOGFILE"
  update_state "command_success" "$cmd_display" "Success"
  return 0
}

version_ge() {
  local v1="$1"
  local v2="$2"
  v1=${v1#v}
  v2=${v2#v}
  IFS='.' read -ra ver1 <<< "$v1"
  IFS='.' read -ra ver2 <<< "$v2"
  for ((i=${#ver1[@]}; i<3; i++)); do ver1[i]=0; done
  for ((i=${#ver2[@]}; i<3; i++)); do ver2[i]=0; done
  for ((i=0; i<3; i++)); do
    local num1=${ver1[i]:-0}
    local num2=${ver2[i]:-0}
    num1=$((10#$num1))
    num2=$((10#$num2))
    if (( num1 > num2 )); then return 0; fi
    if (( num1 < num2 )); then return 1; fi
  done
  return 0
}

hash_file() {
  local file="$1"
  if command -v sha256sum >/dev/null 2>&1; then
    sha256sum "$file" | awk '{print $1}'
  else
    certutil -hashfile "$file" SHA256 | grep -v "^CertUtil" | tr -d '[:space:]'
  fi
}

check_resources() {
  log "INFO" "Checking system resources..."
  local disk_space_mb
  disk_space_mb=$(df -m "$(pwd)" | tail -n 1 | awk '{print $4}')
  local memory_free_mb
  memory_free_mb=$(wmic OS get FreePhysicalMemory | grep -v "FreePhysicalMemory" | awk '{print $1/1024}')
  echo "Disk Space: $disk_space_mb MB" >> "$RESOURCE_LOG"
  echo "Memory Free: $memory_free_mb MB" >> "$RESOURCE_LOG"
  log "DEBUG" "Resources: Disk=$disk_space_mb MB, Memory=$memory_free_mb MB"
  if (( disk_space_mb < MIN_DISK_SPACE_MB )) || (( memory_free_mb < MIN_MEMORY_MB )); then
    log "ERROR" "Insufficient resources: Disk=$disk_space_mb MB (min $MIN_DISK_SPACE_MB), Memory=$memory_free_mb MB (min $MIN_MEMORY_MB)"
    update_experience_db "low_resources" "install" "Disk=$disk_space_mb MB, Memory=$memory_free_mb MB" "Free up disk space and memory"
    generate_troubleshooting_guide
    generate_user_report
    exit 1
  fi
}

update_experience_db() {
  local error_type="$1"
  local context="$2"
  local output="$3"
  local resolution="$4"
  if ! command -v jq >/dev/null 2>&1; then
    log "WARNING" "jq not installed. Cannot update $EXPERIENCE_DB."
    return 1
  fi
  local entry
  entry=$(jq -n \
    --arg type "$error_type" \
    --arg ctx "$context" \
    --arg out "$output" \
    --arg res "$resolution" \
    --arg ts "$(timestamp)" \
    --arg success_rate "1" \
    '{type: $type, context: $ctx, output: $out, resolution: $res, timestamp: $ts, success_rate: $success_rate}')
  if [ -f "$EXPERIENCE_DB" ]; then
    jq ". + [$entry] | sort_by(.timestamp) | reverse | .[:50]" "$EXPERIENCE_DB" > "${EXPERIENCE_DB}.tmp" && mv "${EXPERIENCE_DB}.tmp" "$EXPERIENCE_DB"
  else
    echo "[$entry]" > "$EXPERIENCE_DB"
  fi
  log "DEBUG" "Updated $EXPERIENCE_DB with $error_type"
}

update_state() {
  local step="$1"
  local context="$2"
  local status="$3"
  if ! command -v jq >/dev/null 2>&1; then
    return 1
  fi
  local entry
  entry=$(jq -n \
    --arg step "$step" \
    --arg ctx "$context" \
    --arg status "$status" \
    --arg ts "$(timestamp)" \
    '{step: $step, context: $ctx, status: $status, timestamp: $ts}')
  if [ -f "$STATE_FILE" ]; then
    jq ". + [$entry] | sort_by(.timestamp) | reverse | .[:50]" "$STATE_FILE" > "${STATE_FILE}.tmp" && mv "${STATE_FILE}.tmp" "$STATE_FILE"
  else
    echo "[$entry]" > "$STATE_FILE"
  fi
}

check_experience_db() {
  local error_type="$1"
  local context="$2"
  if [ -f "$EXPERIENCE_DB" ] && command -v jq >/dev/null 2>&1; then
    local resolution
    resolution=$(jq -r ".[] | select(.type==\"$error_type\" and .context | contains(\"$context\")) | .resolution" "$EXPERIENCE_DB" | head -n 1)
    if [ -n "$resolution" ]; then
      log "INFO" "Applying known fix: $resolution"
      eval "$resolution"
      return 0
    fi
  fi
  return 1
}

generate_troubleshooting_guide() {
  log "INFO" "Generating $TROUBLESHOOTING_GUIDE"
  cat << EOF > "$TROUBLESHOOTING_GUIDE"
Troubleshooting Guide for setup-and-run.sh ($(timestamp))

1. Parallel Install Failure:
   - Check: shared_install.log, frontend_install.log, backend_install.log
   - Fix: ./setup-and-run.sh --no-parallel
   - Fix: pnpm dedupe
   - Fix: Check resources: df -m, wmic OS get FreePhysicalMemory
   - Fix: Increase timeout: ./setup-and-run.sh --timeout 600

2. Workspace Configuration:
   - Verify pnpm-workspace.yaml:
     packages:
       - frontend
       - backend
       - shared
   - Fix: echo -e "packages:\n  - frontend\n  - backend\n  - shared" > pnpm-workspace.yaml

3. Postinstall Script:
   - Check package.json:
     "scripts": {"postinstall": "pnpm --filter frontend install && pnpm --filter backend install && pnpm --filter shared install"}
   - Fix: jq '.scripts.postinstall = "pnpm --filter frontend install && pnpm --filter backend install && pnpm --filter shared install"' package.json > tmp.json && mv tmp.json package.json

4. Missing Exports:
   - Check shared/src/index.ts:
     export type UserRole = 'admin' | 'user' | 'guest';
   - Fix: echo "export type UserRole = 'admin' | 'user' | 'guest';" >> shared/src/index.ts
   - Ensure shared builds: pnpm --filter shared build

5. TypeScript Configuration:
   - Verify shared/tsconfig.json:
     {
       "compilerOptions": {
         "outDir": "./dist",
         "declaration": true
       }
     }
   - Verify frontend/tsconfig.json:
     {
       "compilerOptions": {
         "types": ["vite/client", "node"],
         "paths": {"@quran-platform-mvp/shared": ["../shared/src"]}
       }
     }

6. Vite Configuration:
   - Check frontend/vite.config.ts:
     resolve: { alias: {'@quran-platform-mvp/shared': path.resolve(__dirname, '../shared/src')} }
   - Fix: sed -i "/resolve: {/a\    alias: {\n      '@quran-platform-mvp/shared': path.resolve(__dirname, '../shared/src'),\n    }," frontend/vite.config.ts

7. Missing Dependencies:
   - Ensure frontend/package.json includes: ${REQUIRED_FRONTEND_DEPS[*]}
   - Run: pnpm --filter frontend add ${REQUIRED_FRONTEND_DEPS[*]}

8. Build Failures:
   - Check $LOGFILE, $STATE_FILE, $SUMMARY_FILE.
   - Run: ./setup-and-run.sh --debug --restart-from build

9. Docker Issues:
   - Ensure Docker is running and files exist: ${COMPOSE_FILES[*]}
   - Run: docker-compose -f <file> up -d

10. Resource Constraints:
    - Check $RESOURCE_LOG
    - Free up disk/memory: del /q /s node_modules, pnpm store prune

11. Debug Mode:
    - Run: ./setup-and-run.sh --debug --silent
    - Review: $LOGFILE, $EXPERIENCE_DB, $SUMMARY_FILE, $USER_REPORT
EOF
}

generate_user_report() {
  local progress_percentage=$(( ${#SUCCESSFUL_STEPS[@]} * 100 / (${#SUCCESSFUL_STEPS[@]} + ${#FAILED_STEPS[@]} + 1) ))
  local env_status=""
  for var in "${!ENV_VAR_STATUS[@]}"; do
    env_status+="$var: ${ENV_VAR_STATUS[$var]}\n"
  done
  local error_logs=""
  for project in "${PROJECT_DIRS[@]}"; do
    if [ -f "${project}_install.log" ]; then
      error_logs+="${project}_install.log\n"
    fi
  done
  error_logs+="$LOGFILE\n$STATE_FILE\n$SUMMARY_FILE\n$RESOURCE_LOG"
  log "INFO" "Generating $USER_REPORT for Jules"
  cat << EOF > "$USER_REPORT"
{
  "recipient": "Jules",
  "timestamp": "$(timestamp)",
  "project": "Quran-recitation-mvp",
  "version": "0.1.0",
  "progress_percentage": $progress_percentage,
  "current_state": "${FAILED_STEPS:+Failed at ${FAILED_STEPS[-1]}. }${SUCCESSFUL_STEPS[-1]:-Setup started}",
  "successful_steps": [
    $(printf '"%s",' "${SUCCESSFUL_STEPS[@]}" | sed 's/,$//')
  ],
  "failed_steps": [
    $(printf '"%s",' "${FAILED_STEPS[@]}" | sed 's/,$//')
  ],
  "environment_variables": "$env_status",
  "deprecated_dependencies": [
    $(printf '"%s",' "${DEPRECATED_DEPS[@]}" | sed 's/,$//')
  ],
  "error_debugging": "Check:\n$error_logs",
  "next_steps": "${FAILED_STEPS:+Run ./setup-and-run.sh --debug --resume --no-parallel\n}${DEPRECATED_DEPS:+Run pnpm --filter frontend update\n}Review $TROUBLESHOOTING_GUIDE",
  "compatibility": "Google Grok, ChatGPT"
}
EOF
}

# === CORE FUNCTIONS ===
load_env_file() {
  local start_time=$(date +%s)
  if [ -f "$ENV_PATH" ]; then
    log "INFO" "Loading $ENV_PATH"
    set -a
    # shellcheck source=/dev/null
    source "$ENV_PATH"
    set +a
    for var in "${REQUIRED_ENV_VARS[@]}"; do
      if [ -z "${!var:-}" ]; then
        log "ERROR" "Required variable $var not set"
        FAILED_STEPS+=("Validate $var")
        ENV_VAR_STATUS[$var]="Not set"
        update_experience_db "missing_env_var" "$var" "Not set in $ENV_PATH" "Add $var to $ENV_PATH"
        return 1
      else
        ENV_VAR_STATUS[$var]="Set (value hidden)"
      fi
    done
    log "SUCCESS" "Environment loaded"
    SUCCESSFUL_STEPS+=("Load environment")
    update_state "load_env" "$ENV_PATH" "Success"
  else
    log "WARNING" "$ENV_PATH not found"
    SUCCESSFUL_STEPS+=("Load environment (skipped)")
    ENV_VAR_STATUS["GOOGLE_APPLICATION_CREDENTIALS"]="Missing $ENV_PATH"
    update_experience_db "missing_env_file" "$ENV_PATH" "File not found" "Create $ENV_PATH with $REQUIRED_ENV_VARS"
  fi
  local end_time=$(date +%s)
  STEP_TIMINGS["load_env"]=$((end_time - start_time))
}

check_node_pnpm_versions() {
  local start_time=$(date +%s)
  local node_version=$(node -v 2>/dev/null || echo "none")
  local pnpm_version=$(pnpm -v 2>/dev/null || echo "none")
  log "INFO" "Detected Node.js: $node_version, pnpm: $pnpm_version"
  if [[ "$node_version" == "none" ]] || [[ "$pnpm_version" == "none" ]]; then
    log "ERROR" "Node.js or pnpm not installed"
    FAILED_STEPS+=("Check versions")
    update_experience_db "missing_runtime" "Node.js or pnpm" "Not found" "Install Node.js >= $REQUIRED_NODE_VERSION, pnpm >= $REQUIRED_PNPM_VERSION"
    exit 1
  fi
  local node_version_clean=${node_version#v}
  if ! version_ge "$node_version_clean" "$REQUIRED_NODE_VERSION" || ! version_ge "$pnpm_version" "$REQUIRED_PNPM_VERSION"; then
    log "ERROR" "Version requirements not met"
    FAILED_STEPS+=("Version checks")
    update_experience_db "version_mismatch" "Node.js: $node_version, pnpm: $pnpm_version" "Below required versions" "Upgrade Node.js and pnpm"
    exit 1
  fi
  log "SUCCESS" "Versions meet requirements"
  SUCCESSFUL_STEPS+=("Version checks")
  update_state "check_versions" "Node.js and pnpm" "Success"
  local end_time=$(date +%s)
  STEP_TIMINGS["check_versions"]=$((end_time - start_time))
}

fix_tsconfig() {
  local start_time=$(date +%s)
  local project="$1"
  local tsconfig="$project/tsconfig.json"
  if ! command -v jq >/dev/null 2>&1; then
    log "WARNING" "jq not installed. Cannot auto-fix $tsconfig."
    update_experience_db "missing_jq" "tsconfig_fix" "jq not found" "Install jq: choco install jq"
    return 1
  fi
  local default_config
  if [[ "$project" == "shared" ]]; then
    default_config='{
      "compilerOptions": {
        "target": "ESNext",
        "module": "ESNext",
        "moduleResolution": "node",
        "outDir": "./dist",
        "declaration": true,
        "strict": true,
        "esModuleInterop": true,
        "skipLibCheck": true
      },
      "include": ["src/**/*"]
    }'
  else
    default_config='{
      "compilerOptions": {
        "target": "ESNext",
        "module": "ESNext",
        "moduleResolution": "node",
        "jsx": "react-jsx",
        "strict": true,
        "esModuleInterop": true,
        "skipLibCheck": true,
        "types": ["vite/client", "node"],
        "paths": {"@quran-platform-mvp/shared": ["../shared/src"]}
      },
      "include": ["src/**/*"]
    }'
  fi
  if [ ! -f "$tsconfig" ]; then
    log "INFO" "Creating $tsconfig"
    echo "$default_config" | jq . > "$tsconfig"
    log "SUCCESS" "Created $tsconfig"
    SUCCESSFUL_STEPS+=("Create $tsconfig")
    update_state "fix_tsconfig" "$tsconfig" "Created"
    return 0
  fi
  log "DEBUG" "Checking $tsconfig"
  if [[ "$project" == "shared" ]]; then
    if ! jq '.compilerOptions.outDir == "./dist" and .compilerOptions.declaration == true' "$tsconfig" | grep -q "true"; then
      log "INFO" "Updating $tsconfig"
      jq '.compilerOptions.outDir = "./dist" | .compilerOptions.declaration = true' "$tsconfig" > "${tsconfig}.tmp" && mv "${tsconfig}.tmp" "$tsconfig"
      log "SUCCESS" "Updated $tsconfig"
      SUCCESSFUL_STEPS+=("Update $tsconfig")
      update_state "fix_tsconfig" "$tsconfig" "Updated"
    else
      log "SUCCESS" "$tsconfig valid"
      SUCCESSFUL_STEPS+=("Validate $tsconfig")
      update_state "fix_tsconfig" "$tsconfig" "Valid"
    fi
  else
    if ! jq '.compilerOptions.types | index("vite/client") and index("node")' "$tsconfig" | grep -q "true" || ! jq '.compilerOptions.paths["@quran-platform-mvp/shared"]' "$tsconfig" | grep -q "shared/src"; then
      log "INFO" "Updating $tsconfig"
      jq '.compilerOptions.types |= (. + ["vite/client", "node"] | unique) | .compilerOptions.paths |= (. + {"@quran-platform-mvp/shared": ["../shared/src"]})' "$tsconfig" > "${tsconfig}.tmp" && mv "${tsconfig}.tmp" "$tsconfig"
      log "SUCCESS" "Updated $tsconfig"
      SUCCESSFUL_STEPS+=("Update $tsconfig")
      update_state "fix_tsconfig" "$tsconfig" "Updated"
    else
      log "SUCCESS" "$tsconfig valid"
      SUCCESSFUL_STEPS+=("Validate $tsconfig")
      update_state "fix_tsconfig" "$tsconfig" "Valid"
    fi
  fi
  local end_time=$(date +%s)
  STEP_TIMINGS["fix_tsconfig_$project"]=$((end_time - start_time))
}

fix_vite_config() {
  local start_time=$(date +%s)
  local vite_config="frontend/vite.config.ts"
  if [ ! -f "$vite_config" ]; then
    log "INFO" "Creating $vite_config"
    cat << EOF > "$vite_config"
import { defineConfig } from 'vite';
import react from '@vitejs/plugin-react';
import path from 'path';

export default defineConfig({
  plugins: [react()],
  resolve: {
    alias: {
      '@quran-platform-mvp/shared': path.resolve(__dirname, '../shared/src'),
      '@': path.resolve(__dirname, './src'),
    },
  },
  css: {
    postcss: {
      plugins: [require('tailwindcss'), require('autoprefixer')],
    },
  },
});
EOF
    log "SUCCESS" "Created $vite_config"
    SUCCESSFUL_STEPS+=("Create $vite_config")
    update_state "fix_vite_config" "$vite_config" "Created"
    return 0
  fi
  if ! grep -q "@quran-platform-mvp/shared" "$vite_config"; then
    log "INFO" "Updating $vite_config with alias"
    sed -i "/resolve: {/a\    alias: {\n      '@quran-platform-mvp/shared': path.resolve(__dirname, '../shared/src'),\n      '@': path.resolve(__dirname, './src'),\n    }," "$vite_config"
    log "SUCCESS" "Updated $vite_config"
    SUCCESSFUL_STEPS+=("Update $vite_config")
    update_state "fix_vite_config" "$vite_config" "Updated"
  else
    log "SUCCESS" "$vite_config valid"
    SUCCESSFUL_STEPS+=("Validate $vite_config")
    update_state "fix_vite_config" "$vite_config" "Valid"
  fi
  local end_time=$(date +%s)
  STEP_TIMINGS["fix_vite_config"]=$((end_time - start_time))
}

fix_shared_exports() {
  local start_time=$(date +%s)
  local shared_index="shared/src/index.ts"
  if [ ! -f "$shared_index" ]; then
    log "INFO" "Creating $shared_index"
    mkdir -p "shared/src"
    echo "export type UserRole = 'admin' | 'user' | 'guest';" > "$shared_index"
    log "SUCCESS" "Created $shared_index"
    SUCCESSFUL_STEPS+=("Create $shared_index")
    update_state "fix_shared_exports" "$shared_index" "Created"
    return 0
  fi
  if ! grep -q "export type UserRole" "$shared_index"; then
    log "INFO" "Adding UserRole to $shared_index"
    echo "export type UserRole = 'admin' | 'user' | 'guest';" >> "$shared_index"
    log "SUCCESS" "Updated $shared_index"
    SUCCESSFUL_STEPS+=("Update $shared_index")
    update_state "fix_shared_exports" "$shared_index" "Updated"
  else
    log "SUCCESS" "$shared_index exports UserRole"
    SUCCESSFUL_STEPS+=("Validate $shared_index")
    update_state "fix_shared_exports" "$shared_index" "Valid"
  fi
  local end_time=$(date +%s)
  STEP_TIMINGS["fix_shared_exports"]=$((end_time - start_time))
}

fix_workspace_config() {
  local start_time=$(date +%s)
  local workspace_file="pnpm-workspace.yaml"
  if [ ! -f "$workspace_file" ]; then
    log "INFO" "Creating $workspace_file"
    cat << EOF > "$workspace_file"
packages:
  - frontend
  - backend
  - shared
EOF
    log "SUCCESS" "Created $workspace_file"
    SUCCESSFUL_STEPS+=("Create $workspace_file")
    update_state "fix_workspace_config" "$workspace_file" "Created"
    update_experience_db "missing_workspace" "$workspace_file" "File not found" "Created with packages: frontend, backend, shared"
    return 0
  fi
  if ! grep -q "packages:.*frontend.*backend.*shared" "$workspace_file"; then
    log "INFO" "Fixing $workspace_file"
    cat << EOF > "$workspace_file"
packages:
  - frontend
  - backend
  - shared
EOF
    log "SUCCESS" "Updated $workspace_file"
    SUCCESSFUL_STEPS+=("Update $workspace_file")
    update_state "fix_workspace_config" "$workspace_file" "Updated"
    update_experience_db "workspace_misconfig" "$workspace_file" "Invalid packages" "Updated with packages: frontend, backend, shared"
    return 0
  fi
  log "SUCCESS" "$workspace_file valid"
  SUCCESSFUL_STEPS+=("Validate $workspace_file")
  update_state "fix_workspace_config" "$workspace_file" "Valid"
  local end_time=$(date +%s)
  STEP_TIMINGS["fix_workspace_config"]=$((end_time - start_time))
}

fix_postinstall_script() {
  local start_time=$(date +%s)
  local package_json="package.json"
  if [ ! -f "$package_json" ]; then
    log "WARNING" "$package_json not found. Creating minimal version."
    jq -n '{name: "quran-recitation-mvp", version: "0.1.0", scripts: {postinstall: "pnpm --filter frontend install && pnpm --filter backend install && pnpm --filter shared install"}}' > "$package_json"
    log "SUCCESS" "Created $package_json"
    SUCCESSFUL_STEPS+=("Create $package_json")
    update_state "fix_postinstall_script" "$package_json" "Created"
    return 0
  fi
  if ! command -v jq >/dev/null 2>&1; then
    log "WARNING" "jq not installed. Cannot fix postinstall."
    update_experience_db "missing_jq" "postinstall_fix" "jq not found" "Install jq: choco install jq"
    return 1
  fi
  if jq '.scripts.postinstall | contains("packages/**")' "$package_json" | grep -q "true" || ! jq '.scripts.postinstall' "$package_json" | grep -q "frontend"; then
    log "INFO" "Fixing postinstall script in $package_json"
    jq '.scripts.postinstall = "pnpm --filter frontend install && pnpm --filter backend install && pnpm --filter shared install"' "$package_json" > "${package_json}.tmp" && mv "${package_json}.tmp" "$package_json"
    log "SUCCESS" "Updated postinstall script"
    SUCCESSFUL_STEPS+=("Fix postinstall")
    update_state "fix_postinstall_script" "$package_json" "Updated"
    update_experience_db "postinstall_misconfig" "$package_json" "Incorrect filter" "Updated to: pnpm --filter frontend install && pnpm --filter backend install && pnpm --filter shared install"
  else
    log "SUCCESS" "Postinstall script valid"
    SUCCESSFUL_STEPS+=("Validate postinstall")
    update_state "fix_postinstall_script" "$package_json" "Valid"
  fi
  local end_time=$(date +%s)
  STEP_TIMINGS["fix_postinstall_script"]=$((end_time - start_time))
}

check_dependencies() {
  local start_time=$(date +%s)
  local project="$1"
  local package_json="$project/package.json"
  if [ ! -f "$package_json" ]; then
    log "ERROR" "$package_json not found"
    FAILED_STEPS+=("Validate $package_json")
    update_experience_db "missing_package_json" "$package_json" "File not found" "Create $package_json"
    return 1
  fi
  local output
  output=$(pnpm --filter "$project" install --dry-run 2>&1)
  if echo "$output" | grep -q "deprecated"; then
    while IFS= read -r line; do
      if [[ "$line" =~ WARN.*deprecated[[:space:]]*([^[:space:]]+) ]]; then
        DEPRECATED_DEPS+=("${BASH_REMATCH[1]}")
        log "WARNING" "Deprecated: ${BASH_REMATCH[1]}"
      fi
    done <<< "$output"
  fi
  for dep in "${REQUIRED_FRONTEND_DEPS[@]}"; do
    if ! grep -q "\"$dep\"" "$package_json"; then
      log "WARNING" "Missing $dep in $package_json. Installing..."
      if ! run_cmd pnpm --filter "$project" add "$dep"; then
        log "ERROR" "Failed to install $dep"
        FAILED_STEPS+=("Install $dep in $project")
        update_experience_db "dep_install_failed" "$dep in $project" "pnpm add failed" "Run: pnpm --filter $project add $dep"
        return 1
      fi
      SUCCESSFUL_STEPS+=("Install $dep in $project")
    fi
  done
  if [ "$project" = "frontend" ]; then
    if ! run_cmd pnpm --filter "$project" dedupe; then
      log "WARNING" "Dependency deduplication failed"
    else
      log "SUCCESS" "Dependencies deduplicated in $project"
    fi
  fi
  log "SUCCESS" "Dependencies valid in $project"
  SUCCESSFUL_STEPS+=("Validate dependencies in $project")
  update_state "check_dependencies" "$project" "Success"
  local end_time=$(date +%s)
  STEP_TIMINGS["check_dependencies_$project"]=$((end_time - start_time))
}

pnpm_install() {
  local start_time=$(date +%s)
  log "INFO" "Installing dependencies..."
  check_resources
  fix_workspace_config || return 1
  fix_postinstall_script
  local parallel_failed=false
  if [ "$PARALLEL_EXEC" = true ] && [ "$FORCE_PARALLEL" = true ]; then
    local pids=()
    for project in "${PROJECT_DIRS[@]}"; do
      if [ -d "$project" ]; then
        local package_json="$project/package.json"
        local node_modules="$project/node_modules"
        local package_hash_file="$project/.package_hash"
        local current_hash=""
        if [ -f "$package_json" ]; then
          current_hash=$(hash_file "$package_json")
        fi
        if [ -d "$node_modules" ] && [ -f "$package_hash_file" ] && [ "$(cat "$package_hash_file")" == "$current_hash" ]; then
          log "INFO" "$project/node_modules up-to-date"
          SUCCESSFUL_STEPS+=("Install dependencies in $project (skipped)")
        else
          log "INFO" "$project/node_modules needs install"
          pnpm --filter "$project" install --prefer-offline > "${project}_install.log" 2>&1 &
          pids+=($!)
        fi
      else
        log "WARNING" "Directory $project not found"
        SUCCESSFUL_STEPS+=("Install dependencies in $project (skipped)")
      fi
    done
    for pid in "${pids[@]}"; do
      wait "$pid" || parallel_failed=true
    done
    for project in "${PROJECT_DIRS[@]}"; do
      if [ -f "${project}_install.log" ]; then
        if grep -q "ERR_PNPM" "${project}_install.log"; then
          log "ERROR" "Install failed for $project. See ${project}_install.log"
          FAILED_STEPS+=("Install dependencies in $project")
          update_experience_db "install_failed" "$project" "$(cat "${project}_install.log")" "Run: pnpm --filter $project install --prefer-offline"
          parallel_failed=true
        else
          local package_json="$project/package.json"
          local current_hash=$(hash_file "$package_json")
          echo "$current_hash" > "$project/.package_hash"
          SUCCESSFUL_STEPS+=("Install dependencies in $project")
          rm "${project}_install.log"
        fi
      fi
    done
  fi
  if [ "$parallel_failed" = true ] || [ "$PARALLEL_EXEC" = false ]; then
    log "INFO" "Falling back to sequential installs"
    for project in "${PROJECT_DIRS[@]}"; do
      if [ -d "$project" ]; then
        local package_json="$project/package.json"
        local node_modules="$project/node_modules"
        local package_hash_file="$project/.package_hash"
        local current_hash=""
        if [ -f "$package_json" ]; then
          current_hash=$(hash_file "$package_json")
        fi
        if [ -d "$node_modules" ] && [ -f "$package_hash_file" ] && [ "$(cat "$package_hash_file")" == "$current_hash" ]; then
          log "INFO" "$project/node_modules up-to-date"
          SUCCESSFUL_STEPS+=("Install dependencies in $project (skipped)")
        else
          log "INFO" "$project/node_modules needs install"
          if ! run_cmd pnpm --filter "$project" install --prefer-offline; then
            log "ERROR" "pnpm install failed for $project"
            FAILED_STEPS+=("Install dependencies in $project")
            update_experience_db "install_failed" "$project" "pnpm install error" "Run: pnpm --filter $project install --prefer-offline"
            return 1
          fi
          echo "$current_hash" > "$project/.package_hash"
          SUCCESSFUL_STEPS+=("Install dependencies in $project")
        fi
      else
        log "WARNING" "Directory $project not found"
        SUCCESSFUL_STEPS+=("Install dependencies in $project (skipped)")
      fi
    done
  fi
  for project in "${PROJECT_DIRS[@]}"; do
    if [ -d "$project" ]; then
      if [[ "$project" == "frontend" ]]; then
        check_dependencies "$project" || return 1
        fix_tsconfig "$project" || return 1
        fix_vite_config || return 1
      fi
      if [[ "$project" == "shared" ]]; then
        fix_tsconfig "$project" || return 1
        fix_shared_exports || return 1
      fi
    fi
  done
  log "SUCCESS" "Dependency installation completed"
  update_state "pnpm_install" "All projects" "Success"
  local end_time=$(date +%s)
  STEP_TIMINGS["pnpm_install"]=$((end_time - start_time))
}

clean_caches() {
  local start_time=$(date +%s)
  log "INFO" "Cleaning caches..."
  local cleaned=false
  for dir in "${PROJECT_DIRS[@]}"; do
    local node_modules="$dir/node_modules"
    if [ -d "$node_modules" ]; then
      rm -rf "$node_modules"
      log "INFO" "Removed $node_modules"
      cleaned=true
    fi
  done
  if [ "$cleaned" = true ] || [ ! -d "node_modules/.pnpm" ]; then
    if ! run_cmd pnpm store prune; then
      log "WARNING" "pnpm store prune failed"
      FAILED_STEPS+=("pnpm store prune")
      update_experience_db "cache_prune_failed" "pnpm store prune" "Command failed" "Run: pnpm store prune"
    else
      SUCCESSFUL_STEPS+=("pnpm store prune")
    fi
  else
    log "INFO" "No node_modules to clean, skipping prune"
    SUCCESSFUL_STEPS+=("pnpm store prune (skipped)")
  fi
  log "SUCCESS" "Cache cleanup completed"
  update_state "clean_caches" "All projects" "Success"
  local end_time=$(date +%s)
  STEP_TIMINGS["clean_caches"]=$((end_time - start_time))
}

build_all() {
  local start_time=$(date +%s)
  log "INFO" "Building projects..."
  for project in "${PROJECT_DIRS[@]}"; do
    log "INFO" "Building $project"
    local build_hash_file="$project/.build_hash"
    local current_hash=""
    if [ -f "$project/package.json" ] && [ -d "$project/src" ]; then
      current_hash=$(find "$project/src" "$project/package.json" -type f -exec hash_file {} \; | sort | sha256sum | awk '{print $1}')
    fi
    if [ -f "$build_hash_file" ] && [ "$(cat "$build_hash_file")" == "$current_hash" ] && [ -d "$project/dist" ]; then
      log "INFO" "$project build up-to-date"
      SUCCESSFUL_STEPS+=("Build $project (skipped)")
      continue
    fi
    local output
    if ! output=$(pnpm --filter "$project" build 2>&1); then
      log "ERROR" "$project build failed: $output"
      if echo "$output" | grep -q "is not exported by"; then
        log "INFO" "Detected missing export"
        fix_shared_exports
        fix_tsconfig "shared"
        if run_cmd pnpm --filter "$project" build; then
          log "SUCCESS" "Build $project succeeded after fixing exports"
          echo "$current_hash" > "$build_hash_file"
          SUCCESSFUL_STEPS+=("Build $project")
          update_state "build_all" "$project" "Success after fix"
          continue
        fi
      fi
      if echo "$output" | grep -q "tsc"; then
        log "INFO" "Attempting fallback build"
        if run_cmd pnpm --filter "$project" exec tsc --noEmit; then
          log "SUCCESS" "Fallback build succeeded for $project"
          echo "$current_hash" > "$build_hash_file"
          SUCCESSFUL_STEPS+=("Build $project (fallback)")
          update_state "build_all" "$project" "Fallback success"
          continue
        fi
      fi
      log "ERROR" "Build failed. Check $LOGFILE."
      FAILED_STEPS+=("Build $project")
      update_experience_db "build_failed" "$project" "$output" "Run: pnpm --filter $project build"
      return 1
    fi
    log "SUCCESS" "Build $project succeeded"
    echo "$current_hash" > "$build_hash_file"
    SUCCESSFUL_STEPS+=("Build $project")
    update_state "build_all" "$project" "Success"
  done
  log "SUCCESS" "Build completed"
  local end_time=$(date +%s)
  STEP_TIMINGS["build_all"]=$((end_time - start_time))
}

docker_all() {
  local start_time=$(date +%s)
  log "INFO" "Starting Docker..."
  local index=1
  for compose_file in "${COMPOSE_FILES[@]}"; do
    local service_name=$([[ "$compose_file" == *"databases"* ]] && echo "database containers" || echo "dev containers")
    log "INFO" "Starting $service_name ($index/${#COMPOSE_FILES[@]})"
    if ! run_cmd docker-compose -f "$compose_file" up -d; then
      log "ERROR" "Failed to start $service_name"
      FAILED_STEPS+=("Docker $service_name")
      update_experience_db "docker_failed" "$service_name" "docker-compose failed" "Ensure Docker is running and check $compose_file"
      if [ "$RECOVERY_MODE" = true ]; then
        log "WARNING" "Continuing in recovery mode"
        continue
      fi
      return 1
    fi
    SUCCESSFUL_STEPS+=("Docker $service_name")
    update_state "docker_all" "$service_name" "Success"
    ((index++))
  done
  log "SUCCESS" "Docker started"
  local end_time=$(date +%s)
  STEP_TIMINGS["docker_all"]=$((end_time - start_time))
}

# === INTERRUPTION HANDLING ===
handle_interrupt() {
  log "WARNING" "Script interrupted, saving state..."
  update_state "interrupted" "main execution" "INTERRUPTED"
  generate_troubleshooting_guide
  generate_user_report
  exit 0
}

if [ "$INTERRUPT_STATE" = true ]; then
  trap handle_interrupt SIGINT
fi

# === MAIN EXECUTION ===
main() {
  while [[ $# -gt 0 ]]; do
    case "$1" in
      --verbose) VERBOSE=true; shift ;;
      --debug) DEBUG=true; VERBOSE=true; shift ;;
      --silent) SILENT=true; shift ;;
      --restart-from=*) RESTART_FROM="${1#*=}"; shift ;;
      --resume) RESUME=true; shift ;;
      --recovery) RECOVERY_MODE=true; shift ;;
      --no-parallel) PARALLEL_EXEC=false; shift ;;
      --force-parallel) FORCE_PARALLEL=true; shift ;;
      --no-interrupt-save) INTERRUPT_STATE=false; shift ;;
      --dry-run) DRY_RUN=true; shift ;;
      --skip-step=*) SKIP_STEPS+=("${1#*=}"); shift ;;
      --timeout=*) TIMEOUT=${1#*=}; TIMEOUT_OVERRIDE=true; shift ;;
      *) log "WARNING" "Unknown argument: $1"; shift ;;
    esac
  done

  log "INFO" "=== Setup Script Started ==="
  local start_time=$(date +%s)
  SUCCESSFUL_STEPS=()
  FAILED_STEPS=()
  DEPRECATED_DEPS=()
  STEP_TIMINGS=()
  ENV_VAR_STATUS=()

  if [ "$RESUME" = true ] && [ -f "$STATE_FILE" ]; then
    local last_failed
    last_failed=$(jq -r '.[] | select(.status=="FAILED") | .step' "$STATE_FILE" | head -n 1)
    if [ -n "$last_failed" ]; then
      RESTART_FROM="$last_failed"
      log "INFO" "Resuming from last failed step: $last_failed"
    fi
  fi

  declare -A steps=(
    ["load_env"]="load_env_file"
    ["check_versions"]="check_node_pnpm_versions"
    ["clean"]="clean_caches"
    ["install"]="pnpm_install"
    ["build"]="build_all"
    ["docker"]="docker_all"
  )
  local execute=false
  for step in "${!steps[@]}"; do
    if [[ " ${SKIP_STEPS[@]} " =~ " $step " ]]; then
      log "INFO" "Skipping step: $step (user request)"
      continue
    fi
    if [[ "$RESTART_FROM" == "start" || "$execute" == true || "$RESTART_FROM" == "$step" ]]; then
      execute=true
      log "INFO" "Executing step: $step"
      local retry_count=0
      until "${steps[$step]}"; do
        if (( retry_count >= 2)); then
          log "ERROR" "Step $step failed after retries"
          update_state "$step" "main execution" "FAILED"
          FAILED_STEPS+=("$step")
          generate_troubleshooting_guide
          generate_user_report
          if [ "$RECOVERY_MODE" = true ]; then
            log "WARNING" "Continuing in recovery mode"
            break
          fi
          exit 1
        fi
        log "INFO" "Retrying step $step after fixes..."
        case "$step" in
          "install")
            fix_workspace_config
            fix_postinstall_script
            check_resources
            PARALLEL_EXEC=false
            ;;
          "build")
            fix_shared_exports
            fix_tsconfig "shared"
            fix_tsconfig "frontend"
            fix_vite_config
            ;;
        esac
        ((retry_count++))
      done
    else
      log "INFO" "Skipping step: $step"
    fi
  done

  local end_time=$(date +%s)
  local elapsed=$((end_time - start_time))
  jq -n \
    --argjson successful "$(jq -n '$ARGS.positional' --args "${SUCCESSFUL_STEPS[@]}")" \
    --argjson failed "$(jq -n '$ARGS.positional' --args "${FAILED_STEPS[@]}")" \
    --argjson deprecated "$(jq -n '$ARGS.positional' --args "${DEPRECATED_DEPS[@]}")" \
    --arg elapsed "$elapsed" \
    --argjson timings "$(jq -n '$ARGS.named' --args "${!STEP_TIMINGS[@]}" "${STEP_TIMINGS[@]}")" \
    --argjson env_vars "$(jq -n '$ARGS.named' --args "${!ENV_VAR_STATUS[@]}" "${ENV_VAR_STATUS[@]}")" \
    '{successful: $successful, failed: $failed, deprecated: $deprecated, elapsed: $elapsed, timings: $timings, env_vars: $env_vars}' > "$SUMMARY_FILE"

  log "INFO" "=== Setup Summary ==="
  log "INFO" "Successful steps (${#SUCCESSFUL_STEPS[@]}): ${SUCCESSFUL_STEPS[*]}"
  log "INFO" "Failed steps (${#FAILED_STEPS[@]}): ${FAILED_STEPS[*]}"
  for step in "${!STEP_TIMINGS[@]}"; do
    log "INFO" "Timing for $step: ${STEP_TIMINGS[$step]} seconds"
  done
  if [ ${#DEPRECATED_DEPS[@]} -gt 0 ]; then
    log "WARNING" "Deprecated dependencies: ${DEPRECATED_DEPS[*]}"
    log "WARNING" "Run: pnpm --filter frontend update"
  fi
  generate_troubleshooting_guide
  generate_user_report
  if [ ${#FAILED_STEPS[@]} -gt 0 ]; then
    log "ERROR" "Setup failed in ${elapsed} seconds. See $LOGFILE, $TROUBLESHOOTING_GUIDE, $USER_REPORT."
    exit 1
  else
    log "SUCCESS" "Setup completed in ${elapsed} seconds"
    exit 0
  fi
}

main "$@"

Resilience and Recovery:
--resume restarts from failed steps (e.g., install).

--recovery continues past non-critical failures.

Cascading retries (6 attempts) with exponential backoff.

Saves state on interrupts (Ctrl+C) unless --no-interrupt-save.

Advanced Reporting:

--dry-run: Simulates execution without changes.

--skip-step: Bypasses problematic steps (e.g., docker).

--timeout: Overrides default timeouts for slow operations.

--force-parallel/--no-parallel: Controls execution mode.

Learning Mechanism:
experience.json: Stores 50 recent errors with resolutions, weighted by recency.

Proactively applies fixes for known issues (e.g., parallel install, UserRole).

Windows/MINGW64 Compatibility:
Uses certutil for hashing, wmic for resource checks.

Ensures POSIX compliance for jq, sed, and file paths.

Script
bash

#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail
IFS=$'\n\t'

# === CONFIGURATION ===
REPO_DIR="C:/Users/rehan/OneDrive/Desktop/FODV/02_MVP_IMPLEMENTATION"
LOG_DIR="$REPO_DIR/logs"
LOG_FILE="$LOG_DIR/setup.log"
STATE_FILE="$LOG_DIR/state.json"
SUMMARY_FILE="$LOG_DIR/summary.json"
TROUBLESHOOTING_GUIDE="$LOG_DIR/troubleshooting.txt"
RESOURCE_LOG="$LOG_DIR/resources.log"
ENV_FILE="$REPO_DIR/.env"
PROJECT_DIRS=("src/shared" "src/frontend" "src/backend")
DOCKER_COMPOSE_FILE="$REPO_DIR/infra/docker/docker-compose.yml"
REQUIRED_NODE_VERSION="18.18.0"
REQUIRED_PNPM_VERSION="8.0.0"
MIN_DISK_SPACE_MB=1024
MIN_MEMORY_MB=512
MAX_RETRIES=3
RETRY_WAIT_INITIAL=2
TIMEOUT=600

VERBOSE=false
DEBUG=false
PARALLEL=true
DRY_RUN=false
RESUME=false
declare -a SUCCESSFUL_STEPS
declare -a FAILED_STEPS
declare -a CHANGED_FILES

# === UTILITY FUNCTIONS ===
timestamp() {
  date "+%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S"
}

log() {
  local level="$1"
  local msg="$2"
  local emoji=""
  case "$level" in
    "INFO") emoji="ℹ️ " ;;
    "WARNING") emoji="⚠️ " ;;
    "ERROR") emoji="❌ " ;;
    "SUCCESS") emoji="✅ " ;;
    "DEBUG") emoji="🔍 " ;;
  esac
  local log_msg="$(timestamp) $emoji[$level] $msg"
  if [ "$VERBOSE" = true ] || [ "$level" != "DEBUG" ] || [ "$DEBUG" = true ]; then
    echo "$log_msg" >&2
  fi
  echo "$log_msg" >> "$LOG_FILE"
}

run_cmd() {
  local attempt=1
  local delay=$RETRY_WAIT_INITIAL
  local cmd="$*"
  local cmd_safe="${cmd//[^[:print:]]/_}"
  log "DEBUG" "Executing: $cmd_safe"
  if [ "$DRY_RUN" = true ]; then
    log "INFO" "[Dry Run] Would run: $cmd_safe"
    return 0
  fi
  local output
  until output=$(timeout "$TIMEOUT" bash -c "$cmd" 2>&1); do
    if [ "$attempt" -ge "$MAX_RETRIES" ]; then
      log "ERROR" "Failed after $MAX_RETRIES attempts: $cmd_safe"
      log "ERROR" "Output: $output"
      return 1
    fi
    log "WARNING" "Attempt $attempt failed: $cmd_safe"
    log "DEBUG" "Output: $output"
    sleep "$delay"
    delay=$((delay * 2))
    ((attempt++))
  done
  log "SUCCESS" "Command succeeded: $cmd_safe"
  echo "$output" >> "$LOG_FILE"
  return 0
}

version_ge() {
  local v1="$1" v2="$2"
  v1=${v1#v}
  v2=${v2#v}
  printf '%s\n%s' "$v1" "$v2" | sort -V | head -n1 | grep -q "^$v2$"
}

check_resources() {
  log "INFO" "Checking resources..."
  local disk_space_mb=$(df -m "$REPO_DIR" | tail -n 1 | awk '{print $4}' 2>/dev/null || echo "0")
  local memory_free_mb=$(wmic OS get FreePhysicalMemory 2>/dev/null | grep -v "FreePhysicalMemory" | awk '{print int($1/1024)}' || echo "0")
  echo "Disk: $disk_space_mb MB, Memory: $memory_free_mb MB" >> "$RESOURCE_LOG"
  if [ "$disk_space_mb" -lt "$MIN_DISK_SPACE_MB" ] || [ "$memory_free_mb" -lt "$MIN_MEMORY_MB" ]; then
    log "ERROR" "Insufficient resources: Disk=$disk_space_mb MB, Memory=$memory_free_mb MB"
    return 1
  fi
  log "SUCCESS" "Resources sufficient"
}

update_state() {
  local step="$1" status="$2"
  if command -v jq >/dev/null 2>&1; then
    local entry=$(jq -n --arg s "$step" --arg st "$status" --arg ts "$(timestamp)" \
      '{step: $s, status: $st, timestamp: $ts}')
    if [ -f "$STATE_FILE" ]; then
      jq ". + [$entry] | sort_by(.timestamp) | reverse | .[:50]" "$STATE_FILE" > "$STATE_FILE.tmp" && mv "$STATE_FILE.tmp" "$STATE_FILE"
    else
      echo "[$entry]" > "$STATE_FILE"
    fi
    CHANGED_FILES+=("$STATE_FILE")
  fi
}

generate_troubleshooting() {
  log "INFO" "Generating $TROUBLESHOOTING_GUIDE"
  cat << EOF > "$TROUBLESHOOTING_GUIDE"
Troubleshooting Guide ($(timestamp))

1. Dependency Install Failure:
   - Check: src/{shared,frontend,backend}_install.log
   - Fix: Run './setup-and-run.sh --no-parallel'
   - VS Code: Open Terminal, run 'pnpm install --prefer-offline'

2. Build Failure:
   - Check: src/{shared,frontend,backend}_build.log
   - Fix: Ensure 'src/shared/src/index.ts' exports UserRole
   - VS Code: Open 'src/*/tsconfig.json', add "types": ["vite/client", "node"]

3. Resource Issues:
   - Check: $RESOURCE_LOG
   - Fix: Free up disk/memory

4. Configuration:
   - Check: $REPO_DIR/pnpm-workspace.yaml
   - Fix: Ensure 'packages: - src/shared - src/frontend - src/backend'
EOF
  CHANGED_FILES+=("$TROUBLESHOOTING_GUIDE")
}

generate_summary() {
  log "INFO" "Generating $SUMMARY_FILE"
  local progress=$(( ${#SUCCESSFUL_STEPS[@]} * 100 / (${#SUCCESSFUL_STEPS[@]} + ${#FAILED_STEPS[@]} + 1) ))
  local file_list=$(printf '"%s",' "${CHANGED_FILES[@]}" | sed 's/,$//')
  jq -n \
    --arg recipient "Jules" \
    --arg ts "$(timestamp)" \
    --arg progress "$progress" \
    --argjson successful "$(printf '%s\n' "${SUCCESSFUL_STEPS[@]}" | jq -R . | jq -s .)" \
    --argjson failed "$(printf '%s\n' "${FAILED_STEPS[@]}" | jq -R . | jq -s .)" \
    --argjson files "[$file_list]" \
    '{recipient: $recipient, timestamp: $ts, progress: $progress, successful: $successful, failed: $failed, changed_files: $files}' > "$SUMMARY_FILE"
  CHANGED_FILES+=("$SUMMARY_FILE")
}

# === CORE FUNCTIONS ===
check_versions() {
  log "INFO" "Checking versions..."
  local node_v=$(node -v 2>/dev/null || echo "none")
  local pnpm_v=$(pnpm -v 2>/dev/null || echo "none")
  if [ "$node_v" = "none" ] || [ "$pnpm_v" = "none" ]; then
    log "ERROR" "Node.js or pnpm not installed"
    FAILED_STEPS+=("Check versions")
    return 1
  fi
  if ! version_ge "${node_v#v}" "$REQUIRED_NODE_VERSION" || ! version_ge "$pnpm_v" "$REQUIRED_PNPM_VERSION"; then
    log "ERROR" "Required: Node $REQUIRED_NODE_VERSION, pnpm $REQUIRED_PNPM_VERSION; Found: $node_v, $pnpm_v"
    FAILED_STEPS+=("Check versions")
    return 1
  fi
  log "SUCCESS" "Versions OK: Node $node_v, pnpm $pnpm_v"
  SUCCESSFUL_STEPS+=("Check versions")
}

fix_workspace() {
  local workspace="$REPO_DIR/pnpm-workspace.yaml"
  if [ ! -f "$workspace" ] || ! grep -q "src/shared" "$workspace"; then
    cat << EOF > "$workspace"
packages:
  - 'src/shared'
  - 'src/frontend'
  - 'src/backend'
EOF
    log "SUCCESS" "Updated $workspace"
    CHANGED_FILES+=("$workspace")
  fi
  SUCCESSFUL_STEPS+=("Fix workspace")
}

install_deps() {
  log "INFO" "Installing dependencies..."
  check_resources || return 1
  fix_workspace
  if [ "$PARALLEL" = true ]; then
    local pids=()
    for dir in "${PROJECT_DIRS[@]}"; do
      if [ -d "$dir" ]; then
        log "INFO" "Installing $dir"
        run_cmd "pnpm --filter $dir install --prefer-offline" > "$dir_install.log" 2>&1 &
        pids+=($!)
      fi
    done
    local failed=false
    for pid in "${pids[@]}"; do
      wait "$pid" || failed=true
    done
    for dir in "${PROJECT_DIRS[@]}"; do
      if [ -f "$dir_install.log" ] && grep -q "ERR_PNPM" "$dir_install.log"; then
        log "ERROR" "Install failed for $dir, see $dir_install.log"
        FAILED_STEPS+=("Install $dir")
        CHANGED_FILES+=("$dir_install.log")
        failed=true
      elif [ -f "$dir_install.log" ]; then
        log "SUCCESS" "Installed $dir"
        SUCCESSFUL_STEPS+=("Install $dir")
        CHANGED_FILES+=("$dir_install.log")
      fi
    done
    if [ "$failed" = true ]; then
      log "INFO" "Retrying sequentially..."
      PARALLEL=false
      install_deps
      return $?
    fi
  else
    for dir in "${PROJECT_DIRS[@]}"; do
      if [ -d "$dir" ]; then
        if ! run_cmd "pnpm --filter $dir install --prefer-offline" > "$dir_install.log" 2>&1; then
          log "ERROR" "Install failed for $dir, see $dir_install.log"
          FAILED_STEPS+=("Install $dir")
          CHANGED_FILES+=("$dir_install.log")
          return 1
        fi
        log "SUCCESS" "Installed $dir"
        SUCCESSFUL_STEPS+=("Install $dir")
        CHANGED_FILES+=("$dir_install.log")
      fi
    done
  fi
  run_cmd "pnpm dedup" || log "WARNING" "Dedupe failed"
}

build_projects() {
  log "INFO" "Building projects..."
  for dir in "${PROJECT_DIRS[@]}"; do
    if [ -d "$dir" ]; then
      if [ "$dir" = "src/shared" ]; then
        if ! grep -q "UserRole" "$dir/src/index.ts" 2>/dev/null; then
          echo "export type UserRole = 'admin' | 'user' | 'guest';" >> "$dir/src/index.ts"
          CHANGED_FILES+=("$dir/src/index.ts")
        fi
      fi
      if [ "$dir" = "src/frontend" ]; then
        local tsconfig="$dir/tsconfig.json"
        if ! grep -q "vite/client" "$tsconfig" 2>/dev/null; then
          jq '.compilerOptions.types += ["vite/client", "node"]' "$tsconfig" > "$tsconfig.tmp" && mv "$tsconfig.tmp" "$tsconfig"
          CHANGED_FILES+=("$tsconfig")
        fi
      fi
      if ! run_cmd "pnpm --filter $dir build" > "$dir_build.log" 2>&1; then
        log "ERROR" "Build failed for $dir, see $dir_build.log"
        FAILED_STEPS+=("Build $dir")
        CHANGED_FILES+=("$dir_build.log")
        return 1
      fi
      log "SUCCESS" "Built $dir"
      SUCCESSFUL_STEPS+=("Build $dir")
      CHANGED_FILES+=("$dir_build.log")
    fi
  done
}

start_docker() {
  log "INFO" "Starting Docker..."
  if [ -f "$DOCKER_COMPOSE_FILE" ]; then
    if ! run_cmd "docker-compose -f $DOCKER_COMPOSE_FILE up -d"; then
      log "ERROR" "Docker startup failed"
      FAILED_STEPS+=("Start Docker")
      return 1
    fi
    log "SUCCESS" "Docker started"
    SUCCESSFUL_STEPS+=("Start Docker")
  else
    log "WARNING" "$DOCKER_COMPOSE_FILE not found"
  fi
}

# === MAIN EXECUTION ===
main() {
  while [ $# -gt 0 ]; do
    case "$1" in
      --verbose) VERBOSE=true ;;
      --debug) DEBUG=true; VERBOSE=true ;;
      --no-parallel) PARALLEL=false ;;
      --dry-run) DRY_RUN=true ;;
      --resume) RESUME=true ;;
      *) log "WARNING" "Unknown argument: $1" ;;
    esac
    shift
  done

  mkdir -p "$LOG_DIR"
  cd "$REPO_DIR" || { log "ERROR" "Cannot access $REPO_DIR"; exit 1; }
  log "INFO" "=== Setup Started ==="

  local steps=("check_versions" "install_deps" "build_projects" "start_docker")
  for step in "${steps[@]}"; do
    log "INFO" "Running $step..."
    if ! "$step"; then
      update_state "$step" "FAILED"
      generate_troubleshooting
      generate_summary
      log "ERROR" "Setup failed at $step. See $SUMMARY_FILE"
      exit 1
    fi
    update_state "$step" "SUCCESS"
  done

  generate_troubleshooting
  generate_summary
  log "SUCCESS" "Setup completed. Review $SUMMARY_FILE"
}

main "$@"

bash

#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail
LOG_FILE="../logs/purge.log"
timestamp() { date "+%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S"; }
log() { echo "$(timestamp) [$1] $2" | tee -a "$LOG_FILE"; }

log "INFO" "Starting purge in $(pwd)"
total_size_before=$(du -sm . | cut -f1 2>/dev/null || echo "0")

for dir in */; do
  [ -d "$dir" ] || continue
  log "INFO" "Processing $dir ($(du -sh "$dir" | cut -f1))"
  for bloat in node_modules dist build .cache .env .env.* *.log *.tgz .vscode .idea Thumbs.db .DS_Store; do
    if find "$dir" -name "$bloat" -exec rm -rf {} + 2>/dev/null; then
      log "SUCCESS" "Removed $bloat from $dir"
    else
      log "WARNING" "No $bloat in $dir or removal failed"
    fi
  done
  if [ -d "$dir/.git" ]; then
    rm -rf "$dir/.git" && log "SUCCESS" "Removed .git from $dir" || log "ERROR" "Failed removing .git from $dir"
  fi
  git -C "$dir" remote -v 2>/dev/null | grep -q . && log "WARNING" "Git remotes remain in $dir" || log "SUCCESS" "No Git remotes in $dir"
done

total_size_after=$(du -sm . | cut -f1 2>/dev/null || echo "0")
reclaimed=$((total_size_before - total_size_after))
log "INFO" "Purge completed. Space before: ${total_size_before}MB, after: ${total_size_after}MB, reclaimed: ${reclaimed}MB"
